Medical College History & Introduction
Al-Azhar Medical College & Super Speciality Hospital (AAMC),
established in 2014 at Thodupuzha, Idukki District, Kerala, is a premier
medical institution functioning under the Al-Azhar Group of Institutions
and the Noorul Islam. Trust. Nestled in a serene and scenic
environment, the college is affiliated to the Kerala University of Health
Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the National Medical Commission
(NMC), consistently setting benchmarks in medical education and
healthcare delivery since its inception.
The institution offers high-quality MBBS education, supported by
experienced faculty, competency-based curriculum, and
state-of-the-art academic infrastructure. The attached 700+ bedded
Super Speciality Teaching Hospital delivers comprehensive clinical
services, 24/7 emergency and trauma care, and provides extensive


--- Page 2 ---
hands-on clinical training for medical students across all major and
super-specialty disciplines.
With a strong emphasis on academic excellence, patient-centered care,
and community service, Al-Azhar Medical College is committed to
nurturing competent, compassionate, and ethically driven medical
professionals. The college and hospital collectively focus on shaping a
new generation of doctors dedicated to national service while ensuring
affordable, quality healthcare for the common population.
AAMC aspires to deliver world-class and accessible medical care through
advanced infrastructure, skilled healthcare professionals, and regular
medical camps conducted both within the campus and in outreach areas,
enhancing students’ practical exposure and real-world clinical skills.
Special emphasis is placed on soft skills training and doctor—patient
communication, enabling holistic professional development. Since
commencing its academic activities in 2018 under KUHS affiliation, the
institution has also secured approval from the Pharmacy Council of India
(PCI) and the Government of Kerala, reinforcing its commitment to
quality education, healthcare excellence, and social responsibility.

internship) — CBME aligned.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at Al Azhar Medical College are processed
via Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through
centralized counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. Al Azhar Medical College ) + quota options (state-quota,
minority,NRI) — as per your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e lf a seat is allotted to you at Al Azhar Medical College , you get an
allotment memo / letter.


--- Page 6 ---
5.Reporting to College & Document Verification
e Report to Al Azhar Medical College within deadline with original
certificates: NEET scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing
certificates, transfer / conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation
proof (if applicable), ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Al Azhar Medical College with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Theatres : Spacious and well-ventilated lecture halls
equipped with LCD projectors, smart boards, advanced audio-visual
systems, and comfortable seating. These theatres are designed to


--- Page 16 ---
support large group teaching, interactive learning, and effective
knowledge delivery.

e Demonstration & Seminar Halls: Dedicated demonstration rooms
for clinical and practical teaching.Seminar halls are used for
academic discussions, conferences, workshops, and CME programs.
Tutorial rooms support small-group teaching and problem-based
learning.

e Departmental Laboratories:.Fully equipped laboratories in all
pre-clinical and para-clinical departments provide students with
hands-on practical experience, enhancing understanding and interest
in their programs. The labs are well facilitated to support independent
research activities.

e Central Library : A large Central Library with an extensive collection
of medical textbooks and reference books, along with subscriptions to
national and international medical journals. It offers access to digital
resources, e-journals, and online databases, separate reading halls
for students and faculty, and full-time Wi-Fi connectivity, creating a
rich learning environment beyond classrooms.

e Departmental Libraries : Subject-specific libraries maintained in
each department.Provide easy access to reference books, journals,
and teaching materials.

e Computer & Digital Learning Facilities :Well-equipped computer
laboratories with internet connectivity and access to e-learning
platforms, medical databases, and research resources, supporting
academic work, research activities, and online assessments.

e Research Facilities : Dedicated research rooms and facilities for
students and faculty support clinical research, academic projects, and


--- Page 17 ---
scholarly publications, with institutional backing for research ethics
and approvals.

e Examination Halls : Well-designed examination halls with adequate
seating capacity.Facilities for theory, practical, clinical, and university
examinations.

e Skill & Simulation Laboratory: Modern clinical skills lab for
procedural training.Facilities for Basic Life Support (BLS), Advanced
Life Support (ALS), emergency care, and clinical simulations.Enables
students to practice skills before real patient exposure.

e Multy-Gym : A well-maintained gym and fitness center within the
campus provides an excellent wellness experience for students and
faculty. The facility is accessible at scheduled times under the
supervision of a gym instructor.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Al-Azhar Medical College & Teaching Hospital actively conducts
academic events such as CMEs, seminars, workshops, guest
lectures, and foundation programs in line with NMC and KUHS
guidelines.

e Students are encouraged to participate in academic competitions,
conferences, cultural programs, sports events, and community
outreach activities.

e The institution has achieved recognition from the National Medical
Commission and affiliation with the Kerala University of Health
Sciences, with continuous growth in academic infrastructure and
healthcare services.


--- Page 18 ---
e Faculty members regularly publish research papers and present
their work at scientific conferences, while students undertake
research projects under ethical supervision.

e The college places strong emphasis on research in clinical and
community health areas and actively contributes to society through
medical camps, screening programs, vaccination drives, and public
health initiatives, especially in rural and underserved regions.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity : A 1040-bed teaching hospital (expandable) that
provides a wide range of clinical, super-specialty, and emergency
services.

e Critical Care (ICU Complex): AAMC manages a comprehensive ICU
complex with dedicated 5-bed units for the Intensive Coronary Care
Unit (ICCU), General ICU, Surgical ICU (SICU), and a combined
NICU/PICU. The hospital's emergency department also maintains 30
dedicated emergency beds for immediate stabilization.

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD): With an average of over 1,300 OPD
patients daily, students are exposed to a massive variety of clinical
cases ranging from routine tropical diseases to complex
super-specialty referrals.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments: AAMC provides a full
spectrum of healthcare through its Specialty wing (General Medicine,
Surgery, Pediatrics, OBG, Orthopedics, ENT, Ophthalmology,
Psychiatry, Pulmonology, and Dermatology) and its Super Specialty
units (Cardiology, Neurology, Nephrology, Gastroenterology, Urology,
and Endocrinology). This integrated structure, supported by 24/7


--- Page 19 ---
Emergency and advanced Radio-Diagnosis, ensures comprehensive
care while offering medical students intensive clinical exposure
across all levels of healthcare.

Campus Life

e Cultural Vibes: The annual Al-Azhar Fest is the highlight, featuring
arts, music, and dance. The college also frequently hosts the MG
University Kalolsavam, bringing a massive creative energy to the
campus.

e Residential Life: Separate, secure hostels for men and women
provide a "home away from home" with study rooms and common
areas for socializing.

e Fitness & Sports: Students stay active with an on-campus gym and
dedicated facilities for football, basketball, cricket, and badminton.

e Social Hubs: The canteen and cafeteria are the primary hangouts for
quick bites and "chai breaks" between clinical rotations.

e Academic Sanctuary: A massive Central Library with high-speed
internet and silent zones serves as the go-to spot for late-night exam
prep and research.

e Student Support: Active student unions and councils ensure that
student voices are heard and that campus life stays engaging through
various clubs and celebrations like Onam, Eid, and Christmas.

Safety & Support System

e Anti-Ragging Vigilance: The _ institution strictly enforces a
zero-tolerance policy toward ragging. A dedicated Anti-Ragging
Committee, chaired by the Principal and supported by a Nodal


--- Page 20 ---
Officer, maintains continuous surveillance across the campus and
hostels to ensure student well-being.

e Surveillance & Security: The 50-acre campus is under 24/7 CCTV
monitoring in all key areas, including academic blocks and hostels. A
professional security team, led by a Chief Security Officer, manages
secure entry systems and physical patrols.

e Gender Safety (PoSH): An Internal Complaints Committee (ICC)
is active under the PoSH Act to prevent and address sexual
harassment, providing a confidential and structured portal for online
complaints and investigations.

e Grievance Redressal: The college has appointed dedicated
Grievance Officers (PIO and CPIO) to handle administrative and
academic concerns.

Internship Placement Quality - Quick Summary

e Internship is conducted entirely within the attached teaching hospital
as per NMC and KUHS guidelines.

e Interns undergo structured rotational postings in all major clinical and
allied departments.

e Interns receive extensive hands-on clinical exposure through OPDs,
IPDs, wards, operation theatres, emergency services, and critical
care units.

e Upon completing the internship, graduates either go for medical
practice or go for postgraduate programs

Al-Azhar Medical College Student & Parent Review

Student Review

Students generally describe Al-Azhar Medical College as a disciplined
institution with good academic support and strong clinical exposure. The
teaching hospital provides adequate patient inflow, allowing students to
gain hands-on experience across major departments, especially during
clinical years and internship. Faculty are considered supportive and
approachable, with regular academic activities such as seminars, CMEs,
and clinical discussions. The campus is spacious and well-maintained, with
hostel facilities, sports areas, and basic amenities contributing to a
comfortable student life. Students also highlight the strict discipline,
anti-ragging measures, and structured academic environment. Overall, the
college is viewed as a good choice for students seeking solid clinical
training and a focused medical education environment in Kerala.

Overall : Al-Azhar Medical College is widely appreciated for its strong
clinical exposure, disciplined academic environment, and supportive
faculty. Students find the campus facilities and hospital training adequate
for building solid medical knowledge and practical skills.


--- Page 22 ---
Parent review:
Parents generally express positive views about Al-Azhar Medical College,
appreciating its disciplined academic environment, strong safety measures,
and well-structured teaching system. They value the college’s focus on
professional conduct, ethical training, and student welfare. The attached
teaching hospital provides excellent clinical exposure, which reassures
parents about their children’s practical skill development and career
readiness. Hostel facilities, security arrangements, and anti-ragging policies
contribute to a safe and supportive campus life. Parents also acknowledge
the commitment of faculty members in guiding students academically and
personally. Overall, the institution is seen as a reliable choice for quality
medical education and holistic development of future healthcare
professionals.
Overall : Parents generally regard Al-Azhar Medical College as a safe,
disciplined institution with strong academics and clinical training. They
appreciate the supportive faculty, campus security, and focus on student
welfare and professional growth.

Way To Reach

Al-Azhar Medical College and Super Specialty Hospital is located in
Kumaramangalam, approximately 4 km from Thodupuzha town in the
Idukki district.

By Road (Bus)

e From Thodupuzha Town: The college is just a 10-minute drive from
the Thodupuzha KSRTC Bus Station or the Private Bus Stand.

e Local Transport: You can take a local bus heading towards Ezhalloor
or Kumaramangalam and get down at the college stop.
Auto-rickshaws and taxis are readily available from Thodupuzha town
for a direct drop.

e Interstate/Intercity: Direct KSRTC buses run to Thodupuzha from
major cities like Ernakulam (Kochi), Kottayam, and Thrissur.

By Train
There is no railway station in Thodupuzha. The nearest major stations are:

e Aluva (AWY): ~45 km away. This is often the most convenient station
for travelers coming from North Kerala or other states, as it is
well-connected to the Kochi airport route.

e Piravom Road (PVRD): ~43 km away (closer but fewer express trains
stop here).

e Kottayam (KTYM): ~55—-60 km away. A good option for those
traveling from South Kerala.


--- Page 26 ---
e Ernakulam South/North (ERS/ERN): ~60 km away. Major hubs with

the most frequent train options.
By Air

e Cochin International Airport (COK): Located at Nedumbassery, it is
approximately 53 km (about 1.5 hours) from the college. You can hire
a pre-paid taxi from the airport or take a bus to Aluva and then a
connecting bus to Thodupuzha.

LOGO:
Medical College - History &amp; Introduction
Amala Institute of Medical Sciences (AIMS) - "Home for total Healing" -
named after Blessed Virgin Mary, is a multi-disciplinary medical network of
pedagogical, therapeutic, research and outreach programmes. AIMS brings
together a dedicated team of physicians, nurses, and other healthcare
professionals to provide the highest standards of medical treatment. Our
full range of primary and speciality care medical services enables
cross-speciality consultation, which assures outstanding treatment for each
patient. Our extensive infrastructure offers state of art facilities comprising
25 modern operating theatres, 210 fully equipped intensive-care beds, a
fully computerized and networked Hospital Information System (HIS), and a
digital radiology department.At present, Amala is home to a Medical
College, College of Nursing, Nursing School, Super Speciality Hospital,
Teaching Hospital, Cancer Hospital, Cancer Research Centre, Ayurvedic
Hospital & Research Centre, a Homeopathic Hospital and Research centre,
a Pharmacy Production Unit and Bethanygram (A home for the aged).


--- Page 31 ---
The Amala Institute of Medical Sciences (AIMS) offers a diverse range of
undergraduate, postgraduate, and super-speciality medical and nursing
programs with specific seat capacities. For undergraduate medical studies,
the flagship MBBS program has an annual intake of 100 seats. In the
nursing sector, the B.Sc. The nursing program admits approximately 50 to
90 students annually, while postgraduate M.Sc. Nursing specialisations,
such as Medical-Surgical and Psychiatric Nursing, typically have 3 to 5
seats per department. Additionally, the institute offers a three-year Diploma
in General Nursing and Midwifery (GNM) with an intake of 40 students.
Vision: To be a premier teaching hospital providing holistic healthcare,
excellence in medical education, and innovative research.
Mission: To provide affordable, state-of-the-art medical services to all,
especially the poor, while nurturing competent professionals dedicated to
the healing ministry.

Health Training Centres.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management /
minority / NRI) for MBBS at AIMS are processed via Commissioner
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste
/reservation proofs if applicable).

3. Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. AIMS) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your
eligibility & preference

5


--- Page 35 ---
e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.
4. Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority
e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences, and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.
e If a seat is allotted to you at AIMS, you get an allotment memo /
letter.
5. Reporting to College & Document Verification
e Report to AIMS within deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6. Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBB1st year at
AIMS with all admitted students.

Key Strengths

e Integration of academics with clinical practice ensures students gain
real-world medical exposure.

e Holistic development focuses on sports, cultural, and seminar
facilities.

e Modern infrastructure comparable to leading medical institutes in
Kerala.

Events, Achievements &amp; Research Highlights

e MEDEX CONCORDIUM '25: Hosted Kerala's largest medical expo
from November 22-26, 2025, featuring a National MedQuiz, a mega
medical exhibition, and an undergraduate medical conference.

e Integrated Medical Research Department: A state-of-the-art facility
opened in early 2025 to foster interdisciplinary collaboration and rapid
response to public health crises.

e NABH Re-accreditation: Successfully completed its 3rd cycle of
NABH Accreditation in September 2025, complying with the 5th
edition standards for hospitals.

Hospital Infrastructure &amp; Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A massive 1,200-bed facility that includes general
wards, semi-private rooms, and specialized suites to accommodate a
diverse patient demographic.

20


--- Page 50 ---
e Specialized Units: The campus houses a world-class Amala Cancer
Hospital featuring advanced radiotherapy units like Linear
Accelerators (LINAC), PET-CT, and SPECT scans.

e Critical Care & OT: There are 25 high-tech Operation Theatres and
over 210 ICU beds tailored for Neonatal (NICU), Cardiac (CCU), and
Neurosurgical intensive care.

e Diagnostic Prowess: Features fully automated, NABL-accredited
laboratories and a dedicated Nuclear Medicine department.

e Patient Volume: Students encounter an average daily footfall of
2,000—2,500 outpatients, providing an immense volume of cases for
hands-on learning.

e Case Diversity: Due to its reputation as a cancer research hub,
students gain rare exposure to complex Oncology, Cardiology, and
Neurosurgery cases alongside primary health conditions.

Campus Life

e Infrastructure: Students have access to a massive Central Library
with extensive digital and print resources, a modern gymnasium, and
dedicated courts for basketball, volleyball, and football.

e Social Engagement: The Students’ Union organizes annual cultural
festivals and sports meets, though the calendar remains heavily
focused on ensuring high academic and clinical attendance.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: In strict compliance with National Medical

Zero Tolerance Policy toward ragging. An active Anti-Ragging
Committee ensures a safe transition for freshers.

e Counseling Services: A dedicated Student Guidance and Counseling
Cell provides professional mental health support to help students
manage the academic pressure and emotional challenges of medical
education.

Internship Structure at AIMS
e Duration: 1 year compulsory rotating internship for MBBS students.
e Departments covered: Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, Obstetrics &
Gynecology, Community Medicine, and specialty rotations.
e Stipend: 212,000—%15,000 per month during internship.
e Post-internship opportunities: Junior resident positions with
salaries around %40,000 per month.
Bond & obligations: Standard internship requirements as per Kerala
University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and National Medical Commission
(NMC)

Key Insights
e Interns: Receive 16,000 monthly plus free hostel accommodation,
which is competitive among Kerala private medical colleges.
e PG Residents: Stipends increase annually from %53,000 to 55,000,
aligning with Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) norms.
e Payment mode: All stipends are transferred directly to bank
accounts.
e Support: Free hostel facilities for interns reduce living costs
significantly.
Conduct & Discipline
e Anti-ragging policy: Students must submit an anti-ragging
undertaking during admission; ragging is strictly prohibited.
e Anti-dowry affidavit: Required as part of admission documentation.
e Campus behavior: Use of mobile phones is restricted in classrooms
and clinical areas.
e Substance-free campus: Alcohol, drugs, and smoking are banned.
Hostel Rules
e Separate hostels: For men and women, with strict entry/exit timings.
e Mess discipline: Meals provided at fixed times; outside food
restrictions apply.
e Visitors: Limited visiting hours; outsiders not allowed without
permission.
e Quiet hours: Maintained to support study and rest.

Student Review
Amala Institute of Medical Sciences highly for its strong academics and
massive clinical exposure due to the high patient volume in the hospital.
While the campus is described as disciplined and _ strict, especially
regarding hostel timings and attendance, the faculty are considered highly
experienced and approachable. The infrastructure is noted as being
well-maintained with ongoing renovations, and the institution is praised for
providing a solid clinical foundation for future doctors despite a more
traditional, academic-focused environment.
Overall:Amala Institute of Medical Sciences is a highly-reputed, disciplined
institution offering excellent clinical exposure and strong academic
foundations through its state-of-the-art teaching hospital and experienced
faculty.
Parent Review
Parents generally view Amala Institute of Medical Sciences as a safe,
value-driven, and highly disciplined environment that prioritises academic
excellence and moral character over campus social life. They frequently
praise the institution for its top-tier hospital facilities, the high quality of
clinical training their children receive, and the institution's longstanding
reputation as a premier Christian minority medical college in Kerala. While
some find the strict hostel regulations and rigorous schedule demanding,

professional integrity in future doctors.
Overall:Parents consistently trust Amala Institute of Medical Sciences for its
disciplined, safe environment and its reputation for producing ethically
grounded, clinically competent doctors through rigorous academic training.

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Azeezia Medical College Sciences and Research is one of the finest
Medical institutions in Kerala which commenced in the year 2008. The
Medical College is the first venture of Podikunju Musaliar Memorial
Charitable & Educational Trust established in 2001. Affiliated with the
Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the
National Medical Commission (NMC), the college has grown into a
reputed center for undergraduate and postgraduate medical training.
Azeezia Medical College Sciences and Research provides a great
ambience to learn Medicine. The experienced faculty is dedicated to
mould its students into highly disciplined professionals fulfilling the
motto “education with healing touch’. The college offers the best of its
facilities to enhance the overall development of a student. The
mentor-mentee system is effectively implemented aiming at the progress
of academic, mental, and emotional quotient of the student. The
serene campus offers ample opportunities for the overall development of
a student and is committed to provide state-of-the-art clinical facilities to
the community.


--- Page 60 ---
The institution’s vision is to be a leading institution in medical education,
healthcare, and research, recognized nationally and internationally for
its commitment to excellence, innovation, and compassionate care. And
the mission is to provide high-quality medical education, deliver
exceptional healthcare services, and conduct groundbreaking research
that transforms lives.
Basic College Profile

e Institution Type: Private Self-Financing Medical College

e Religious Affiliation : Muslim

e Management: Podikunju Musaliar Memorial Health Education Trust

e Campus: The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located

in Meeyanoor,Kollam.
e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)
e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences, National Medical
Commission.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at Azeezia Medical College are processed
via Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through
centralized counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. Azeezia Medical College ) + quota options (state-quota,
minority,NRI) — as per your eligibility & preference.


--- Page 63 ---
e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.
4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority
e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.
e lf a seat is allotted to you at Azeezia Medical College, you get an
allotment memo / letter.
5.Reporting to College & Document Verification
e Report to Azeezia Medical College within deadline with original
certificates: NEET scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing
certificates,transfer / conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation
proof (if applicable), ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Azeezia Medical College with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Halls: The campus features over six spacious lecture halls
equipped with advanced audio-visual aids and smart classroom
technology to facilitate interactive learning.
e Central Library: Located on the 2nd floor, the fully automated
Azeezia Central Library houses over 7,550 books, including national


--- Page 73 ---
and international journals, PG research theses, and digital resources
accessible via Integrated Library Management Software.

e Laboratories: Advanced, well-equipped labs are available for
pre-clinical, para-clinical, and clinical training. These include
specialized units such as Dissection Labs for human anatomy and
Histology Labs with high-end imaging equipment.

e Examination Hall: A dedicated examination hall covering 800 square
metres can accommodate up to 700 students simultaneously.

e Anatomical Museum: The Anatomy Department maintains a
comprehensive museum with a collection of anatomical specimens,
models, and charts for research and student reference.

e Teaching Hospital: The attached 540-bed NABH-accredited hospital
provides hands-on clinical exposure across 10+ departments and
super-specialties like Cardiology (with a 24/7 Cath Lab), Nephrology,
and Neurosurgery.

e Sports & Recreation: The campus includes a cricket ground, football
ground, basketball court, and a gymnasium to promote physical
fitness.

e Seminar & Conference Halls: Modern auditorium and seminar halls
are frequently used for CMEs, fests, and academic conferences.

Hostel & Mess facilities

e There are four hostels available. Three hostels for girls and
one hostel for the boys.

e Of the four hostels, only one is outside the campus at
Kummallor. Bus service is provided for those staying at the
hostel.


--- Page 74 ---
e Hostel room types range from double rooms to triple rooms.

e The hostels have back-up generators. Electricity and water are
available 24/7.

e Each room has a study table with a cabinet to store books,
wardrobes and cots.

e There is 24 hour security and CCTV surveillance.

e The hostel mess provides good quality & hygienic food.

e Campus canteens provide snacks, beverages and lunch at
affordable rates.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Students consistently achieve outstanding academic results, securing
top ranks in university examinations. Many of our graduates have
been awarded prestigious scholarships and fellowships for their
exceptional academic performance.

e Azeezia Medical College encourages a strong research culture
across all departments. Faculty and students are actively involved in
research projects and have published in national and international
peer-reviewed journals.

e The institution conducts regular research methodology workshops
and seminars, with an active Institutional Ethics Committee
ensuring ethical standards. Student participation in programs such as
the ICMR Short Term Studentship (STS) further strengthens the
research environment.

e The college has consistently demonstrated strong academic
performance with commendable results in university examinations.


--- Page 75 ---
e Faculty members have received recognition at state and national
levels for their contributions to medical education and healthcare.

e The institution has successfully met regulatory standards and
received approvals from statutory bodies, while students have
achieved awards and accolades in academics, cultural activities, and
sports at university and inter-collegiate levels.

e Azeezia Medical College regularly organizes a wide range of
academic, cultural, and sports events to promote holistic
development among students. These include annual college day
celebrations, cultural festivals, sports meets, inter-collegiate
competitions, academic conferences, CME programs, workshops,
and guest lectures. The institution also actively conducts health
camps, medical outreach programs, and national health observance
activities such as World Health Day, Doctors’ Day, and blood donation
camps.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A 540-bed teaching hospital (expandable) that
provides a wide range of clinical, super-specialty, and emergency
services.

e Operation Theatres: The hospital features 11 modern Operating
Theatres (OTs) equipped for both major open surgeries and
advanced laparoscopic (minimally invasive) procedures.

e Patient Inflow : Historically, the hospital manages an average of 800
to 1,000+ outpatients per day. And average daily admissions range
from 60 to 90 patients across various specialties. (figures are based


--- Page 76 ---
on recent institutional and regulatory data and may vary from time to
time.)

e Emergency & Trauma: A 24-hour Emergency Department with
advanced life support systems and a dedicated ambulance fleet.

e Super-Specialty Access: Unlike many smaller colleges, students
here gain exposure to "Super-Specialty" departments including:
Cardiology & Cardiothoracic Surgery,Nephrology ,Neurology &
Neurosurgery,Gastroenterology & Pulmonology.

Campus Life

e Vibrant Student Community: The campus hosts students from
diverse backgrounds, fostering a multicultural and _ inclusive
environment.

e Clubs & Societies: Students can participate in cultural, literary, and
sports clubs, encouraging creativity and teamwork outside
academics.

e Sports & Fitness: Facilities for indoor and outdoor sports like cricket,

e Secure Campus Environment: The college has a gated campus

students at all times.

e CCTV Surveillance: Key areas of the campus, including hostels,
corridors, and common areas, are under CCTV surveillance for

e On-Campus Medical Facilities: Immediate access to healthcare is
available through the college hospital, including emergency care and
routine medical support.

e Counseling & Mental Health Support: Students have access to
professional counselors and mentorship programs to help manage
stress, academic pressure, and personal challenges.

e Grievance Redressal: The college has formal procedures for
addressing student complaints related to academics, safety, or
interpersonal issues.

e Peer & Faculty Mentoring: Seniors and faculty provide guidance,
ensuring new students have support during adjustment periods.

Azeezia Medical College maintains comprehensive rules and regulations
covering academics, discipline, hostel conduct, safety, and professional

Way to reach

Azeezia Medical College is located in Meeyannoor, a serene hamlet in the
Kollam district of Kerala. While it is tucked away from the main city buzz, it
is well-connected to major transport hubs.

By Road (Most Convenient)

The college is situated about 8 km away from the NH-47
(Kollam-Thiruvananthapuram stretch).

e From Kollam City: It is approximately 18-20 km from the city center.
A taxi or auto-rickshaw usually takes about 40—50 minutes.

e From Chathannoor: This is the nearest major town on the National
Highway. The college is about 6 km. from the Chathannoor Bus
Stand.

e Bus Services: Private and KSRTC buses frequently run between
Kollam and Chathannoor. From Chathannoor, you can take local
buses or an auto to Meeyannoor.

By Rail

e Kollam Junction (QLN): This is the primary railway station, located
about 20 km from the campus. It is a major stop for all express trains.

e Paravur Railway Station: This is a closer, smaller station (about
14-15 km away), but only limited passenger and some express trains
stop here.


--- Page 83 ---
By Air

e Thiruvananthapuram International Airport (TRV): This is the
nearest airport, located approximately 56 km away.

e Travel Time: It typically takes 1.5 to 2 hours to reach the college from
the airport via NH-47, depending on traffic.

(+) BELIEVERS CHURCH MEDICAL COLLEGE
Medical College History & Introduction
Believers Church Medical College and Hospital is the healthcare arm of
Believers Church. It is devoted to excellence in teaching, learning, and
healing. The college, has an enrollment of 100 students per year The
teaching program is centered on a holistic student learning program
The college was founded with the vision of bringing hope and healing
through the love of Christ and strives to be a world-class center of
scholarship in the art and science of healing—exhibiting professionalism,
excellence, compassion, and a holistic Christ-centered understanding of
healing. It aims to partner with like-minded healthcare providers to support
and extend the medical mission, making a larger impact on health and
healthcare through policy advocacy. The objective is to create
professionally competent medical graduates with high standards of skills,
ethics, and research aptitude, imbued with values of compassion, love, and
sacrifice, enabling them to lead meaningful lives as healers in society.
Basic College Profile

e Believers Church Medical College and Hospital is the healthcare arm

of Believers Church.


--- Page 92 ---
e Established in 2016 (with the hospital beginning operations in 2014).
e Institution Type : Private Self-Financing Medical College
e Minority Status: Christian-minority institution.
e Campus: The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located
in Thiruvalla
e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)
e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences
e Recognised by National Medical Commission (NMC)
Official Contact Details

competency/OSCE-based components as per CBME_ guidelines.
Refer to the college prospectus and university regulations for exact
pass marks and internal assessment weightage.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at BCMCH are processed via Commissioner
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. BCMCH) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per
your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and

seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.


--- Page 95 ---
e If a seat is allotted to you at BCMCH, you get an allotment memo /
letter.
5.Reporting to College & Document Verification
e Report to BCMCH within deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at BCMCH with all admitted students.

Core Academic Facilities

e Lecture Halls & Classrooms: The campus houses five large,
air-conditioned lecture theatres (four for the college and one for the
hospital) with seating for 120-214 students. These are equipped with
smart boards, high-speed Wi-Fi, and advanced audio-visual aids.

e Central Library: Located in the "Knowledge Centre," the
computerized library covers 1,740 square meters across two floors. It
offers:

o Seating for over 420 students simultaneously.

o Acollection of approximately 10,000 books and 60 periodicals.

o Access to e-journal databases (Delnet) and a digital library with
25 computer terminals.

e Specialized Labs: State-of-the-art laboratories include a dedicated
anatomy dissection hall, a pathology museum for specimen display,
and clinical skill labs equipped with 32 manikins for practical training.


--- Page 105 ---
e Examination Hall: A 250-seat, air-conditioned hall featuring CCTV

monitoring and mobile signal jammers to ensure academic integrity.
Teaching Hospital Infrastructure

e Bed Capacity : The academic experience is integrated with the
750-bed multi-specialty teaching hospital.

e Operation Theaters: 17 ultra-modern theaters equipped with HEPA
filters, monitoring systems, and volumetric analysis for sterile,
high-precision surgeries.

e Intensive Care Units (ICUs): Over 100 ICU beds _ including
specialized units NICU & PICU,CCU,ECMO Centre.

e Accreditations: It holds NABH accreditation and houses the first
NABL-accredited laboratory in a medical college hospital in India.

e Emergency & Trauma: A 35-bed Emergency Department featuring a
multi-bed resuscitation bay and dedicated triage areas, handling
approximately 30,000 cases annually

Hostel Mess Facilities

e BCMC provides well-maintained separate hostels for boys and girls
within the campus, ensuring a safe and comfortable living
environment for students.

e The hostels are equipped with modern amenities, including Wi-Fi,
common study areas, recreational spaces, and 24/7 security.

e The college also operates an on-campus mess serving nutritious and
hygienic meals, catering to diverse dietary needs and ensuring the
overall well-being of the students.


--- Page 106 ---
e Meals are prepared under supervision to ensure hygiene and

nutritional standards are met.
Safety & Support System

e Zero-Tolerance Anti-Ragging Policy: The campus is strictly
anti-ragging. It features a dedicated Anti-Ragging Committee and a
Squad that conducts surprise raids in hostels and "hotspots." A
toll-free helpline (1800-425-3010) is available for immediate reporting.

e The "Foster Family" Program: A unique initiative where each
student is assigned to a faculty member's family. This "Foster Family"
acts as an emotional support system, providing a "home away from
home" to help students cope with homesickness or personal stress.

e Academic Mentorship: Every student is assigned a junior faculty
mentor to guide them through their academic journey and clinical
rotations.

e Counseling Services: The institution employs professional Student
Counselors (such as Ann George) who specialize in adolescent care
and mental wellness.

Internship & Placement Quality -— Quick Summary:

e BCMC provides extensive hands-on clinical training during the
internship period, ensuring students gain practical experience across
diverse medical specialties.

e The college has strong hospital affiliations and networks, helping
graduates secure quality placements and opportunities for further
specialization. Students are guided by experienced faculty, and the
structured internship program emphasizes professionalism, patient


--- Page 107 ---
care, and skill development, preparing them effectively for medical

careers and postgraduate studies.
College rules & discipline
Institutional rules & hostel regulations : the college prospectus/admission
download pages include the institution’s rules and hostel regulations
(disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance rules). Read the prospectus
carefully before admission.
BCMCH Student & Parent Review
Student Review:
Believers Church Medical College offers students a unique blend of quality
medical education and Christ-centered values. Students appreciate the
well-structured curriculum that balances theory and practical learning,
providing excellent clinical exposure across various hospital departments.
The faculty are described as highly supportive, approachable, and
experienced, guiding students in academics, research, and professional
development. Campus life at BCMC is considered safe, inclusive, and
vibrant, with separate hostels for boys and girls, hygienic mess facilities,
recreational areas, and 24/7 security, ensuring overall comfort and
well-being. Students also value the emphasis on ethics, compassion, and
holistic patient care, which prepares them to become competent and
empathetic medical professionals. Many alumni highlight that the college
encourages research initiatives, extracurricular involvement, and leadership
development, fostering both personal and professional growth. Overall,


--- Page 108 ---
students feel well-prepared to serve society and pursue successful careers
in medicine.

Overall : Students appreciate Believers Church Medical College for its
excellent academics, clinical exposure, and supportive faculty. The campus
provides a safe, inclusive environment with modern facilities, preparing
them well for a professional medical career.

Parent Review:

Parents of students at Believers Church Medical College highly appreciate
the institution’s commitment to academic excellence, ethical values, and
holistic development. They note that the college provides a safe and
nurturing environment, with separate hostels for boys and girls, hygienic
mess facilities, and strict security measures, ensuring their children’s
well-being. Parents value the Christ-centered approach, which instills
compassion, integrity, and social responsibility in students alongside
rigorous medical training. The college’s emphasis on practical clinical
exposure, modern infrastructure, and experienced faculty reassures
parents that their children are receiving top-quality education and hands-on
learning. Many parents also highlight the college’s support for research,
extracurricular activities, and personal development, which helps students
grow into well-rounded professionals. Overall, parents feel confident that
BCMC equips their children with the skills, knowledge, and values
necessary to become competent and empathetic medical practitioners,
ready to serve society effectively.

Mission Medical College

and student support systems. Believers Church Mission Medical College,

offering MBBS and PG programs, backed by a large multi-specialty
teaching hospital that caters to patients from Central Kerala and
neighboring districts.

Student Perspective

e The college follows a systematic academic structure with regular
internal assessments, well-planned postings, and curriculum-oriented
teaching.

e Strong clinical exposure is provided through the attached Believers
Church Medical College Hospital, which experiences high patient
inflow across multiple specialties.

e Faculty members are regarded as experienced, approachable, and
academically supportive, especially in clinical departments.


--- Page 110 ---

Overall Assessment

Believers Church Mission Medical College offers a robust medical
education ecosystem supported by a high-volume tertiary care hospital.

exposure, the institution provides an environment well-suited for serious

clinical learning within a structured and disciplined framework.

LOGO

Medical College History & Introduction
Sree Gokulam Medical College & Research Foundation (GSGMC&RF) was
established in 2004 on a scenic 40-acre green campus and is managed by
the Foundation of Non-Resident Indians Trust. Founded with the vision of
becoming a centre of excellence in medical education, healthcare delivery,
and meaningful research, the institution is affiliated with Kerala University
of Health Sciences (KUHS). The teaching hospital was also established in
2004 with the mission of providing quality healthcare at affordable costs to
all sections of society. In December 2005, the institution was dedicated to
the nation by Dr. A. P. J. Abdul Kalam, the then Honourable President of
India.
The college, envisioned by its Chairman, Sree Gokulam Gopalan, admitted
its first batch of 50 MBBS students in 2005 and has since expanded
significantly. Today, it admits 150 undergraduate medical students annually,
along with more than 50 postgraduate and postdoctoral students across
various specialties, over 100 students in undergraduate and postgraduate


--- Page 121 ---
nursing programs, and more than 50 students each year in para-clinical
courses. The institution remains affiliated with KUHS, Thrissur, and aligned
with the regulatory standards of the Medical Council of India (now NMC).
The vision of the institution is to emerge as a centre of excellence and set
new standards in medical education, healthcare delivery, and meaningful
medical research. Medical college hospital has a vision to provide quality
health care at an affordable cost to all the sections of our society.The
mission of the institution is to provide excellent medical education for
undergraduate, postgraduate, and post-doctoral students, shaping them
into competent and conscientious doctors with strong ethical and social
values. The _ institution is committed to delivering compassionate,
high-quality healthcare to patients from all sections of society and
continuously upgrading its learning resources and infrastructure to meet the
evolving demands of evidence-based medical education, healthcare, and
research.
Basic College Profile

e Sree Gokulam Medical College & Research Foundation was

established in 2004.

e The medical college hospital was established in 2004 .

e Institution Type: Private Self-Financing Medical College.

e Campus: The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located

in Trivandrum city.

e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)

e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences.

e Recognised by: National Medical Commission (NMC)

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust &
Research Foundation are processed via Commissioner for Entrance


--- Page 124 ---
Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized counselling /
web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g.Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust & Research Foundation) +
quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your eligibility &
preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e lf a seat is allotted to you at Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust &
Research Foundation, you get an allotment memo / letter.

5.Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust & Research
Foundation within deadline with original certificates: NEET scorecard,
10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer / conduct
certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable), ID proof,
birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.


--- Page 125 ---
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust & Research Foundation with
all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
e Central Library : A well-established central library with a wide
collection of national and international medical textbooks, journals,
e-resources, reading halls, and digital access facilities for students
and faculty.
e Skill Lab:

o Clinical Skill Laboratory . provides hands-on _ learning
experiences to the medical fraternity for the practice of clinical
skills, which are deemed essential for the effective and safe
management of patients prior to facing a real patient
population.

o Faculty members are trained by Kerala University of Health
Sciences under the ‘Training the Trainers Program’ as well as
by the college organised workshops on Creation of E-Learning
Materials. Utilisation of the Laboratory by various departments
is by booking slots as required, through the Departmental
Secretary of Department of Anaesthesiology & Critical Care.


--- Page 138 ---
e Lecture Theatre & Halls : Spacious, air-conditioned lecture theatres,
demonstration rooms, and seminar halls fitted with smart boards,
projectors, and advanced audio-visual teaching systems.

e Wi-Fi & LAN : Campus-wide high-speed Wi-Fi and LAN connectivity
supporting digital learning, online resources, and academic research
activities.

e Auditoriums / Exam Halls : Dedicated auditoriums for academic
events, conferences, and seminars, along with well-structured
examination halls for internal assessments and_ university
examinations.

e Central & Research Lab : Central laboratory and research facilities
supporting diagnostics, academic projects, institutional research, and
postgraduate studies.

e Museums : Well-maintained anatomy, pathology, and forensic
medicine museums with specimens, models, charts, and digital aids
to enhance conceptual learning.

e Student Lab : Multiple student laboratories across preclinical and
paraclinical departments for practical training, experiments,
dissections, and hands-on academic sessions.

e Bank & ATM : On-campus banking facilities and ATM services for
students, staff, patients, and visitors.

e Cafeteria : Hygienic and affordable cafeteria serving a variety of
meals, snacks, and beverages for students, faculty, and hospital
visitors.

e Day Care : Day care facility available for children of staff and
healthcare workers, ensuring a supportive work-study environment.


--- Page 139 ---
e Buggy Service :_ Internal transport/buggy services for patient
movement and mobility support within the campus.

e Parking Service : Designated parking areas for students, staff,
patients, and visitors with organized traffic management.

e Shops & Parlours : On-campus convenience stores, medical shops,
and personal care parlours catering to daily needs.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Sree Gokulam Medical College strongly promotes researchers at all
levels. Various undergraduate, postgraduate and faculty research
projects are being carried out with inter-disciplinary and external
collaborations.

e All the postgraduate students are required to complete a thesis in
their respective disciplines in two-years as a part of the requirement
of their course completion.

e Undergraduate students are encouraged to take up short,
community-based projects, of which, some have applied for and
received ICMR funding.

e All the postgraduate departments have been recognised as research
centres by the Kerala University of Health Sciences.

e The institution encourages community service through health camps,
NSS activities, and outreach programs, helping students develop
social responsibility alongside clinical competence.

e Ethics Committee : All the research projects in the institution are
scrutinized independently from the viewpoint of ethical issues and


--- Page 140 ---
project management by a strong and efficient Institutional Ethics
Committee.

e Institutional Research Cell: All the research projects in the institution
are scrutinised for scientific aspects and use of sound and
appropriate research methodology prior to the submission of the
protocols for the approval of the Institutional Ethics Committee. IRC in
collaboration with the Department of Community Medicine also
conducts various workshops to train the faculty and students (both
undergraduate & postgraduate).

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Teaching Hospital: 880 to 900+ bed multi-specialty hospital

e Operation Theatres: 17 modern, fully equipped OTs

e ICU Beds: ~100 (MICU, SICU, NICU, PICU, CCU, Trauma ICU)

e Emergency & Trauma Care: 24x7 emergency services with
advanced trauma support

e Blood Bank: Well-equipped and NABH-standard blood bank

e Patient Inflow: ~1,200—1,500 OPD patients per day with steady IPD
admissions

e Clinical Exposure: Strong hands-on training for MBBS students from
early years through ward postings, emergency duties, and specialty
rotations.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments: SGMC offers major
specialties like Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, OBG, Orthopedics,
ENT, Ophthalmology, Psychiatry, Radiology, and Anesthesiology,
along with super-specialties including Cardiology, Neurology,


--- Page 141 ---
Nephrology, Gastroenterology, Pulmonology, Urology, Neurosurgery,
and Plastic Surgery, ensuring strong clinical exposure.
Campus Life

e Fests and Events: The college union, Navodhan, organizes annual
inter-batch sports and arts festivals (cultural fests) that feature events
like arm wrestling, makeovers, and music concerts.

e Clubs and Communities: There are student-led clubs for music,
sports, and literature. Charitable groups like "Jeevan" (for blood
donation) and "Thanal" (for geriatric and social care) also exist,
promoting community service.

e Hangout Spots: Popular spots for students to socialize include the
college lobby, the cafeteria, the on-campus restaurant Cilantro, and a
nearby hilltop or the college terrace for scenic views

e Learning & IT: The campus has a central library, skill labs, lecture
halls equipped with smart technology, auditoriums, and campus-wide
Wi-Fi/LAN connectivity.

e Recreation & Sports: Facilities include an indoor stadium, outdoor
playgrounds, a swimming pool, gymnasium, and courts for basketball,
football, and cricket. Indoor games like table tennis and carroms are
also available.

e General Amenities: Other on-campus facilities include a cafeteria, a
restaurant called Cilantro, bank and ATM services, shops, and
separate hostels for boys and girls.


--- Page 142 ---
Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Sree Gokulam Medical College (SGMC) provides separate,
well-maintained hostel facilities for both boys and girls with good
infrastructure and a common mess system. The annual fee for hostel
and mess is approximately =1,73,198/- per year.

e The college provides separate, well-maintained hostels for male and
female students with comfortable rooms, adequate ventilation, and
round-the-clock security.

e Hostels are located within or close to the campus, ensuring easy
access to academic and hospital facilities.

e The mess offers hygienic, nutritious, and balanced meals catering to
diverse dietary preferences. Clean dining halls, regular food quality
checks, and student feedback systems help maintain consistent
standards and overall student satisfaction.

Safety & Support Systems

e 24/7 Surveillance: The campus is under continuous CCTV
surveillance with a dedicated security team.

e Controlled Access: Entrance to student hostels is strictly regulated;
residents must be present by 10:00 PM and sign an in-out register for
any campus departure.

e Infrastructure Maintenance: A Biomedical Engineering Department
ensures all medical equipment is tested and safe, while a dedicated
CSSD manages the 24/7 sterilization of surgical tools.


--- Page 143 ---
Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Sree Gokulam Medical College provides strong internship placement
quality with in-house postings across all major clinical and
super-specialty departments, ensuring comprehensive hands-on
training.

e In-house placement for interns is strong: final-year students and fresh
graduates normally get their internship posting inside the parent
teaching hospital (the mandatory 12-month rotatory internship occurs
at the teaching hospital). That gives direct access to wards, OT, ICU
and specialty clinics.

e After internship many graduates either take jobs at hospitals, or
pursue PG entrance.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)

e Anti-Ragging: SGMC strictly prohibits ragging and operates an
Anti-Ragging Core Committee (ARCC). Incidents can be reported via
a toll-free helpline at 1800 891 8992.

e Grievance Redressal: A Student Grievance Redressal Committee
manages complaints through a formal investigation process.

e Gender Sensitization: An Internal Complaints Committee and
Gender Harassment Grievance Redressal Committee provide a safe
environment for reporting misconduct.

e Mentorship & Welfare: Includes a Student Support Guidance
Program (SSGP) to assist with academic and personal challenges.


--- Page 144 ---
Sree Gokulam Medical College Trust & Research Foundation
— Student & Parent Review

Student Review

Students generally appreciate the college for its modern infrastructure,
supportive faculty, and structured academic environment. The classrooms,
laboratories, library, and skill labs are well-equipped, making learning
efficient and interactive. Clinical exposure is considered good, with steady
patient inflow allowing students to gain practical experience across major
specialties.

Campus life is described as balanced, with decent hostel and mess
facilities, active student activities, and a peaceful atmosphere. While
academics are demanding, students feel well-guided through mentoring
and departmental support, making SGMC a dependable choice for medical
education.

Overall : Sree Gokulam Medical College offers strong academics, modern
infrastructure, and good clinical exposure in a supportive learning
environment. Overall, it is a reliable institution for quality medical education
with balanced campus life.

Parent review

Parents appreciate Sree Gokulam Medical College for its strong academic
standards, disciplined environment, and focus on student safety and
wellbeing. The faculty are experienced and approachable, providing proper
guidance throughout the course. Modern infrastructure, well-equipped
laboratories, and good hospital exposure reassure parents about the


--- Page 145 ---
quality of training their children receive. Hostel and mess facilities are
considered satisfactory, with adequate security and support services.
Parents also value the structured campus life, which balances academics
with extracurricular activities. Overall, SGMC is viewed as a reliable
institution that offers a safe, supportive, and academically sound
environment for medical education and professional development.
Overall: Parents are satisfied with the college’s academic quality, safety,
and disciplined environment. Overall, Sree Gokulam Medical College is
seen as a reliable and supportive institution for medical education.

Way to reach

By Road

The college is located right on Main Central (MC) Road.

e From Trivandrum City: It's about a 25-30 km drive (roughly 45-60
minutes).

e Bus Services: Frequent KSRTC and private buses running between
Trivandrum and Kottayam/MC Road stop at Venjaramoodu. From the
Venjaramoodu bus stand, the college is just a short auto-rickshaw
ride away.

By Rail

e Thiruvananthapuram Central (TVC): The major railway station is
approximately 28 km away. You can easily find taxis or take a bus
from the Thampanoor bus station (opposite the railway station)
towards Venjaramoodu.

By Air

e Trivandrum International Airport (TRV): The airport is about 32 km
from the campus. Pre-paid taxis are available at the terminal, and the
journey typically takes about an hour depending on traffic.

aS, Government

T.D. MEDICAL COLLEGE

el Zee Vandanam, Alappuzha
LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Established in 1963 under the patronage of the Anantha Narayana Puram
Thirumala Devaswom (T.D.) Temple, Government T.D. Medical College
(TDMC) in Alappuzha holds the distinction of being the first medical
college in Kerala started under private management. Founded by the
visionary Sri N.V. Prabhu, the institution began its academic journey with an
initial batch of 50 MBBS students on August 17, 1963. Due to financial
challenges, the Kerala Government. assumed management in 1967 and
officially took full ownership on October 17, 1972, making it the state's
fourth government medical college. Today, the college and its hospital are
fully integrated on a massive 162-acre campus at Vandanam, serving as
a premier center for medical education and healthcare in the region.
The number of seats for the M.B.B.S course in T.D. Medical College,
Alappuzha was 50 to begin with. It was raised to 100 in 1967. But as per
the recommendation of the Indian Medical Council, the number was again
reduced to 80 in 1973. It was again raised to 100 as per the
recommendation of the Indian Medical Council in 1979.Now the


--- Page 157 ---
number of seats has been raised to 150 from the academic year
2007-08 onwards. Post Graduate Course in Medicine and Surgery (2
seats each) were started in the year 1982-83 and the Paramedical Course
for MLT was started in the year 1985-86 with 15 seats. Diploma Course in
Pharmacy was also started with 35 seats and later it increased to 40 seats.
The Government T.D. Medical College (TDMC) Alappuzha envisions
providing the best healthcare facilities to the people of Kerala by
developing the institute into a Centre of Excellence in all aspects of modern
medicine. Its mission is to maintain a state-of-the-art medical college that is
fully equipped in all respects and to produce excellent medical
professionals with a strong academic base and sound _ technical
competence who can effectively serve the community. Furthermore, the
college strives to be a pioneer medical institution at par with the best
medical colleges in the country while offering education with care and
quality.

Vision

To provide best Health Care facilities to the people of Kerala by developing
this Institute as a Centre of Excellence in every aspect of Modern Medicine.
Mission

To have a state of the art Medical College fully equipped in all respects. To
produce excellent Medical professionals with strong academic base and
sound technical competence who can effectively serve the community. To


--- Page 158 ---
make it a Pioneer Medical Institution at par with the best Medical College of
the Country.

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

T D Medical College, Alleppey

e Total Hospital Beds: Approximately 1,050 beds.

e Total ICU Beds: The hospital has a total of 55 ICU beds in the old
building complex, which includes a recently expanded 37-bed
Multidisciplinary ICU (MDICU), a 9-bed Emergency ICU, and a 9-bed
Trauma ICU. Additionally, there are dedicated specialized units like
the 14-bed Intensive Coronary Care Unit (ICCU) and a 9-bed Cath
ICU.

e Total Operation Theatres: The facility includes multiple specialized
operation theatres, including those in the Super Speciality Block.

e Total Outpatients: The hospital records a high patient volume,
seeing more than 2,000 outpatients daily.


--- Page 160 ---
e Emergency Services: Provides 24/7 emergency care and trauma
services, with round-the-clock lab, X-ray, and scanning departments.

e Hospital Accreditation: Affiliated with the Kerala University of
Health Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the National Medical
Commission (NMC). It also holds recognitions from the Indian
Nursing Council (INC) and Pharmacy Council of India (PCI).

e Clinical Exposure: Students receive extensive hands-on training
due to the hospital's high patient load and diverse speciality
departments covering everything from general medicine to advanced
super-specialties like Cardiology and Neurosurgery.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

Step 1: Entrance Examination & KEAM Registration
You must appear for the NEET-UG 2026 exam (conducted by NTA),
as it is the sole basis for medical admission.

e KEAM Registration: Even though admission is via NEET, you
must register on the Kerala CEE portal (cee.kerala.gov.in).

e Document Upload: You must upload your Nativity proof (to
claim Keralite status), Class 10 certificate, and Category
certificates during this initial phase.

Step 2: Result Submission & Option Registration
Once the NEET-UG results are declared (expected June 2026), you
must link your scores to your KEAM application.

e NEET Score Submission: Log in to the KEAM candidate portal
and enter your NEET roll number and score.

e Option Entry: During the "Centralised Allotment Process"
(CAP), you will list your college preferences. To get into TDMC
Alappuzha, you should place it high on your list.

Step 3: Allotment, Fee Payment & Physical Reporting
If your rank meets the cutoff for TDMC Alappuzha, you will receive an
allotment memo.

e Acceptance: Download the Allotment Memo and pay the
required tuition fee (approx. ¥31,570 for the first year) via the
CEE portal or designated bank branches.

e Physical Reporting: You must physically visit the TDMC
Alappuzha campus with all original documents (TC, Conduct
Certificate, Marksheets, and Physical Fitness Certificate) to
verify your identity and confirm your seat.


--- Page 163 ---
e Finalization: Once the college office verifies your documents
and the "Data Sheet" from CEE, your admission is officially
recorded.

Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Halls & Classrooms: The college features modern,
spacious lecture halls equipped with Smart Boards, audio-visual aids,
and full automation for interactive learning. Specific halls, such as the


--- Page 180 ---
New Anatomy Lecture Hall, cater to large batches of up to 175
students.

e Central Library: Located on the ground floor of the main
administrative block, the library spans approximately 7,200 sq. ft..

© Collection: Holds over 24,000 medical books, 8,700+ bound
volumes, and a vast array of journals, atlases, and
encyclopedias.

o Special Sections: Includes a General Reference Section,
Journal Section, Book Bank, and an air-conditioned Internet
Section.

o Digital Resources: The Learning Resource Centre (LRC)
provides high-speed internet (leased line), a Linux server, and
13 PC workstations with access to databases like Science
Direct and UpToDate.

e Laboratories & Museums: Every department (pre-clinical,
para-clinical, and clinical) is equipped with specialized laboratories
and departmental museums for practical training.

e Auditorium: A large, dedicated auditorium is situated deep within the
campus for academic conferences, seminars, and graduation
ceremonies.

e SYNAPSE 25: A major resident and alumni get-together was held in
Alappuzha on December 21, 2025.

e Medical Education: The college conducted a specialized Foundation
Course for the 2025 MBBS batch in October 2025, led by Principal
Dr. B. Padmakumar


--- Page 181 ---
e Ethical Oversight: Research is strictly governed by the Institutional
Research Committee (IRC) and the Institutional Ethics Committee
(IEC), the latter being registered with both CDSCO and DHR.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e The hospital transitioned from the old Alappuzha District Hospital to a
unified complex at the Vandanam campus, spanning 60 acres of the
total 162-acre site.

e Bed Capacity: Currently operates with 1,050+ beds, ensuring a
massive inpatient volume.

e Patient Inflow: The hospital manages an average daily
outpatient (OP) attendance of 2,500 to 3,000 patients, offering
students exposure to a vast spectrum of pathologies.

e PMSSY Super-Specialty Block: A state-of-the-art multi-story
block funded by the Pradhan Mantri Swasthya Suraksha
Yojana. It. houses advanced departments like Cardiology,
Neurology, and Nephrology with modern ICUs and modular
operation theaters.

e Emergency & Trauma: A 24/7 Casualty and Trauma Care unit
that handles high-velocity road traffic accidents (given its
location on NH 66) and medical emergencies.

e Mother & Child Block: Dedicated wings for Obstetrics &
Gynaecology and Paediatrics, including a high-tech Neonatal
ICU (NICU).


--- Page 182 ---
e Cardiology Center: Features a dedicated Cath Lab performing
over 1,200 echocardiographies and 200+ interventional
procedures (Angioplasty, Pacemakers) monthly.

e Radiotherapy Unit: One of the few government centers in
Central Kerala equipped with a Linear Accelerator (LINAC) and
Cobalt units for comprehensive cancer care.

Campus Life

1. Student Union & Events: The active college union organizes
numerous events throughout the year, ensuring a dynamic
atmosphere.

2. Sports Culture: The college is well known for its strong sports
culture and is often referred to as a "sports college" among other
institutions in the state.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Accommodation: Separate hostels for boys and girls, with additional
specific accommodation for interns, residents, and nursing students.
The rooms are typically shared by three students and include
furnishings such as beds, study tables, shelves, cupboards, lights,
and fans.

Mess Facilities

e Availability: Mess facilities are present within the campus for all hostel
residents and staff.

e Food Quality: Student opinions on food quality vary, ranging from
"good" for the boys' mess to "average" or "inconsistent" in general,
but the canteens and dining areas are noted for their cleanliness. The


--- Page 183 ---
menu can sometimes change based on the wishes of the cooking
staff.
Safety & Support Systems

e Hostel Security: Female hostels have dedicated wardens and strict
evening curfews to ensure student safety. Entry for outsiders is
strictly regulated .

e Anti-Ragging Committee: In compliance with UGC and NMC
regulations, the college maintains a _ proactive Anti-Ragging
Committee and Squad. Freshers are provided with emergency
contact numbers for immediate assistance.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Case Diversity: As the primary tertiary care center for Alappuzha
and nearby districts, interns manage a high patient load (over 2,000
outpatients. daily), providing extensive hands-on experience in
emergency care, common tropical diseases, and super-specialty
interventions.

e Learning Curve: The one-year Compulsory Rotating Residential
Internship (CRRI) is widely regarded as an excellent learning curve,
where students develop clinical reasoning and practical skills across
all major medical and surgical disciplines.

e Placement Status: In medical education, "placements" refer to the
transition into professional practice. Approximately 82% to 90% of
graduates secure roles in reputed hospitals or government health
services shortly after their internship.


--- Page 184 ---
e Post-Graduation: A significant majority of interns utilize the clinical
experience to prepare for the NEET-PG exam, with many securing
seats in top-tier specialized MD/MS programs.

Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
Figures
MBBS Interns (House Surgeons)

e Stipend: Approximately $25,000 to ¥27,000 per month.

e Duration: 12 months of mandatory Compulsory Rotatory Residential
Internship (CRRI).

Postgraduate (MD/MS) Residents
Stipends for Junior Residents (PG students) in Kerala government
medical colleges. are structured with annual increments:
e 1st Year: 57,876 per month.
e 2nd Year: $58,968 per month.
e 3rd Year: 60,060 per month.
College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Zero Tolerance Policy: Ragging is considered a cognizable offense.
As of 2026, the college reports zero incidents due to strict monitoring.

e Mandatory Affidavits: Both students and parents must submit
signed anti-ragging undertakings and affidavits at the time of
admission.


--- Page 185 ---
e Ladies' hostels have strict entry/exit timings monitored by a dedicated
warden. While male hostels are generally more flexible, 24-hour
security with CCTV is maintained at all entrances.

e Prohibited Activities: Consumption of alcohol, drugs, and smoking is
strictly forbidden on campus and in residential areas.

GMA Verdict

T D Medical College, Alappuzha, is a clinically strong, academically
reliable, and cost-effective institution for medical education. With
unmatched patient exposure, experienced faculty, and government-backed
affordability, the college offers exceptional value for MBBS and PG
aspirants.

GMA strongly recommends T D Medical College for students who prioritize
Clinical competence, real-world exposure, and academic rigor within
Kerala’s government medical education system.

Way to reach

To reach Government T.D. Medical College in Vandanam, Alappuzha
(688005), you can use the following methods:

e By Rail: The most convenient way is via Alappuzha Railway Station
(ALLP), located approximately 7 km from the campus, where taxis
and auto-rickshaws are readily available. [1]

e By Air: The nearest major airport is Cochin International Airport
(COK), about 83 km away; from there, you can take a pre-paid taxi or
a bus for the roughly 2.5-hour journey. [1]

e By Road: The college is situated directly on NH 66 (9 km south of
Alappuzha town), making it easily accessible via KSRTC or private
buses running between Kochi and Thiruvananthapuram. [1]
