LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Govt.Medical College, Kozhikode( Calicut medical College) is a premier
medical college located in the city of Kozhikode in Kerala. It was
established in 1957 as the second medical college in Kerala. Since then
the institution has grown into a premier centre of medical education in the
state. The vast and sprawling Medical College campus is spread over an
extensive area of 270 acres (1.1 km?) and is located about 8 km east from
the heart of Kozhikode city. It was formerly affiliated to the University of
Calicut and now to the Kerala University for Health Sciences (KUHS). This
college and allied institutions serve 40% of the population of Kerala.
The foundation stone of the college was laid on 29 May 1957 by the then
Governor of Kerala, Dr. B. Ramakrishna Rao. The College was formally
inaugurated on 5 August 1957 by the then minister of Health, Kerala state
Dr. A. R. Menon, whose initiative and zeal were responsible for the
establishment of the institution. Dr. K. N. Pisharoty, the first principal, was
responsible for the task of organizing the college.
The main hospital was commissioned in 1966 with 1183 beds. The present
bed strength is 3025.From its modest beginning, the institution has grown


--- Page 194 ---
steadily for more than 57 years. The annual intake of undergraduate
students has been increased from 50 to 250. The consolidation of
undergraduate medical education was achieved in the 1960s. The 1970s
witnessed the establishment and expansion of postgraduate medical
education in various branches.
The vision of the college is to be a premier Medical college in the country
providing socially committed medical graduates to the society.And mission
is to discover and translate new knowledge in the field of medical sciences
to provide cutting-edge, interdisciplinary and compassionate care of the
highest quality to improve the health of the people we serve.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration
e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.


--- Page 197 ---
e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).

e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-I) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal
(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE
portal when the window opens.
All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).

2. Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College,Calicut" as one of your preferred
choices.

e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.

3 .College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the Government Medical College,Calicut campus within the
stipulated timeframe for document verification and final admission.

Infrastructure & Facilities
Lecture Halls: The campus features multiple spacious, gallery-style lecture
theaters. A newer Lecture Theater Complex has been developed to
accommodate the increased annual intake of 250 MBBS students.
Laboratories: Every pre-clinical and para-clinical department (such as
Anatomy, Physiology, and Pathology) is equipped with high-end
laboratories. The college also houses a Multidisciplinary Research Unit
(MRU) for advanced scientific inquiry.


--- Page 215 ---
Museums: Specialized departmental museums (e.g., Forensic Medicine
and Anatomy) house extensive collections of specimens and models for
student reference.

Medical Education Technology (MET) Unit: GMC Calicut hosts an
MCl-recognized Regional Centre for MET, which provides training for
faculty from 12 other medical colleges.

Central Library: A dedicated, multi-story library building that operates
24/7. It houses an extensive collection of medical textbooks, journals, and
digital resources.

e Digital Library: Includes a server and 23 terminals with 24-hour
broadband access to global medical databases.

e Departmental Libraries: Every postgraduate department maintains its
own specialized library for focused research.

Auditoriums: The campus features large auditoriums, such as Aurora, for
seminars, guest lectures, and cultural events.

Sports & Recreation: Extensive facilities including a large ground with a
synthetic track, football field, cricket nets, and courts for basketball and
volleyball. A well-equipped college gym is also available.

Clinical Training Infrastructure

The college is attached to several major tertiary care hospitals that
provide massive clinical exposure due to high patient volume:

e Main Hospital & SSB: Features a multistoried Super Specialty Block
(SSB) with advanced facilities like a Cardiac Cath Lab, MRI scans,
and digital radiography.

e Specialized Institutes: Includes the Institute of Maternal and Child
Health (IMCH) with 1,100 beds ,the Institute of Chest Diseases, the


--- Page 216 ---
Institute of Mental Health & Neuroscience (IMHANS), Institute of
Palliative Medicine (IPM)[WHOcollaboration centre].

e Departmental Museums: Used for teaching and showcasing
anatomical and pathological specimens.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Rankings: Consistently ranked among the top 25 medical colleges in
India by major ranking bodies like IIRF and Collegedunia, maintaining
a high clinical placement performance score.

e KIRF Recognition: The_ institution received an appreciation
certificate from the Kerala Institutional Ranking Framework (KIRF) in
February 2025 for its excellence in higher education.

e Arts College Literature Festival: While technically an arts event, the
medical students often collaborate with the neighboring Government
Arts and Science College for this massive literary gathering.

e Multidisciplinary Research Unit (MRU): A central hub for advanced
medical research, facilitating studies in clinical epidemiology and
diagnostics.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity-Government Medical College (GMC) Calicut is widely
recognized as the largest bedded hospital in India. As of 2026, the
total sanctioned bed capacity across all its constituent units is 3,025
beds.

e ICU beds & Operation Theatres:GMC Calicut features over 300 ICU
beds, including a massive 190-bed critical care wing in the Super


--- Page 217 ---
Specialty Block, and more than 40 Operation Theatres, featuring 19
high-end modular suites for advanced procedures like organ
transplants.

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD): Approximately 8,000 to 10,000+ patients
visit the various OPDs daily.According to official data submitted for
NIRF 2025, the average daily OPD attendance is recorded at 4,427
for the main medical college unit alone, though the combined number
across all specialized centers (IMCH, SSB, Chest, etc.) is much
higher.The hospital records over 1,00,000+ admissions annually
across all its constituent units.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments: Government Medical
College, Calicut offers a wide range of specialty departments
including Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, OBG, Orthopaedics, ENT,
Ophthalmology, Psychiatry, and diagnostic sciences. Super-specialty
services include Cardiology, Neurology, Neurosurgery, Nephrology,
Gastroenterology, Oncology, Urology, | Endocrinology, and
Cardiothoracic Surgery, providing comprehensive tertiary care and
Clinical training.

Campus Life

e Arts & Cultural Festivals: The campus hosts a number of cultural
programs, inter-batch arts festivals, film fests, and musical concerts,
with major events like the annual Calicut MedFest. Festivals such as
Onam, Eid, and Christmas are celebrated by the student community.

e Clubs & Societies: Various student-run clubs are available,
including:

o Literary Club


--- Page 218 ---
o Nature Club

o Debate and Quiz Clubs

o Social Service Club (Imprints is a widely acclaimed charity
program run by students)

e Sports: A strong emphasis is placed on physical fitness and
sportsmanship. The college features excellent facilities including a
large ground with a synthetic running track, a football field, cricket
nets, and courts for basketball and volleyball. Annual and
inter-college sports meets are held regularly, with winners competing
at state levels.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Government Medical College,Calicut.. provides separate hostel
facilities for male and female students within or close to the campus,
ensuring safe, comfortable, and convenient accommodation.

e The hostel mess facilities are centrally managed. and provide
hygienic, nutritious, and affordable meals to students.

e Adequate provisions for drinking water, sanitation, electricity, and
round-the-clock security are available.

e Warden supervision and administrative support ensure discipline,
safety, and smooth functioning of hostel life, contributing to a
conducive academic and living atmosphere.

Safety & Support Systems

e Anti-Ragging Policy: The institution enforces a strict anti-ragging

policy as per the Kerala Prohibition of Ragging Act, 1998.


--- Page 219 ---
o An Anti-Ragging Committee is constituted with the Principal as
chairman and various officials as members.

o Awareness is maintained through posters and guidelines.

o All students and their parents must sign anti-ragging affidavits
at the time of admission.

o The college works to maintain a supportive senior-junior
relationship and a ragging-free environment

e Hostel Security: The campus provides separate, secure hostels for
both male and female students with round-the-clock security. Visitors
must register their details, and unauthorized access is strictly
monitored.

e Campus Monitoring: Corridors and sensitive areas are well-lit and
covered by CCTV cameras to ensure a monitored environment for
staff and students.

e Emergency Services: Students have access to immediate
on-campus medical support, including first aid availability, necessary
medical equipment, and ambulance services during emergencies.

e Counselling Services: Students experiencing mental stress or
personal problems can avail of counselling services. The college
provides internal and external counsellors for periodic sessions and
one-on-one advice.

e Student Welfare: The Students’ Union actively addresses student
issues and organizes social service programs, fostering a strong
community spirit.

e Grievance Redressal: A system is in place for students to register
complaints or suggestions regarding hostel facilities (e.g., mess


--- Page 220 ---
hygiene) or other campus issues, which are then addressed by
authorities like the Warden or Assistant Warden.

e Women's Safety: The campus is considered women-friendly, with
specific measures to address safety and wellness, including
increased washrooms, sanitary disposal corners, and_ specific
guidelines for hostel access times for female students.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Clinical Exposure: Unmatched. Due to the massive patient load
(8,000+ OPD daily), interns perform a high volume of hands-on
procedures (suturing, intubation, deliveries, and assisting in major
surgeries) that students in private colleges rarely experience.

e Stipend (2025-2026): Approximately $26,000 — %28,000 per month.
While modest compared to Central Institutes (like AIIMS), it is
competitive within the state government sector, with periodic hikes
(usually 5% annually).

e Skill Development: Interns graduate with high clinical confidence. By
the end of the year, most are capable of managing casualty
(emergency) rooms independently, making them highly sought after
for Junior Resident (JR) positions in private hospitals.

e Placement "Value": While there are no formal "campus placements"
(standard for MBBS), the brand value of GMC Calicut is immense.
Completing an internship here is a significant advantage for securing
jobs in corporate hospitals or for pursuing PG abroad.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)
Anti-Ragging Measures
GMC Kozhikode maintains a zero-tolerance policy toward ragging.

e Committee & Squad: An active Anti-Ragging Committee (chaired by
the Principal) and a mobile squad conduct surprise checks in hostels
and common areas.

e Mandatory Affidavits: Both students and parents must submit signed
anti-ragging undertakings at the time of admission.

e Severe Penalties: Violations can lead to immediate suspension,
forfeiture of campus placements, or expulsion. Under the Kerala
Prohibition of Ragging Act, offenders may also face up to two years
of imprisonment.


--- Page 222 ---
Grievance Redressal Mechanism
e Formal Channel: Students can voice concerns regarding academic,
administrative, or personal matters through the Student Grievance
Redressal Committee.
e Counselling & Support: Dedicated counselling services are available
to help students manage academic pressure and personal issues.
e Administrative Hierarchy: Routine issues should be communicated
through the Class Coordinator to the Principal
Hostel regulations : Students will be under the disciplinary control of the
assistant wardens and the wardens.The hostels (separate for men and
women) are governed by strict codes of conduct.
Government Medical College, Calicut - Student & Parent
Review
Student Review:
Government Medical College, Kozhikode is highly regarded by students for
its strong academics, experienced faculty, and exceptional clinical
exposure due to its very high patient inflow. The hospital infrastructure and
wide range of specialty and super-specialty departments provide excellent
hands-on learning and case diversity.
Students appreciate the supportive academic environment, active campus
life, and opportunities for research and extracurricular activities. While the
workload is demanding, most students feel it prepares them well for
postgraduate entrance exams and future clinical practice, making GMC
Kozhikode one of the top government medical colleges in Kerala.


--- Page 223 ---
Overall : Government Medical College, Kozhikode is a premier medical
institution known for excellent academics, outstanding clinical exposure,
experienced faculty, and strong overall student satisfaction.

Parent Review:

Parents regard Government Medical College, Kozhikode as one of the
most reliable and prestigious medical institutions in Kerala. They appreciate
the strong academic framework, experienced faculty, and the excellent
Clinical exposure provided through its large tertiary care hospital with high
patient inflow. Parents feel reassured by the disciplined campus
environment, strict anti-ragging policies, and well-functioning grievance
redressal systems that ensure student safety and welfare.

The hostel facilities are generally considered safe and well-managed, with
proper supervision and essential amenities. Parents also value the
availability of counseling and student support services that help students
manage academic stress. The _ institution’s emphasis on ethics,
professionalism, and compassionate patient care is highly appreciated.
Overall, parents feel confident that GMC Kozhikode offers their children
quality education, strong career prospects, and a supportive environment
that promotes both academic excellence and personal growth.

Overall : Parents view Government Medical College, Kozhikode as a highly

exposure, and a safe, disciplined environment. They feel confident about
their child’s education, career prospects, and overall well-being at the
college.

Way to reach

GMC Calicut is located about 8 km from the heart of Kozhikode (Calicut)
city. It is well-connected by road, rail, and air.

1. By Road (Local & Long Distance)

The road is the most convenient way to reach the campus once you are in
the city.

e From City Center (Mananchira/Railway Station): You can take a
green city bus labeled "Medical College" from the bus stop near the
Income Tax office (Mananchira). The ride takes about 20-30 minutes.

e From KSRTC Bus Stand: Direct buses are available from the KSRTC
stand on Mavoor Road.

e Auto/Taxi: Readily available across the city. A trip from the railway
station to the Medical College Junction typically costs between %150
and 250.


--- Page 227 ---
2. By Train

e Nearest Major Station: Kozhikode Main (CLT), which is approximately
8 km away. Most major trains from across India stop here.

e Local Station: West Hill (WH) is technically closer (~6 km), but only
local passenger trains stop there. For most travelers, Kozhikode Main
is the better option.

3. By Air

e Nearest Airport: Calicut International Airport (CCJ), located in Karipur.

e Distance: Approximately 26 km from the college.

e Commute: You can take a prepaid taxi directly to the college (around
45-60 minutes) or take a bus from the airport to Kozhikode city and
then transfer to a local bus.

Medical College History & Introduction

Government Medical College Ernakulam (GMCE) is one of the premier
medical institutions in Kerala, known for its excellence in medical
education, research, and healthcare. It was a government-owned institution
established by the Co-operative Academy of Professional
Education(CAPE) under the Department of Co-operation, Government of
Kerala, established in 1999.. The institution was formally taken over by the
Government of Kerala on December 17, 2013 and is now entirely managed
under state administration. Admissions and academic operations follow the
rules and regulations set by the government, ensuring a standardized and
quality-driven approach to medical education.

With a dedicated faculty, state-of-the-art facilities, and a dynamic academic
environment, the institution continues to excel in both academic and
extracurricular domains, setting new benchmarks in medical education. The
vision and mission of the institution are to improve the standard of
medical education in the state, build competent and ethical doctors, provide
high-quality healthcare to the public at an affordable cost, and actively
promote medical research and innovation.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration

e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.

e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).


--- Page 235 ---
e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-I) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal

(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE

portal when the window opens.

All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).
2.Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College, Ernakulam" as one of your
preferred choices.

e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.

3.College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the GMC Ernakulam campus within the stipulated timeframe
for document verification and final admission.

Academic Infrastructure

Government Medical College, Ernakulam has a well-developed academic
infrastructure to support undergraduate and postgraduate medical
education in accordance with NMC and KUHS standards.The academic
infrastructure is designed to provide a comprehensive learning environment
across its 60-acre campus in Kalamassery.

e Lecture Halls: The college features five spacious, well-furnished
lecture halls. Each hall has a seating capacity of over 100 students
and is equipped with modern audio-visual technology, including LCD
projectors, computers, and integrated microphone systems.

e Examination & Seminar Halls: A dedicated examination hall is
available to accommodate 200 students simultaneously. Additionally,
every department is equipped with its own seminar hall for
specialized academic discussions.

e Departmental Facilities: Each department maintains independent
demonstration and research rooms, as well as dedicated libraries and
laboratories outfitted with the latest medical equipment.


--- Page 245 ---
e Auditorium: A centrally located, well-furnished auditorium provides a
seating capacity of 400 for major events and academic functions.

e Power Supply: The campus is served by a dedicated 110 KV
substation, supported by a 24-hour standby generator to ensure
uninterrupted electricity.

e Water Supply: Round-the-clock purified water is provided through
two deep-water wells that offer a perennial supply.

e Waste Management: The institution prioritizes eco-friendly practices,
utilizing environmental incineration and categorized waste disposal. A
specialized bio-gas plant is also part of the facility's waste-to-energy
initiative.

e Banking: The Ernakulam District Co-operative Bank and its ATM are
located directly on campus. Several other banks and ATMs are
available within short walking distance.

e Sports & Fitness: A well-equipped gymnasium is available to
students, alongside comprehensive facilities for both indoor and
outdoor games.

e Arts & Culture: The college provides dedicated resources and
platforms to help students develop individual talents in various artistic
and cultural activities.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Kayakalp Award 2024-25: The affiliated hospital systems in the
region, including the Ernakulam General Hospital (which works in
synergy with the medical college network), secured the ‘1st Place in
Kerala for excellence in cleanliness, infection control, and eco-friendly
practices.


--- Page 246 ---
e Superspeciality Block: Construction of the multi-crore
Superspeciality Block has reached over 60% completion. Once fully
operational, it will host advanced departments like Cardiology,
Neurology, and Nephrology, significantly enhancing clinical exposure
for MBBS students.

e Regional Hub for Medical Excellence: The college is now a key
part of the central Kerala healthcare grid, supporting the Cochin
Cancer Research Centre (CCRC) located within the same 60-acre
campus.

e Public Health Campaigns: The college’s Indian Medical Association
Medical Students Network (IMA MSN) unit is highly active in social
initiatives, including anti-narcotic campaigns and environmental
awareness drives.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A 700-bedded hospital, featuring 500 general
category beds specifically for clinical teaching, and additional beds for
emergency and private wards.

e ICU beds & Operation Theatres: 12 operation theatres with 8 major
and 4 minor OTs available in the hospital. 5 critical care units
including Neonatal, Cardiac, Pulmonary, Surgical and Pediatric ICU
are also available.(Numbers are from institutional overviews; confirm
latest figures directly with hospital admin if needed).

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD):The OPD at GMC Ernakulam serves as
the primary point of contact for thousands of patients daily from
Ernakulam and neighboring districts like Alappuzha, Idukki, and


--- Page 247 ---
Thrissur.The IPD facilities provide students with intensive bedside
learning opportunities through long-term patient management

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments: The core specialty
departments—including General Medicine, General Surgery,
Obstetrics & Gynaecology, Paediatrics, Orthopaedics, and
Psychiatry. The institution has recently reached a significant milestone
with the commissioning of a massive Super-specialty Block, which
integrates advanced departments such as Cardiology (with a
dedicated Cath Lab), Neurology, Nephrology (with 24/7 dialysis),
Urology, Paediatric Surgery, and Neurosurgery.

e Blood bank; Emergency & trauma care: Full diagnostic services,
blood bank, emergency/trauma services and critical care blocks are
present as part of the hospital infrastructure.

Campus Life

e The institution lays special emphasis on sports activities which are
monitored by an experienced and highly qualified Physical Director.

e The campus has facilities for all the outdoor games like cricket,
football, volley ball, lawn tennis, throw ball,shuttle badminton, table
tennis etc.

e A multigym facility is available for all the students in the campus.

e A vibrant campus culture anchored by the 'REVERA' sports fest and
the 'Opparam'’ arts festival, with separate on-campus hostels for men
and women.


--- Page 248 ---
Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Separate hostel facilities for boys and girls, with spacious rooms
three, double and single bedded.

e Basic furniture is provided in the rooms. They also have common
rooms for recreation facilities, reading rooms and TV rooms.

e Round the clock security is provided to all the hostels.

e Each hostel have a mess hall with seating capacity of more than 150
people and the mess is run by students themselves under a common
dividing system

e Students will be under the disciplinary control of the assistant
wardens and the wardens.

Safety & Support Systems

e GMC Ernakulam maintains a strict zero-tolerance policy through its
Anti-Ragging Committee (chaired by the Principal and including
police and parent reps) and a Grievance Redressal Cell that handles
academic and personal complaints.

e Fire safety measures, disaster management protocols, and infection
control practices are in place across clinical and non-clinical areas,
while administrative and welfare committees work to promote a safe,
inclusive, and professional campus environment.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Internship placement quality at Government Medical College,
Ernakulam is strong, driven by high patient volume and wide case
diversity. Interns receive extensive hands-on training across core and


--- Page 249 ---
super-specialty departments, with significant exposure to emergency
care, ward management, and common procedures under supervision.
e As a government institution, it provides a monthly stipend as per
current Kerala State Government norms.
e The rigorous clinical exposure at GMC Ernakulam prepares
graduates well for postgraduate entrance examinations (NEET-PG,
INI-CET), higher studies in India or abroad, and careers in
government service, private hospitals, academia, public health, and
research.

College rules & discipline

Anti-Ragging Committee : Government Medical College (GMC),
Ernakulam, maintains a strict Anti-Ragging Committee and a proactive
Anti-Ragging Squad to ensure a zero-tolerance environment against
ragging. The committee is chaired by the Principal and includes key faculty,
administration, and external representatives.

Grievance Redressal Committee (GRDC): Chaired by the Principal, this
committee includes senior faculty and student representatives. It addresses
issues ranging from unfair academic evaluations to administrative delays.
Hostel regulations : Students will be under the disciplinary control of the
assistant wardens and the wardens.The hostels (separate for men and
women) are governed by strict codes of conduct.

Government Medical College, Ernakulam - Student &
Parent Review

Student Review:

Student review of Government Medical College, Ernakulam is generally
positive, especially with respect to clinical exposure and academic rigor.
Students commonly highlight the high patient inflow and wide variety of
cases as major strengths, which provide excellent hands-on learning and
build strong clinical confidence. Faculty support and structured academic
activities are appreciated, though the workload and duty hours are often
described as demanding. Infrastructure and hostel facilities are considered
adequate but functional rather than luxurious. Overall, students view GMC
Ernakulam as a solid government medical college that offers strong clinical


--- Page 251 ---
training, good academic discipline, and reliable career preparation, making
it well suited for students who are committed, hardworking, and clinically
oriented.

Overall : Government Medical College, Ernakulam offers strong clinical
exposure, disciplined academics, and reliable career preparation, making it
a solid choice for serious medical students.

Parent Review:

Government Medical College, Ernakulam is a trustworthy institution that
provides quality medical education, strong clinical training, and a
disciplined academic environment. The government setting ensures
experienced faculty, excellent patient exposure, and affordable education,
which adds to long-term career stability. Although the workload is
demanding and facilities are functional rather than luxurious, the emphasis
on safety, supervision, and professional values gives parents confidence in
their child’s overall development and future prospects.
Overall : From a parent’s viewpoint, GMC Ernakulam offers dependable
medical education, strong clinical exposure, disciplined campus life, and
secure long-term career prospects at an affordable cost.

Way to reach

By Ajr:

Cochin International Airport (COK) is about 18-20 km away. From the
airport, taxis and app-based cabs are available; travel time is around 30-45
minutes.

By Train:

Aluva Railway Station (=5 km) and Ernakulam Junction / Ernakulam Town
(=10-12 km) are the nearest major stations. From these stations, buses,
autos, and taxis connect directly to Kalamassery.

By Metro:

Kalamassery Town Metro Station is the nearest stop. From there, the
college is about 1—1.5 km, reachable by auto-rickshaw or a short walk.
By Bus:

Frequent KSRTC and private buses run to Kalamassery / HMT Junction
from all parts of Kochi. The medical college is very close to HMT Junction.
By Road:

Located near NH 544 (Salem—Kochi Highway), the campus is easily
accessible by car or taxi from anywhere in Ernakulam city.

Landmark: Near HMT Junction, Kalamassery

@ Government Medical College, Idukki
Idukki Colony P.O, Cheruthoni, Kerala, 685602
LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Government Medical college Idukki was established in 2014 GO (Rt )
No,2363 | 201.4 / H &FWD dated.11.07:2014 as up gradation of
existing district hospital Idukki as a policy decision of the Government
of Kerala to provide tertiary care and research and teaching facilities
to all districts of Kerala especially to get benefits for tribal areas and
socially backward and distant remote hilly terrains of the state. As a
policy decision Government has arranged all amenities to start the
Government medical college Idukki and work entrusted to KITCO as
per norms and they have completed and made available the
academic block, new hospital complex and residential facilities,
Renovated the existing district hospital to maternal and child health
block. The Medical College campus extends over 90 acres in the
heart of district headquarters.
In 2014 and 2015 MBBS batch was admitted here and passed the
first year with a 100% pass rate. And during the 2017 period, the
admission was withheld due to a lack of infrastructure. By the past 3
year period, the Government has rectified all the infrastructure gaps


--- Page 260 ---
to sustain the college affiliation through timely and sincere effort.
Currently, we have applied & awaiting for the NMC approval for an
annual intake of 100 MBBS seats for the academic year 2022-23.
Vision
To provide quality health care service to the people of Kerala by
developing this Institute as a centre of excellence in every aspect of
Modern Medicine.
Mission
"QUALIW CARE AT LOW COST" To have a state of the art Medical
College fully equipped in all aspect. To produce excellent medical
professionals who can effectively serve the society. To make this a
pioneer Medical Institute at par with the best medical college of the
country.
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Government Medical College, Idukki (GMCI).

e Location: Cheruthoni (near Painavu), Idukki District, Kerala, PIN -
685602.

e Year of Establishment: 2014 (received NMC approval for 100 seats in
2022).

e Type of College: Government (Public).

e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur.

e Counselling Authority: Medical Counselling Committee (MCC) for All
India Quota and Commissioner for Entrance Examinations (CEE),
Kerala for State Quota.


--- Page 261 ---
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC).
e MBBS Intake: 100 seats annually.
e Course Duration: 5.5 years (4.5 years of academic study + 1 year
compulsory rotating internship).
e Hospital Type: Government Tertiary Care Hospital (upgraded from the
District Hospital, Idukki).
Official contact details(2025)

Cheruthoni, Idukki District, Kerala, PIN - 685602.

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: Approximately 300 to 500 beds. The initial block
was designed with a 300-bed capacity, while newer infrastructure
planning aims for expansion to 500.

e Total ICU Beds: The hospital includes dedicated Surgical ICU units,
as well as specialized NICU (Neonatal) and SNCU (Special Newborn
Care) units.

e Total Operation Theatres: Multiple OTs including Major and Minor
Operation Theatres supporting departments like General Surgery and
Obstetrics.

e Total Outpatients: The hospital serves as a primary hub for the
district; while exact daily counts fluctuate, the new OP section was
specifically designed to handle the high volume of rural and tribal
patients.

e Emergency Services: Available 24/7 with on-call consultants and
Casualty services.

e Hospital Accreditation: Affiliated with the Kerala University of Health
Sciences (KUHS) and approved by the National Medical Commission
(NMC). It follows State Government health standards for public
tertiary care.


--- Page 263 ---
e Clinical Exposure: Students receive extensive hands-on experience
through clinical rotations and Early Clinical Exposure (ECE) modules
starting from the first year, focusing on diverse cases unique to hilly
and rural populations.

Courses Offered
MBBS (Bachelor of Medicine and Bachelor of Surgery): The cornerstone
program with an annual intake of 100 seats. The course lasts 5.5 years,
including a mandatory one-year rotating internship.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
Step 1: Appear for NEET UG
The absolute prerequisite is qualifying for the NEET UG 2026
(National Eligibility cum Entrance Test).
e Application: Usually opens in February/March.
e Exam: Typically held on the first Sunday of May.
e Eligibility: Must have 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology (40% for SC/ST/OBC) in Class 12.
Step 2: Registration for Counseling
Depending on the quota you are aiming for, you must register on
different portals:
e For State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM)
website (cee.kerala.gov.in).

o Note: Even though MBBS does not require the KEAM
entrance exam, you must register as a medical aspirant
on the KEAM portal to be considered for Kerala state
counseling.

e For All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC (Medical
Counselling Committee) website (mcc.nic.in).
Step 3: Centralized Allotment Process (CAP)
Once the NEET results are out, the counseling authorities will release
a rank list.


--- Page 265 ---
1. Option Entry: You will log in to the portal and list "Government
Medical College, Idukki" as one of your preferred choices.
2. Seat Allotment: Seats are allotted based on your NEET rank,
category reservation, and the availability of seats at GMCI.
3. Allotment Memo: If selected, you will download an allotment
memo from the website.
Step 4: Physical Reporting & Document Verification
After receiving an allotment, you must physically report to the
Principal’s Office at GMC Idukki (Cheruthoni) to confirm your seat.
MBBS Seat Distribution (2025)
For the 2025-26 academic year, Government Medical College, Idukki
has an approved annual intake of 100 MBBS seats. The distribution
is split between the national and state-level quotas as per the
National Medical Commission (NMC) and the Commissioner for
Entrance Examinations (CEE), Kerala.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: Multiple spacious, tiered lecture theaters equipped with
smart boards, projectors, and sound systems to facilitate interactive
learning.

e Examination Hall: A large, centralized hall designed to accommodate
over 100 students for university and internal examinations.

e Auditorium: A facility used for academic seminars, guest lectures, and
cultural events.

e Pre-Clinical Labs: Advanced labs for Anatomy (Dissection Hall &
Histology), Physiology, and Biochemistry.

e Para-Clinical Labs: Well-equipped facilities for Pathology,
Microbiology, Pharmacology, and Forensic Medicine.

e Museums: Anatomy and Forensic Medicine departments maintain
curated museums with specimens and models for self-directed
learning.

e Collection: Houses over 7,000 medical textbooks and subscriptions to
various national and international medical journals.


--- Page 272 ---
e E-Library: A digital section providing access to online databases,
e-journals, and research materials through the KUHS consortium.

e Study Areas: Includes separate reading rooms for students and
faculty, as well as a "Common Room" for group discussions.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Top University Rankings: In 2022 and 2023, the college was ranked
1st and 2nd respectively in pass percentage among all medical
colleges under KUHS.

e Batch Performance: The initial batches (2014 & 2015) recorded a
100% pass rate in their first-year university examinations.

e Educational Research: Faculty members have published comparative
studies on Self-Directed Learning (SDL) vs. interactive lectures to
optimize the new Competency-Based Medical Education (CBME)
curriculum.

e Clinical Studies: Notable research has been conducted on the
prevalence. of menopausal symptoms in rural hilly tracts and the
diagnostic profiles of Gestational Diabetes Mellitus in the region.

e The annual inter-batch cultural competition involving dance, music,
and literary events.

e Annual athletic meet held at the campus grounds; students often
participate in inter-medical college football and cricket tournaments.

e Large-scale celebrations for Onam (including Pookalam competitions)
and Christmas.

e An annual foundation day celebration featuring guest speakers and
cultural nights.


--- Page 273 ---
Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: Currently features 300+ beds across various
specialties.

e Emergency & Trauma: A 24/7 Casualty and Emergency department
equipped with life-support systems and a dedicated triage area.

e Operating Theatres: Includes 5 advanced major Operation Theaters
(OTs) and several minor OTs for specialized surgeries.

e Intensive Care: Dedicated ICUs for critical care, including specialized
units for Pediatrics (PICU) and Neonates (NICU).

e Diagnostic Wing: Fully functional Radiology (X-ray, Ultrasound, CT
scan) and Pathology labs that handle a heavy daily diagnostic load.

e Obstetrics: Handles a high volume of deliveries and Cesarean
sections.

e Pediatrics: Offers comprehensive care from newborn screenings to
adolescent health, serving as the main referral center for Idukki's hilly
terrains.

e Tropical Diseases: High exposure to monsoon-related illnesses and
leptospirosis.

e Trauma: Frequent cases of road traffic accidents (RTA) and falls from
heights due to the hilly terrain.

e Animal Bites: High incidence of snake bites and wild animal-related
injuries requiring specialized toxicology knowledge.

Campus Life

e Cultural Events: Major festivals like Onam and Christmas are
celebrated with grand traditional feasts (Sadhya), Pookalam (floral
carpets), and performances.


--- Page 274 ---
e Arts Fest: An annual inter-batch competition where students
showcase talents in music, dance, and literature.

e Sports: Despite the hilly terrain, the college has an active sports club.
Students participate in inter-medical tournaments across Kerala,
particularly in football and cricket.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Accommodation: Separate hostel buildings for boys and girls are
available. Rooms are typically double or triple occupancy for the first
few years, with single rooms sometimes available for final year or
intern students.

e Amenities: Rooms are well-ventilated and furnished, with each
student provided a bed, study table, chair, and steel cupboard.

e Hygiene: The dining areas are spacious, well-maintained, and follow
strict cleanliness standards, offering both vegetarian and
non-vegetarian options.

e On-Campus Canteen: A general college canteen is also available,
providing snacks and refreshments at reasonable rates for students
and staff.

Safety & Support Systems
The institution maintains several official channels and committees to
address student concerns and provide support:

e Anti-Ragging Committee: The college strictly adheres to anti-ragging
regulations. Students and parents are required to file an online
anti-ragging affidavit during admission.


--- Page 275 ---
o National Anti-Ragging Helpline: A 24x7 toll-free number is
available to report incidents at 1800-180-5522.

o Email for Complaints: Complaints can also be emailed to
helpline@antiragging.in.

e Mentorship Programs: Each student is often assigned to a staff
advisor who guides them on curricular and extracurricular activities.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Hands-on Experience: Because it is the main government hospital for
the Idukki district, interns get significant "hands-on" practice with
procedures, emergency cases, and a high volume of patients.

e Diverse Cases: You will treat a wide variety of conditions, including
unique cases related to the hilly terrain and tribal populations, which
prepares you well for real-world medical practice.

e Stipend: Interns receive a monthly government stipend of
approximately 25,000—%26,000.

e Mandatory Service: You are bonded to serve one year of rural service
in Kerala after your internship.

e Employability: Graduates from GMC Idukki are highly preferred for
government medical officer roles via the Kerala PSC due to their
experience in challenging terrains.

Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
Figures

e MBBS interns undergo a mandatory 12-month Compulsory Rotatory

Residential Internship (CRRI).


--- Page 276 ---
e Monthly Stipend: $25,000 to 27,000.

e Context: While central government institutes (like AIIMS) pay
approximately ~30,070, Kerala state government colleges typically
range between %25,000 and &27,000 depending on the most recent
state enhancement orders.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Anti-Ragging Committee: Led by the Principal and including the
Hospital Superintendent, HODs, local police (Idukki SHO), and media
representatives.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically for addressing
sexual harassment or gender-based discrimination.

e Student Grievance Cell: For academic or administrative complaints.

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Government Medical College, Kannur, popularly known as Pariyaram
Medical College, was established in March 1993 as the first medical
college in the cooperative sector in India under the Academy of Medical
Sciences (ACME). The associated hospital, a massive 1,000+ bed
super-specialty facility, commenced its operations in March 1994. The
institution is officially recognized by the National Medical Commission
(NMC) and is affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences
(KUHS). Its history is marked by a significant transition; originally founded
through a cooperative society, the Government of Kerala officially took over
the college and its assets on April 17, 2019, to ensure more affordable
medical education and healthcare.
The college offers 150 MBBS seats annually, which were increased to meet
the growing demand for medical professionals. Its Postgraduate
Programmes (MD/MS) cover a wide spectrum of disciplines, including


--- Page 284 ---
General Medicine, Pediatrics, General Surgery, Orthopaedics,
Anaesthesiology, and Radiology. For advanced medical training, the
institution provides Super-Specialty courses such as DM Cardiology.
Located on a sprawling 119-acre campus, the college continues to serve as
a vital referral center for North Kerala.
Mission
To improve the overall health status of people of Kerala by providing
comprehensive quality health care of high standards
Vision
A Centre of Excellence for Medical Education & an Institution for
Comprehensive Health Care.
Basic College Profile
e Name of Institution: Government Medical College, Kannur
e Location: Pariyaram, Kannur, Kerala, India - 670503
e Year of Establishment: 1993 (established as ACME); 2019 (officially
taken over by the Government of Kerala)
e Type of College: Government
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala (for 85% State Quota) and Medical Counselling
Committee (MCC) (for 15% All India Quota)
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC)
e MBBS Intake: 150 seats

e Course Duration: 5.5 years (4.5 years of academic study + 1-year
mandatory rotating internship)
e Hospital Type: Tertiary Care / Super-specialty Teaching Hospital
(1,200 beds)

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: 1,200 beds, supported by more than 20
specialty and 8 super-specialty departments.

e Total ICU Beds: 180 beds institution-wide. This includes dedicated
units such as a 20-bedded Medical ICU, a 14-bedded Surgical ICU,
a 14-bedded Neuro ICU, and a 16-bedded Neonatal ICU.

e Total Operation Theatres: 18 fully equipped Operation Theatres
designed for advanced and complicated surgical procedures across
all specialties.

e Total Outpatients: Serves as a major referral center for North Kerala,
handling a high volume of patients from Kannur, Kasargod, Wayanad,
and Kozhikode.

e Emergency Services: Features a 56-bedded Emergency
Department operational 24/7, with specialized triage, 16
resuscitation beds, and a dedicated Toxicology ICU for snake bites
and poisoning.

e Hospital Accreditation: The institution and its facilities hold
certifications from NABL, NABH, ISO 9001:2008, and OHSAS
18001:2007.

e Clinical Exposure: As the ultimate destination for healthcare in the
Malabar region, students receive extensive hands-on clinical training
across diverse cases in specialty and super-specialty units.

e For 15% All India Quota: You must register at the MCC
website.

preferred choice in the list.

Memo.

e You must then physically report to. the college campus in

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Skill Workshops: Conducted hands-on First Aid & CPR training
for students and faculty.

e National Gold Medal:Dr. Sithara Nasar, a college alumna,
received the DNB Gold Medal from the President of India for
topping the National Board examinations.

e UNARV Project: A major research initiative evaluating the
nutritional and health status of children (3-5 years) in
Anganwadis across the district

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Strength: A 1,000 to 1,200-bed multi-specialty complex that
serves as the primary health destination for Kannur, Kasaragod, and
parts of Wayanad and Kozhikode.

e Surgical Infrastructure: Equipped with 18 modern operation
theatres capable of performing complex procedures, including cardiac
and neurosurgeries.

e Specialized Units: Includes a dedicated Cardiovascular Unit
(Sahakarana Hrudayalaya), one of the most prominent in North
Malabar.

e Advanced ICUs: Features separate, well-equipped intensive care
units for Medical (20 beds), Surgical (14 beds), Neuro Surgery (14
beds), Pediatrics (6 beds), and Neonatal (16 beds) care.


--- Page 305 ---
e High Patient Load: Undergraduates (MBBS) and postgraduates gain
direct exposure to a diverse range of clinical cases, with daily
outpatient (OP) attendance often exceeding 1,500 patients.

e Integrated Learning: The hospital block itself includes a lecture
theatre where clinical subjects are taught during postings, bridging
the gap between theory and bedside practice.

e Super-Specialty Training: Students interact with over 20 specialty
and 8 super-specialty departments, including Nephrology, Urology,
Neurology, and Gastroenterology.

e 24/7 Support: The Trauma & Critical Care Unit and Blood Bank offer
24-hour support with specialized teams and advanced life-support
ambulances.

e Dialysis Services: Operates a unit with 23 modern dialysis
machines, providing critical care to patients from across North Kerala.

Campus Life

e Sports Complex: The campus features a large sports complex
dedicated to various outdoor and indoor games.

e Fitness: A gymnasium/fitness center is usually accessible to students.

e Arts Festival: The annual arts festival ("Arts Fest") is a major cultural
highlight, featuring inter-batch competitions in dance, music, drama,
literary events, and fine arts.

e Student Associations: Active student unions and associations
organize various social events, academic seminars (CMEs), and
workshops throughout the year.

e Medical Camps: Students actively participate in community outreach
programs and medical camps organized by the college, fostering
social responsibility and practical experience.


--- Page 306 ---
Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Hostels: Separate, modern, and secure hostels are available for male
and female students. They typically offer single, double, or triple
occupancy rooms with mess facilities (vegetarian/non-vegetarian
options) and common areas for recreation.

e Essential Services: The campus functions as a mini-township,
featuring essential amenities such as a bank with ATM services, a
post office, co-operative stores, and canteens.

Safety & Support Systems

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A high-level committee including the
Principal, senior faculty, and local police representatives monitors the
campus 24/7.

e Gender Safety: In compliance with the POSH Act, the ICC handles
complaints related to sexual harassment and ensures a safe working
and learning environment for female students and staff.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e High Patient Volume: With 1,200 beds and over 1,500 daily
outpatients, interns get massive hands-on experience with diverse
medical cases.

e Skill Development: Interns perform essential procedures like suturing,
intubation, and assisting in surgeries under expert supervision.

e Rotational Training: You rotate through all major departments
(Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, etc.) and super-specialties like
Cardiology.

e Monthly Stipend: Interns receive a government-mandated stipend of
approximately 20,000 — =27,000.


--- Page 307 ---
e Rural Exposure: Mandatory postings in rural health centers help you
learn to manage cases with limited resources.
e Career Readiness: The heavy workload and clinical variety make
graduates highly confident for future practice and NEET-PG exams.
Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)
e Anti-Ragging Committee: A high-level body led by the Principal,
including faculty and local police, oversees campus safety.
e Institutional Committee: A dedicated cell manages complaints
regarding academic, administrative, or personal issues.


--- Page 308 ---
e Curfew Timings: Entry and exit for hostels are strictly regulated.
Generally, students must be inside the hostel by 9:00 PM unless they
have prior permission for night shifts or library study.
e Alcohol & Tobacco: The entire campus is a Tobacco-Free and
Alcohol-Free Zone. Possession or consumption of these substances
leads to immediate expulsion from the hostel.

Mt MEDIC, Government Medical College (GMC),

ote KA. Kasaragod

© m

eo i of - Ukkinadka, Kasaragod, Kerala, 671123.
LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Established with the laying of its foundation stone on November 30, 2013,
Government Medical College, Kasaragod (GMC Kasaragod) was
envisioned to address the long-standing healthcare needs of northern
Kerala. The institution's development saw a significant pivot in April 2020,
when its partially completed academic block was rapidly converted into a
200-bed specialty hospital to manage the regional COVID-19 crisis. After
over a decade of infrastructure challenges, the college reached a historic
milestone on October 3, 2025, when it officially launched its first academic
session following approval from the National Medical Commission (NMC).
Currently, the college exclusively offers the MBBS (Bachelor of Medicine
and Bachelor of Surgery) undergraduate program, with an initial intake of
50 students for the 2025-2026 academic year. Affiliated with the Kerala
University of Health Sciences (KUHS), the institution provides medical
education through its modern academic block while utilizing the Kasaragod
General Hospital as a temporary teaching facility. Although postgraduate
and paramedical courses are not yet available, the campus is undergoing
expansion to include a dedicated 500-bed multi-specialty hospital and


--- Page 317 ---
specialized units like the Endosulfan Specialty Rehabilitation Centre,
aiming to become a comprehensive medical hub for the district.
The vision of Government Medical College, Kasaragod is to provide
high-quality medical education and modern healthcare facilities to the
people of northern Kerala. Its mission is to train compassionate, skilled
doctors while offering affordable and expert medical services to the local
community through the Directorate of Medical Education.
Basic College Profile
e Name of Institution: Government Medical College, Kasaragod (GMC
Kasaragod)
e Location: Ukkinadka, Kasaragod District, Kerala - 671552
e Year of Establishment: 2013 (Foundation stone); 2025 (Official
academic launch)
e Type of College: Government / Public
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner of Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC)
e MBBS Intake: 50 students (for the inaugural academic batch)
e Course Duration: 5.5 Years (4.5 years of academics + 1 year of
compulsory internship)
e Hospital Type: Multi-Specialty Teaching Hospital


--- Page 318 ---

Teaching Hospital

e Hospital Name: Government Medical College Hospital, Kasaragod
(formerly General Hospital Kasaragod).

e Phone: 04994-222999 or 04994-230080.

e Emergency Contact: 112 (National Emergency Helpline) or
04994-222999 (Direct Hospital Line).

e Hospital Website: kasargodgeneralhospital.in

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: Approximately 349 beds at the General Hospital
(temporary teaching hospital). A dedicated 500-bed multi-specialty
block is currently under final-stage construction at the main
Ukkinadka campus.


--- Page 319 ---
e Total ICU Beds: 14 beds currently available at the General Hospital
(including 6 Adult ICU and 8 Newborn ICU beds). The new campus
block has a planned capacity for more than 20 ICU beds.

e Total Operation Theatres: 10 operation theatres are functional at the
designated teaching hospital.

e Total Outpatients: Averaging over 800—1,000 patients daily, providing
a high volume for student learning.

e Emergency Services: 24-hour Casualty and Trauma Care services
are available, supported by 24/7 laboratory, pharmacy, and
ambulance facilities.

e Hospital Accreditation: Affiliated with the Kerala University of Health
Sciences (KUHS) and fully approved by the National Medical
Commission (NMC) for medical training.

e Clinical Exposure: Students gain hands-on experience in major
departments including General Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics,
OBGYN, Orthopedics, and Psychiatry, as well as specialized units
like the Dialysis and Dental Units.

MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Total Duration: 5.5 years, comprising 4.5 years of academic
study and a mandatory 1-year Compulsory Rotating Medical
Internship (CRMI).

e Intake Capacity: The college is sanctioned for 50 MBBS seats
annually.


--- Page 320 ---
e Affiliation & Approval: Affiliated with the Kerala University of
Health Sciences (KUHS) and approved by the National Medical
Commission (NMC).

Internal Assessment (Formative)

e Eligibility to Sit for Exams: Students must secure a minimum of 50%
marks combined in theory and practical/clinical internal assessments,
with at least 40% separately in each.

e Frequency: Typically, there are three periodic internal assessments
per subject in each academic phase.

Courses Offered.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1.Mandatory Entrance Exam

e NEET-UG 2026: All candidates must appear for and qualify in the
National Eligibility cum Entrance Test (Undergraduate).

2. Admission Steps

1. Application: Apply online for NEET-UG via NTA and KEAM 2026 via
CEE Kerala.

2. Counseling Rounds: Participate in choice filling where you select
"Government Medical College, Kasaragod" as a preference.

3. Seat Allotment: Allotments are issued based on NEET rank, category,
and seat availability.

4. Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, report to the college campus in
Ukkinadka for document verification and fee payment to confirm
admission.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: The administrative and academic block houses modern
classrooms and lecture theatres equipped with audio-visual aids and
digital teaching tools.

e Specialized Laboratories: The college features dedicated laboratories
for pre-clinical and para-clinical subjects, including an Anatomy
Dissection Hall, Physiology Lab, and Biochemistry Lab

e Medical Library: The campus includes a central medical library with a
growing collection of over 10,000 textbooks, reference volumes, and
national/international journals.

e Digital Resources: Students have access to an E-library with internet
connectivity to support research and digital learning.

e Teaching Hospital: Practical clinical training is conducted at the
on-campus specialty block and the associated hospital, which is
designed as a 500-bed multi-specialty facility.

e Departmental Clinical Units: Clinical teaching is supported by
functional departments in General Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, and
more.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Inaugural Batch Induction (2025): The most significant recent event
was the official commencement of the first MBBS batch with 50
students, following final clearance from the National Medical
Commission (NMC).

e NMC Accreditation: Securing NMC approval in 2025 was the
college's primary institutional achievement, ending a decade-long
wait for the region to have a functional government medical college.


--- Page 327 ---
e Emerging Research Cell: The college is currently establishing its
Institutional Ethics Committee (IEC) and Research Cell to facilitate
future faculty and student research projects.

e Regional Health Studies: Initial academic focus is directed toward
public health studies relevant to the Kasaragod region, including
long-term health monitoring related to Endosulfan exposure.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The final plan is for a 500-bed multi-specialty hospital.
The college commenced clinical operations in late 2025 with the
minimum required operational beds (approximately 200-220) to meet
National Medical Commission (NMC) norms.

e Operation Theaters: The completed hospital complex is designed to
house a number of operating theatres, with reports indicating several
are currently functional to support specialty surgeries.

e Facilities: The hospital offers a 24-hour casualty service, pharmacy,
X-ray, lab, blood bank, CT scan, and a dialysis unit

e Outpatient Department (OP): Operates daily, providing the first point
of patient contact for students. The current OP volume helps fulfill the
required patient interaction metrics for accreditation.

e Learning Environment: Students begin patient encounters from the
early years of the course, integrating theory with real-time practical
learning in a functional hospital environment right on the campus.


--- Page 328 ---
Campus Life

e Physical Activity: The college grounds offer space for outdoor sports
like cricket and football, while indoor games facilities provide options
for leisure activities such as carrom and chess.

e Well-being: A dedicated student health center is available on campus
to manage immediate medical needs and emergencies.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Capacity and Structure: The campus features separate buildings for
men and women, designed as a secure gated complex.

e Room Types: Junior students (MBBS Phase 1) typically reside in
twin-sharing rooms.

e Furnishing: Each student is provided with essential furniture,
including a bed/cot, study table, chair, and cupboard.

e Amenities: The hostels offer 24/7 water and electricity supply with
backup power systems dedicated to study areas. High-speed Wi-Fi is
available in common areas and study rooms.

Safety & Support Systems

e 24/7 Security: The campus and hostels are monitored by experienced
security personnel around the clock.

e CCTV Surveillance: Advanced CCTV cameras are installed across
the campus, including common areas and entrances, for continuous
surveillance and heightened safety.


--- Page 329 ---
Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Clinical Environment: Since the college only admitted its first MBBS
batch in late 2025, the first full-scale "placement" of its own students
into the Compulsory Rotating Medical Internship (CRMI) will not occur
until 2030.

e Training Quality: Interns will benefit from hands-on training at the
on-campus 500-bed teaching hospital, which features modern
specialty blocks. The high patient diversity common in the
Kasaragod-Mangaluru corridor ensures exposure to a wide variety of
Clinical cases.

Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures
Medical graduates undergoing their Compulsory Rotating Medical
Internship (CRMI) receive a monthly stipend.

e Current Monthly Amount: %26,000 to ¥27,000.

e Note for GMC Kasaragod: Since the first MBBS batch at this
institution began in late 2025, they will only be eligible for this
stipend upon reaching their internship year in 2030. Currently,
these figures apply to any Foreign Medical Graduates (FMGs)
or transfer students completing rotations at the hospital.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Zero Tolerance: The institution enforces a zero-tolerance policy
toward ragging in any form (physical, verbal, or psychological) in
accordance with the Kerala Prohibition of Ragging Act, 1998.


--- Page 330 ---
e Institutional Committees: A dedicated Anti-Ragging Committee and a
surprise-monitoring Anti-Ragging Squad are active on campus.

e Reporting: Incidents can be reported directly to the Principal
(Chairman of the committee) or through the National Anti-Ragging
Helpline at 1800-180-5522.

e Attendance & Curfew: Students must adhere to a mandatory curfew,
typically requiring them to be inside the hostel by 9:00 PM or 10:00
PM.

e Prohibited Items: Possession or consumption of alcohol, tobacco, and
drugs is strictly forbidden and results in immediate expulsion and
police reporting.

e Visitors: Day scholars and guests are generally restricted from
entering hostel rooms; they are only permitted in designated visiting
areas during specific hours (e.g., 5:00 PM — 7:00 PM).

Government Medical College(GMC),Student & Parent Review

Student Review
Students appreciate the "prominent and extraordinary" professors,
many of whom hold doctorates and bring years of experience to the
classroom.Faculty members are described as friendly and helpful,
fostering a productive teaching environment that makes difficult
concepts easier to grasp.The teaching quality is rated highly, with a
curriculum aligned with modern standards (CBME) and a strong
emphasis on practical training and regular class tests.


--- Page 331 ---
Overall:Students consistently praise the faculty, noting that many
professors are experienced specialists transferred from established
colleges. The teaching is described as structured and supportive,
strictly following the NMC’s Competency-Based Medical Education
(CBME).

Parent Review
The most common sentiment among parents is affordability. Securing
an MBBS seat at a government fee (approx. %23,150/year) is highly
valued, as it provides a top-tier medical education without the
immense financial burden of private or deemed universities. They also
appreciate the presence of specialty departments (like Neurology and
Cardiology) which serves as a double benefit: quality training for their
children and better healthcare for the family.
Overall:The gated campus and 24/7 security at hostels provide a
high sense of safety. Parents frequently comment that the quiet
environment, away from city distractions, is ideal for the rigorous
study required for medicine.

GetMyAdmission — Professional Review of Government
Medical College, Kasaragod
At GetMyAdmission (GMA), we evaluate medical institutions based on
academic quality, clinical exposure, infrastructure, affordability, and overall
student development. Government Medical College, Kasaragod is one of
Kerala’s newer government medical colleges and is currently in its
developmental phase, steadily strengthening its academic and hospital
systems for MBBS education.
Student Perspective
Students commonly highlight:
e Astructured academic system following KUHS curriculum properly.
e Supportive faculty members who focus on building strong basic
medical concepts.
e A calm and less crowded learning environment compared to older
government colleges.
e Safe and manageable hostel facilities.
Students also note that:
e Clinical exposure is still moderate and not yet comparable to
long-established government colleges.
e Certain specialty departments and advanced facilities are still
expanding.


--- Page 333 ---
Parent Perspective
Parents appreciate:

e The strong credibility and security of a government medical college.

e Very affordable fee structure compared to private institutions.

e Safe campus atmosphere with disciplined academic supervision.

e Steady institutional growth and long-term development potential.
Overall Assessment
Government Medical College, Kasaragod provides a stable academic
foundation in an affordable government setup. While it does not yet match
the clinical intensity of senior government medical colleges in Kerala, it
offers a disciplined environment and gradual improvement in facilities.
It is suitable for students who prioritize affordability and are comfortable
studying in a developing institution with long-term growth prospects.

Way to reach
The college is connected to Kasaragod and surrounding regions via
NH-66 and local roads.

e Public Transport: Local buses connect Kasaragod town and the
Badiyadka panchayat area to the Ukkinadka campus.

e Kasaragod Railway Station (KGQ): This is the nearest major
station, located about 27 km from the college. It is
well-connected to major cities in Kerala and Karnataka.

e Kumbla Railway Station (KMQ): A closer local option, situated
approximately 14.36 km from the college.

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Government Medical College, Kollam, was established in 2013 by the
Government of Kerala with an objective to meet the ever- growing need of
medical professionals who are equipped with the best of knowledge and
techniques. Initially it was named ESIC medical College and was
constructed by the ESI Corporation of India.It is the earnest endeavor of
the Government to galvanize the entire Health Service sector of this region
through this pioneer Institution. This Medical College is having state of the
art infrastructure facilities and it is being equipped with the latest medical
equipment.
The vision of the institute is to provide the best healthcare facilities to the
people of Kerala by developing the institute as a center of excellence in
every aspect of modern medicine. The mission is to produce excellent
medical professionals with a strong academic foundation and technical
competence who can effectively serve the community.


--- Page 337 ---

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration

e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.

e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).

e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-I) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal
(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE
portal when the window opens.
All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).

2. Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College,Kollam" as one of your preferred
choices.


--- Page 341 ---
e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.

3 .College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the Government Medical College,Kollam campus within the
stipulated timeframe for document verification and final admission.

MBBS Seat Distribution (2025)
The distribution of MBBS seats at Government Medical College, Kollam is
carried out as per Government of India, Government of Kerala, and
National Medical Commission (NMC) norms.

Infrastructure & Facilities

e Lecture theatres : State of the art Lecture theatres with advanced
audiovisual aids

e Demonstration Rooms: Well-designed demonstration rooms for
small group teaching, case discussions, clinical demonstrations, and
skill-based learning, ensuring better student—faculty interaction.

e Laboratories:Fully equipped departmental laboratories for Anatomy,
Physiology, Biochemistry, Pathology, Microbiology, Pharmacology,
and Community Medicine with modern instruments and
safety-compliant infrastructure to support practical training and
research.

e Central Library : A spacious, well-stocked central library with a large
collection of medical textbooks, reference books, national and
international journals, digital resources, e-books, reading halls, and
extended study hours.


--- Page 351 ---
e Computer aided labs : Dedicated computer labs with high-speed
internet, digital learning software, simulation tools, and access to
online medical databases and academic platforms.

e Auditorium : A large, modern auditorium with professional acoustics,
lighting systems, projection facilities, and seating arrangements,
suitable for conferences, seminars, cultural programs, and academic
events.

e Common Rooms : Separate common rooms for boys and girls
equipped with seating, recreational facilities, rest areas, and basic
amenities to support student relaxation and social interaction.

e Outdoor and indoor recreation facilities : Well-developed sports
infrastructure including playgrounds for outdoor games (football,
cricket, volleyball, badminton) and indoor recreation facilities such as
table tennis, chess, carrom, and fitness centers.

e Medical facilities for students and staff : On-campus medical
services including OPD access, emergency care, routine health
checkups, and referral services through the attached teaching
hospital for students and staff.

Also the medical college has its own

e Kitchen Services : Centralized kitchen facilities ensuring hygienic
food preparation for hospital, hostels, and staff.

e Sewage Treatment Plant : In-house sewage treatment system
ensuring proper waste management and environmental sustainability.

e Civil & Electrical Maintenance: Dedicated maintenance wing
responsible for infrastructure upkeep, power supply, plumbing, HVAC
systems, and emergency repairs.


--- Page 352 ---
e Security Services : 24x7 professional security with CCTV

surveillance, access control systems, and campus safety monitoring.
Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e State Ranking: As of 2025, the institution is ranked approximately
6th among medical colleges in Kerala and has seen a consistent rise
in its national competitive standing.

e Faculty Publications: Ongoing research outputs are documented
annually, with significant contributions in fields such as dermatology,
pathology, and microbiology

e CME and Workshops: The college regularly hosts Continuing
Medical Education (CME) programs, including workshops on
Antimicrobial Resistance Surveillance (KARS-NET) and Clinical
Instructional Skills Programs (CISP) for faculty.

e Community Outreach: Ongoing annual events include World No
Tobacco Day awareness campaigns and monthly perinatal meetings
in conjunction with the Obstetrics & Gynecology department.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Total Bed Capacity: The hospital is a 500+ bedded facility designed
for both patient care and medical training.

e Surgical Facilities: Features 10 state-of-the-art modular operation
theatres equipped for complex procedures.

e Critical Care: Specialized units include an ICU, CCU, and Neonatal
ICU (NICU) to handle emergency and high-risk cases.


--- Page 353 ---
e Specialized Units: The hospital includes a modern mortuary
complex (capable of two simultaneous autopsies), a Central Sterile
Supply Department (CSSD), and a Theatre Sterile Surgical Unit
(TSSU).

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD): The hospital records a daily OP
attendance of more than 500 patients per day.Also the hospital is a
500-bed facility, with 470 beds dedicated to general wards and
specialized units, and 20—30 beds for emergency observation.

e Super-Specialty Interaction: Unlike many newer medical colleges,
GMC Kollam has active super-specialty units (like Cardiology with its
own Cath Lab items), allowing students to observe advanced cardiac
and neurological procedures.

Campus Life

e Cultural Activities — Annual college arts festivals, cultural programs,
and celebrations of national and regional events encourage creativity
and student bonding.

e Sports & Fitness — Facilities for indoor and outdoor games, sports
competitions, and fitness activities support physical well-being and
teamwork.

e Student Organizations — Active student unions, academic clubs,
and medical associations provide leadership opportunities and
student representation.

e Community Engagement — Students participate in health camps,
awareness programs, and _ outreach activities, strengthening
real-world clinical and social exposure.


--- Page 354 ---
Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Residential facilities for undergraduate students including
hostels, Cafeteria and mess: Well-maintained residential facilities
including separate hostels for undergraduate students, hygienic mess
services, and cafeterias providing nutritious meals, safe drinking
water, and comfortable living environments.

e Mess facility : The mess facilities serve hygienic, nutritious, and
balanced meals, catering to diverse dietary needs. Clean dining
areas, safe drinking water, and regular quality monitoring ensure
student health and satisfaction.

Safety & Support Systems

e Campus Security: The campus and hostels are secured round the
clock by security personnel and monitored by CCTV surveillance,
including in the examination halls.

e Anti-Ragging Measures: The college maintains a zero-tolerance
policy towards ragging and is strictly guided by UGC Regulations
2009 and the Kerala Prohibition of Ragging Act, 1998.

o An Anti-Ragging Committee and squad are actively formed to
prevent such incidents, conduct awareness programs, and
investigate any complaints.

o Punishments for ragging can be severe, including suspension,
expulsion, cancellation of admission, heavy fines (up to %2.5
lakhs), and even imprisonment.


--- Page 355 ---
e Women’s Safety & Gender Justice :GMC Kollam has a robust
mechanism to handle gender-related grievances and ensure the
safety of female students and staff.

e Gender Harassment Committee (Internal Complaints
Committee): This body is specifically tasked with addressing
complaints of sexual harassment. It includes senior female professors
and an external legal advocate to ensure impartial proceedings.

e Student Support & Mental Health:Recognizing the high-pressure
nature of medical education, the college provides integrated
psychological support.

e Mentorship Program: Each student is assigned a faculty mentor
who provides academic and personal guidance throughout the MBBS
course.

e Counseling Services: The Department of Psychiatry offers
confidential counseling for students dealing with stress, burnout, or
personal challenges.

e Student Grievance Cell: A formal platform where students can raise
concerns regarding academic facilities, hostel amenities, or
administrative issues without fear of reprisal.
