College rules & discipline- (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)
Anti-Ragging Policy
The college maintains a zero-tolerance policy towards ragging in any form.
An active Anti-Ragging Committee and Squad function round-the-clock to
prevent and address_ incidents. Awareness programs, — student
undertakings, surprise inspections, and confidential reporting mechanisms
are in place. Any violation is dealt with strictly as per UGC, NMC, and
Kerala Government regulations, including suspension, expulsion, or legal
action.
Grievance Redressal System
A structured Student Grievance Redressal Cell ensures that academic,
administrative, hostel-related, or personal grievances are addressed fairly
and promptly. Students can submit complaints through designated
channels, and all issues are resolved in a transparent, time-bound manner,
ensuring justice and student welfare.


--- Page 357 ---
Hostel Rules & Discipline

Hostel residents are expected to follow established rules related to
attendance, entry/exit timings, cleanliness, noise control, and respectful
behavior. Ragging, substance abuse, vandalism, or misconduct in hostels
is strictly prohibited. Hostel wardens and supervisory staff ensure safety,
discipline, and a conducive living environment. Regular inspections and
grievance mechanisms are in place for hostel-related concerns.
Government Medical College,Kollam - Student & Parent
Review

Student Review:

Students at Government Medical College, Kollam generally appreciate the
college for its strong academic environment, good clinical exposure, and
supportive faculty. The attached teaching hospital provides a high patient
load, enabling students to gain hands-on experience early in their training.
Faculty members are considered knowledgeable, approachable, and
committed to student learning, especially in clinical departments.

The campus infrastructure is steadily improving, with modern lecture
theatres, laboratories, library facilities, and hostels. Students value the
balanced campus life, availability of extracurricular activities, and strong
peer support system. While administrative processes and infrastructure
development are still evolving, overall student satisfaction remains high due
to the college’s academic standards, clinical training quality, and safe,
disciplined campus atmosphere.

Overall: Government Medical College, Kollam offers strong academics
with excellent clinical exposure supported by a high patient load and


--- Page 358 ---
dedicated faculty. Overall, it provides a safe, disciplined, and academically
enriching environment for medical students.
Parent review
Parents generally view Government Medical College, Kollam as a
dependable and well-established institution that provides quality medical
education and strong clinical training. They appreciate the high patient
exposure at the attached teaching hospital, which helps students gain
practical skills and confidence from an early stage. The faculty are seen as
experienced, supportive, and committed to academic excellence, ensuring
proper guidance and mentorship throughout the course.
Parents are also satisfied with the disciplined campus environment, strict
anti-ragging measures, and effective grievance redressal systems, which
contribute to student safety and well-being. Hostel and mess facilities are
considered adequate and hygienic, providing a comfortable living
environment for students away from home.
Overall: Parents consider Government Medical College, Kollam a safe and
reliable institution offering quality education with strong clinical training.
They appreciate the disciplined environment, supportive faculty, and steady
academic progress of students.

GMA Verdict:

Government Medical College, Kollam is a reliable and steadily improving
government medical institution, offering strong clinical exposure, affordable
education, and a supportive academic environment. It is a recommended
choice for MBBS and PG aspirants seeking government medical education
in Kerala.

Way to reach

1. By Road (Bus)

This is the most common way to reach the college as it lies on the major
transit artery of Kerala.

e KSRTC & Private Buses: Almost all buses traveling between Kollam
and Thiruvananthapuram (including Fast Passenger, Super Fast, and
Minnal services) stop at Parippally Junction.

e From Parippally Junction: The college is just 1-2 km from the
junction. You can take a local auto-rickshaw (a 5-minute ride) or a
local bus heading towards Paravur.

e Distances:

o From Kollam City: ~24 km (approx. 45-60 mins).

o From Thiruvananthapuram City: ~45 km (approx. 1.5 hours).
2. By Train
There is no railway station directly at the medical college, but several are
nearby:

e Paravur Railway Station (9.7 km): This is the nearest station. Many
passengers and some express trains stop here. From Paravur, you
can take an auto-rickshaw or a local bus to Parippally.


--- Page 362 ---
e Varkala Sivagiri Railway Station (11 km): A major stop for most
express trains. It is a convenient option if you are coming from the
south (Trivandrum) or north.

e Kollam Junction (QLN) (24 km): The nearest major rail head where all
long-distance and super-fast trains stop. From here, you can take a
KSRTC bus from the stand opposite the station or a taxi/auto directly
to Parippally.

3. By Air
Thiruvananthapuram International Airport (TRV): Located about 45
km away.

e Upon landing, you can take a pre-paid taxi directly to the college
(approx. 1 hour 15 mins via NH 66).

e Alternatively, take a bus from the airport or Thiruvananthapuram
Central Bus Station (Thampanoor) heading towards
Kollam/Ernakulam.

() GOVERNMENT MEDICAL COLLEGE, KOTTAYAM
Gandhinager,Kottayam,Kerala ,PIN-686008

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Government Medical College Kottayam is the third Medical College in
Kerala, was established in 1962. It was formally inaugurated on 03.12.1962
by Sri.R Sankar,the then Chief Minister of Kerala in the presence of Sri.M P
Govindan Nair, the Health Minister.First batch (1961 batch) of 50 MBBS
students were selected and accommodated at Medical College,
Thiruvananthapuram from 01.08.1961.It has a campus which spreads
across 265 acres .This college, in its sixty years of development, has
become one of the top-graded academic institutions and along with that,
won the trust and hope of the common man in Central Kerala as a center of
excellence for advanced treatments . On the academic front, it is
recognized as the Regional Medical Education Center of the National
Medical Commission. The Vision is to be a world-class institution that
excels in medical education, research, and healthcare delivery. We aspire
to foster a culture of excellence, innovation, and compassion to shape the
future of healthcare in our region and beyond.The mission of College is to
provide exemplary medical education, conduct innovative research, and
deliver exceptional healthcare services to the community and beyond. The
institution is committed to offering comprehensive and high-quality medical
education that equips students with the knowledge, skills, and professional


--- Page 367 ---
attitudes necessary for clinical practice and research. It strives to advance
medical knowledge and improve patient care through cutting-edge and
interdisciplinary research, fostering a vibrant research culture among
faculty, students, and staff. The college is also dedicated to providing
compassionate, ethical, and evidence-based healthcare, with a strong
emphasis on preventive care, early diagnosis, and comprehensive
treatment for individuals and communities.It is the first Government
Medical College in Kerala to get A+ accreditation by KUHS.
Basic College Profile

Kerala, was established in 1962.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration

e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.

e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).

e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-I) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal
(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE
portal when the window opens.

All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).

2. Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College,Kottayam" as one of your
preferred choices.

e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.


--- Page 371 ---
3. College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the Government Medical College, Kottayam campus within
the stipulated timeframe for document verification and_ final
admission.

MBBS Seat Distribution (2025)
The distribution of MBBS seats at Government Medical College, Kottayam
is carried out as per Government of India, Government of Kerala, and
National Medical Commission (NMC) norms.

Academic Infrastructure
Government Medical College (GMC), Kottayam is equipped with a strong
academic infrastructure that supports high-quality medical education and
Clinical training.
Central Library - The Central Library serves as the academic hub of the
campus,situated near the Administrative Block.
e Collection: Houses over 23,700 books and a vast collection of
national and international journals.


--- Page 386 ---
e Digital Library: Provides access to E-resources via the ONOS (One
Nation One Subscription) consortium, offering over 13,000 journals
from 30 Publishers,from January 2025 onwards.

e Infrastructure: A 895 sq. m. area with a seating capacity for 200
students, including separate reference and reading sections.

e Book Bank: A dedicated section is available for SC/ST students to
ensure equitable access to resources.

e The library follows Dewey Decimal Classification Scheme and is
automated with the open source software KOHA.

Sports Facilities

e Indoor Fitness Centre and Gymnasium

e Standard Football Court — 1nos

e Standard Cricket Ground — 1nos

e Basketball Court — 3 nos

e Volleyball court — 2 nos

e Shuttle Badminton — 2 nos

e Table Tennis — 4 nos

Arts & Culture: The college provides dedicated resources and platforms to
help students develop individual talents in various artistic and cultural
activities.

Laboratories and Museums : Practical training is facilitated through
specialized laboratories for every department.

Teaching Hospitals :

e Medical College Hospital (MCH): A 2,100+ bed tertiary care facility
where students undergo rigorous clinical rotations.


--- Page 387 ---
e Institute of Child Health (ICH): Located 1.5 km from the main
campus, it serves as the pediatric training center with its own
specialized wards and a leukemia center

e Specialized Units: Students gain exposure to advanced units like
the Multi-Disciplinary Research Unit (MRU) and_ the first
government-sector Heart Transplant unit in India

e Multi-Disciplinary Research Unit (MRU): The MRU is a
Government of India initiative within the college that promotes basic
and clinical research. It allows students and faculty to engage in
high-level medical research, supported by modern equipment and
funding

e Lecture Halls and Examination Rooms: The college features
modern lecture halls specifically designed to accommodate the
annual intake of 175 MBBS students.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Triple Organ Transplant Milestone: In October 2025, GMC
Kottayam became the first government hospital in India to
successfully perform heart, lung, and kidney transplants in a single
day.

e Pioneering Lung Surgery: The institution performed the first-ever
lung transplant in the Kerala government sector (and only the second
after AIIMS Delhi nationally) on October 22, 2025.

e Completed the first knee replacement surgery on a hemophilia patient
in December 2025.


--- Page 388 ---
e The HIV Testing Laboratory (SRL) under the Microbiology
Department achieved NABL accreditation in November 2025.

e The campus is scheduled to host the International Conference on
Medical and Health Sciences (ICMHS) on February 16, March 16,
and April 16, 2026.

e The prestigious Arogya Manthan 3.0 national award for providing the
highest number of free treatments under the AYUSHMAN Bharat
Pradhan Mantri Jan Arogya Scheme

e Best Performer award of MEDISEP were bestowed on this institution
in 2022. Recognitions from LaQshya (Labour Room Quality
Improvement Scheme of NHM)

e In its diamond jubilee year the institution is aspiring for NABH
accreditation and NIRF Ranking.

e Research Day 2025: In May 2025, the college hosted its 3rd annual
International Seminar on Medical Research, themed "Research
Odyssey from Stethoscope to Science," which focused on Al in
academic research.

e Ph.D. Recognition: The Department of Microbiology is now an
approved center for Ph.D. studies under the Kerala University of
Health Sciences (KUHS).

e Recognized as the Regional Medical Education Center of the
National Medical Commission.

e The Department of Cardiology has the distinction of performing the
highest number of primary angioplasty in India.

e The first heart transplant in government sector medical colleges in
India was performed by the CTVS Department in this hospital.


--- Page 389 ---
e A test tube baby was born for the first time in Kerala in the
Department of Obstetrics and Gynecology of this hospital.

e The Departments of Orthopedics and Plastic Surgery perform the
highest number of trauma surgeries and micro vascular surgeries
respectively in Kerala.

e The first liver transplant surgery in the government sector was done
in 2022 in the Department of Surgical Gastroenterology.

e First multidisciplinary Transgender Clinic in India at the government
sector began here in 2017.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity- The hospital has a total bed capacity of 2,178. It
frequently operates at full capacity, sometimes even higher, ensuring
a large patient volume for clinical training.

e ICU beds & Operation Theatres: The hospital is equipped with
multiple intensive care units (ICUs) including medical, surgical,
pediatric, neonatal, and specialty ICUs, along with well-maintained
and fully functional operation theatres catering to both routine and
advanced surgical procedures.

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD):The hospital manages approximately
3,000 outpatients and over 500+ emergency cases daily. Annually,
more than 100,000 inpatients are treated.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments:All major clinical
specialties and several super-specialty departments function actively,
offering comprehensive diagnostic, therapeutic, and surgical services,
and ensuring wide-ranging clinical exposure for students.

Campus Life

e Sports & recreation: Campus has sports facilities, gym, indoor
games and organizes cultural events & student activities.

e Student clubs & academic events:Government Medical College,
Kottayam has an active and diverse student community supported by
various academic, cultural, literary, and specialty clubs. These clubs
organize regular activities that promote professional development,
creativity, leadership, and teamwork among _ students.Academic
events such as seminars, workshops, CMEs, symposiums, medical
quizzes, paper and poster presentations, and_ intercollegiate
competitions are conducted throughout the year.

e Government Medical College, Kottayam offers strong internship
placement quality through its large, well-equipped teaching hospital
with high patient inflow, ensuring extensive hands-on clinical

postings, experienced faculty supervision, and diverse case loads,

e As a government institution, it provides a monthly stipend as per

e The rigorous clinical exposure at Government Medical College
Kottayam prepares graduates well for postgraduate entrance

and careers in government service, private hospitals, academia,
public health, and research.

Government Medical College, Kottayam - Student & Parent
Review
e Student Review:
GMC Kottayam is highly valued for its massive patient volume and
diverse clinical cases, which students describe as the best "practical
classroom" in the state. While the faculty is supportive and the
senior-junior bond is exceptionally strong, the experience is defined


--- Page 394 ---
by a heavy workload and aging hostel infrastructure. Students
appreciate the affordable student-run messes and vibrant campus
festivals, though they note that the high-pressure environment and
ongoing campus construction require significant resilience.
Overall : GMC Kottayam offers an elite clinical education with
unmatched patient exposure and a strong community spirit, though it
requires students to navigate a high-pressure workload and aging
infrastructure.

e Parent Review:
Parents of students at GMC Kottayam generally view the institution
as a prestigious and safe gateway to a medical career, frequently
highlighting the extraordinary clinical exposure and low tuition fees as
its primary advantages. Through the active Parent Teacher
Association (PTA), which has been operational since 1988, parents
are closely involved in campus welfare and regularly meet with faculty
to monitor academic performance. While they express high trust in
the "brand" and the safety of the campus—noting a lack of ragging
and a supportive peer environment—a common concern among
parents is the deteriorating state of the 60-year-old hostels. Recent
feedback indicates that parents have become more vocal about
structural safety and hygiene issues, often relying on the PTA to
advocate for renovations and better living conditions for their children.
Overall : Parents highly value GMC Kottayam for its academic
prestige and the immense clinical growth it offers at a nominal cost,
though they remain deeply concerned about the deteriorating safety
and hygiene of the aging hostel buildings.

Medical College History & Introduction

Government Medical College, Manjeri also known as GMC Manjeri is a fully
government controlled medical college in Kerala.It is the sixth government
medical college under the Government of Kerala , inaugurated on 1
September 2013 by Kerala Chief Minister Oommen Chandy. The college is
affiliated to Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS).The college is
situated in the heart of the city of Manjeri in Malappuram District. The
college is affiliated to Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS), and
has 500 beds and 12 operation theatres with an intake of 110 students for
MBBS every year. This is the first medical college in the government sector
in the State in 31 years, is a fulfillment of a long-cherished dream of the
largest populated district in Kerala state. The campus is equipped with
modern facilities, including well-established laboratories, classrooms, and a
library.

The institution’s vision is to be a leading institution in medical education,
research, and patient care, committed to fostering compassionate,
innovative, and socially responsible healthcare professionals who will lead
the future of medicine. Its mission is to be a beacon of innovation and
excellence in medical education, producing forward-thinking,


--- Page 405 ---
compassionate healthcare leaders who are dedicated to advancing global
health and improving lives. The institution values the adoption of
cutting-edge technologies and methodologies to transform medical
education, research, and patient care, while consistently striving for
excellence through rigorous standards and continuous improvement.
Basic College Profile
e Government Medical College, Manjeri inaugurated on 1 September
2013.
e Status : Government Medical College
e Campus : The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located
in Manjeri, Malappuram.
e Counselling Authority : Commissioner for Entrance Examination
(CEE)
e Affiliation : Kerala University of Health Sciences.
e Recognised by : National Medical Commission (NMC).

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration

e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.

e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).

e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-Il) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal
(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE
portal when the window opens.
All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).

2. Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College,Manjeri,Malappuram" as one of
your preferred choices.

e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.


--- Page 409 ---
3 College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the Government Medical College,Manjeri campus within the
stipulated timeframe for document verification and final admission.

Kerala, and National Medical Commission (NMC) norms.

Infrastructure & Facilities
e Hospital: The college is associated with a large government hospital,
providing students with extensive clinical exposure and hands-on
experience in diverse medical fields.


--- Page 417 ---
e Library and Research Facilities: Equipped with modern libraries,
research labs, and learning resources to support students and faculty
in their academic and research pursuits.

e Hostels and Accommodation: Offers accommodation facilities for
students and staff, ensuring a comfortable and conducive learning
environment.

e Mess facilities : Mess facilities are provided within the campus for
students and residents.

e Museums: The Anatomy department maintains a_ specialized
museum with dissected specimens, models, and charts.

e Fitness & Recreation: On-campus gym facilities and space for
sports and cultural activities.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e The college has achieved recognition from the National Medical
Commission and continues to expand its academic and clinical
departments in accordance with regulatory standards.

e Viral Research & Diagnostic Laboratory (VRDL): The college
gained national attention for its critical role in managing the Nipah
outbreak and the COVID-19 pandemic. The Microbiology department
received awards from the State Government and IMA for its
diagnostic excellence.

e Academic Events: The college regularly conducts CME (Continuing
Medical Education) programs and workshops, such as the "NATCON"
student research conferences, providing a _ platform for
undergraduates to present papers.


--- Page 418 ---
e Community Outreach: Students are highly active in community
health camps and blood donation drives, often collaborating with
organizations like the NSS (National Service Scheme).

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The teaching hospital, upgraded from the former
Manjeri General Hospital, maintains over 500 beds for inpatient care.

e Surgical Facilities: Features 12 modular operation theatres
equipped for both elective and emergency major surgeries.

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD):Hospital handles an average of 2,500 —
3,000+ Outpatients (OPD) daily and over 1,500 Inpatient (IPD)
admissions monthly, maintaining a bed occupancy rate of 90% —
120%.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments:Government Medical
College, Manjeri offers a wide range of specialty departments
including Medicine, Surgery, Obstetrics & Gynaecology, Paediatrics,
Orthopaedics, ENT, Ophthalmology, Anaesthesiology, Psychiatry,
Dermatology, Radiology, and major pre-clinical and para-clinical
subjects. The institution also provides super-specialty services in
areas such as Cardiology, Neurology, Nephrology, Pulmonology, and
Medical Gastroenterology, supporting advanced patient care and
Clinical training.


--- Page 419 ---
Campus Life

e Clubs: A variety of active clubs cater to diverse interests, including
eco groups, adventure groups, drama, music, dance, arts, literature,
quiz, movie lovers, and technical groups.

e Events: Regular cultural and sports events, including annual arts and
sports fests, college day, and celebrations for festivals like Onam,
Christmas, Eid, and Holi are conducted throughout the year, often
featuring invited guests and celebrities.

e Sports: While lacking an eleven-a-side football ground, the college
provides facilities for various indoor and outdoor games such as
chess, table tennis, cricket, and basketball, along with a gymnasium.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Government Medical College, Manjeri provides separate hostel
facilities for undergraduate students, interns, and postgraduate
trainees within the campus.

e Mess facilities are available to ensure hygienic and regular food
services for residents, supporting a comfortable and disciplined living
environment conducive to academic and clinical training.

e Warden supervision and administrative support ensure discipline,
safety, and smooth functioning of hostel life, contributing to a
conducive academic and living atmosphere.

Safety & Support Systems

e Anti-Ragging Committee: The college maintains a Zero-Tolerance

Policy toward ragging, with a multi-layered oversight system.


--- Page 420 ---
Students must submit an online affidavit during admission.Committee
is chaired by the Principal, this committee includes the Vice-Principal,
senior faculty, the Inspector of Police (Gandhinagar), and student
representatives.

e Grievance Redressal: The institution provides internal mechanisms
for students to voice concerns regarding academics or campus life,
often managed through the Principal’s office.

e Student Counseling System: Faculty mentors are assigned to small
groups of students (Mentor-Mentee program) to provide academic
guidance and emotional support.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Internships at GMC Manjeri are characterized by high-intensity
clinical work and exceptional procedural exposure, largely due to the
massive patient load from the Malappuram district.

e Interns (House Surgeons) benefit from a high patient-to-doctor ratio.
Because there are fewer PG students compared to older colleges,
interns often get to perform more hands-on procedures (minor
surgeries, suturing, intubations) themselves.

e Rotations: Includes mandatory postings in General Medicine,
Surgery, OBG, and Pediatrics, plus specialized community postings
in Rural/Urban Health Centers and even Tribal Hospitals (e.g., GTSH
Attapadi).

e As a government institution, it provides a monthly stipend as per
current Kerala State Government norms.


--- Page 421 ---
e Post-Internship Value: The sheer variety of cases (from tropical
fevers to trauma) makes graduates highly competent for
"first-contact" practice or for securing Junior Resident (JR) positions
in major hospitals.

due to high patient inflow and _ its growing academic environment. The
faculty are regarded as supportive and academically competent, helping

is steadily improving, with adequate academic and hospital facilities to
meet training requirements.

Hostel and mess facilities are considered satisfactory, and the campus
environment is disciplined and focused on medical education. While some
students note that certain facilities are still developing compared to older
government medical colleges, overall student satisfaction remains positive
due to good clinical training, government institutional support, and a
professional learning atmosphere.

Overall : Government Medical College, Manjeri offers strong clinical
exposure, supportive faculty, and a disciplined academic environment.

improving infrastructure and good student satisfaction.
Parent Review:
From a parent’s perspective, Government Medical College, Manjeri is a
dependable and well-structured government institution that provides quality
medical education in a safe and disciplined environment. The attached
teaching hospital offers extensive clinical exposure, which gives confidence
that students receive strong practical training alongside academic learning.
Parents generally appreciate the supportive and qualified faculty, who
guide students academically and professionally. Hostel facilities are
considered satisfactory, with proper supervision, security, and mess
services, ensuring students’ well-being and comfort away from home. The
campus follows strict rules on discipline, anti-ragging, and student welfare,
which reassures parents about their children’s safety.
Overall: parents view GMC Manjeri as a trustworthy choice for medical
education, combining affordable government education, good clinical
training, and a secure campus atmosphere that supports both academic
success and personal development.

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Government Medical College, Palakkad, also known as the Institute of
Integrated Medical Sciences (IIMS), was established in 2014 by the
Government of Kerala with the vision of expanding access to quality
medical education and healthcare services in the northern regions of the
state. Affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and
approved by the National Medical Commission (NMC), the institution has
rapidly emerged as a center of academic excellence, modern infrastructure,
and quality patient care.
The establishment of the college was a strategic initiative to decentralize
medical education, especially for students from Palakkad and neighboring
districts who earlier had to travel long distances to pursue medical studies.
The district administration identified an unutilized site for the project,
recognizing the need for a government medical college in a region with a
significant population from Scheduled Castes and backward communities.
The project is funded under the Scheduled Caste Component Plan (SCP)
and envisioned as a residential, integrated healthcare education campus


--- Page 432 ---
with in-house facilities to meet all basic needs. The institution is designed
as an eco-friendly green campus, with emphasis on renewable energy
sources such as solar and wind. In addition to MBBS education, the college
aims to expand into paramedical, super-specialty, research, and
international exchange programs, making it a future-ready institution
committed to inclusive growth, social equity, and excellence in healthcare
education.
The institution’s vision is to build a center of excellence for the education
and development of the next generation of physicians and scientists , to
develop a holistic approach in the management of patients , to integrate
traditional and new knowledge in the field of health care to foster research
and innovation ,to provide compassionate clinical care of the highest quality
at the lowest possible cost.And its mission is to improve the quality and
health of the lives of the communities we serve through dedication,
understanding, discovery and healing and develop evidence based
treatment strategies most suited for our nation.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Core Eligibility Requirements & Registration

e NEET-UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify in the
NEET-UG exam conducted by the NTA.

e Academic: Must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry,
Biology/Biotechnology, and English as separate subjects, achieving
at least 50% aggregate in Physics, Chemistry, and
Biology/Biotechnology (40% for SC/ST and 45% for SEBC).

e Nativity: Only candidates classified as Keralite or Non-Keralite
Category | (NK-I) are generally eligible for 85% State Quota seats in
Government Medical Colleges.

e Registration:

State Quota (85%): Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal
(cee.kerala.gov.in). You must upload your NEET results to the CEE
portal when the window opens.
All India Quota (15%): Register on the MCC portal (mcc.nic.in).

2. Counselling & Choice Filling

e Option Entry: During the counselling rounds, you must log in and
select "Government Medical College,Palakkad" as one of your
preferred choices.

e Trial & Final Allotments: CEE/MCC will release trial allotments
followed by final allotment memos based on your NEET rank and
reservation category.


--- Page 436 ---
3.College Reporting & Admission

e Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to CEE (online) as
specified in your allotment memo.

e Physical Reporting: Once a seat is allotted, you must physically
report to the Government Medical College, Palakkad campus within
the stipulated timeframe for document verification and_ final
admission.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls & Classrooms: The campus includes air-conditioned
lecture theaters and smart classrooms equipped with advanced
audio-visual aids to facilitate interactive learning.

e Laboratories: Modern, well-equipped labs are available for
pre-clinical and para-clinical departments, including Anatomy,
Physiology, and Biochemistry.

e Central Library: An air-conditioned facility housing over 50,000
medical books, journals (Indian and foreign), and e-resources. It
includes dedicated reading spaces for students and faculty and
remains open until 8 PM

e Skill Development & Research: The _ infrastructure features
dedicated skill development centers, museums for various
departments, and research wings for biomedical innovation.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Medical Conferences: The college is slated to be a primary venue
and participant in various International Medical Conferences in
Palakkad scheduled for 2025 and 2026. These events focus on early
diagnostics, vaccine preparation, and clinical research.

e National Ranking: GMC Palakkad has been ranked 177th in India
and 14th in Kerala for its medical programs by Collegedunia (2025).


--- Page 441 ---
e Faculty-led research projects in community medicine, public health,

clinical medicine, and medical education.
Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The teaching hospital maintains 544 teaching beds,
providing a significant clinical base for the 100 annual MBBS
students.

e ICU beds & Operation Theatres:The hospital is equipped with 21
dedicated Intensive Care beds distributed across _ specialized
units. The hospital includes 6 major operation theaters and multiple
minor OTs, as well as a 22-bed central casualty and emergency
trauma care service.

e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD):The hospital records a high daily
outpatient turnover, with approximately 950 to 1,118 patients treated
each day across various departments. It has a teaching bed strength
of 544 beds, accommodating a large number of inpatient admissions.
The average IPD occupancy is approximately 450 patients per day.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments:Government Medical
College, Palakkad offers a wide range of specialty departments
including General Medicine, General Surgery, Pediatrics, Obstetrics &
Gynecology, Orthopedics, Psychiatry, Dermatology, ENT,
Ophthalmology, Radiology, Anesthesiology, Pathology, Microbiology,
Forensic Medicine, and Community Medicine. The institution is
progressively developing super-specialty services to enhance
advanced patient care.

auto-rickshaw or taxi ride will get you to the campus.

e Palakkad Junction (PGT): Also known as Olavakkode, this is the
main station where most long-distance trains stop. It is approximately
9-11 km away. Taxis and autos are available 24/7 at the exit.

travel very viable:

e KSRTC / Private Bus Stands: The Palakkad KSRTC terminal and the

intersection.

f > % Government Medical College, Konni,
% P YJ Pathanamthitta
Kummannoor PO, Konni, Pathanamthitta
LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
The Government Medical College (GMC), Konni, located in the
Pathanamthitta district of Kerala, was officially established in 2022 when it
admitted its first batch of medical students. Affiliated with the Kerala
University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the National
Medical Commission (NMC), the institution currently offers a single
undergraduate program: the Bachelor of Medicine and Bachelor of Surgery
(MBBS). This course has an annual intake of 100 seats and follows a
5.5-year duration, including a mandatory one-year rotating internship.
Admission is strictly based on National Eligibility cum Entrance Test
(NEET-UG) scores. While the college currently focuses on undergraduate
education, there are future plans to introduce postgraduate (MD/MS)
programs as the institution matures.
The history of GMC Konni began as a strategic initiative to provide tertiary
healthcare to a region where residents previously had to travel nearly
100km to Kottayam or Thiruvananthapuram for specialist services. The
foundation stone was laid on January 26, 2013, by then-Chief Minister


--- Page 456 ---
Oommen Chandy on a 50-acre campus atop Nedumpara Hill. Developed
with a budget of approximately %200 crore, the project saw its teaching
hospital inaugurated by Chief Minister Pinarayi Vijayan on September 14,
2020. Today, the 500-bedded multi-specialty hospital serves as a vital
healthcare hub and the primary base hospital for Sabarimala pilgrims,
featuring advanced facilities like modular operation theatres, intensive care
units (ICUs), and 24/7 emergency services.

Mission and Key Objectives

e Quality Healthcare: Promoting health with compassion and
high-quality treatment in a patient-friendly environment.

e Comprehensive Services: Offering 24-hour emergency care, IP
services, and modern diagnostic capabilities.

e Medical Education: Fostering academic and clinical training for
medical students under the Kerala University of Health Sciences
(KUHS).

Vision

The institution aims to be a leading center for medical education and
excellence in healthcare, providing accessible, modern medical services to
the community, including serving as a critical healthcare base for the
region, such as for Sabarimala pilgrims.

Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Government Medical College (GMC), Konni

e Location: Nedumpara Hill, near Vattamon, Anakuthy, Konni,
Pathanamthitta District, Kerala — 689691

e Year of Establishment: 2022 (admitted first batch); foundation stone
laid in 2013


--- Page 457 ---
e Type of College: Government / State-run Medical Institution
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala (KEAM) for state quota; MCC for All India Quota
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC)
e MBBS Intake: 100 seats
e Course Duration: 5.5 years (4.5 years of academic study plus 1 year
of mandatory rotating internship)
e Hospital Type: 500-bedded Multi-Specialty Government Teaching
Hospital; serves as the primary base hospital for Sabarimala pilgrims.

due to the hospital's role as the base hospital for Sabarimala pilgrims,

providing a diverse demographic of cases ranging from routine
infectious diseases to high-volume emergency trauma
MBBS (Course) — Core Details
e Total Duration: 5.5 years.

o Academic Phase: 4.5 years of medical study divided into 9
semesters.

© Compulsory Internship: 1 year of mandatory rotating medical
internship in the attached 500-bed multispecialty hospital.

e Seat Capacity: 100 students annually.
e Assessment / exam format:

o Components: Includes Theory tests (Part Completion Tests -
PCTs), Practicals, Viva-voce, Logbook maintenance, and
AETCOM (Attitude, Ethics, and Communication) modules.

o Frequency: Usually, there are at least two PCTs per phase and
a Mandatory Prelim Exam (which mimics the University pattern)
before the finals.

o Eligibility Criteria: You must secure a minimum of 50% marks in
total (with at least 40% separately in theory and practicals) to
be eligible for University exams.

e MBBS (Bachelor of Medicine & Bachelor of Surgery)

o Duration: 4.5 years + 1 year internship

o Intake: 100 seats per year

o Admission through NEET-UG

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. Appear for NEET UG: Qualify in the National Eligibility cum Entrance
Test (NEET UG) conducted by the NTA.

2. Register for Kerala Counseling: Visit the official website,
cee.kerala.gov.in, during the specified dates to register and fill out the
online application.

3. Option Entry: Enter your choices for medical colleges (including GMC
Konni) in order of preference on the CEE portal.


--- Page 461 ---
4. Document Verification: Selected candidates will be called for online or
offline verification of original documents (NEET scorecard, 10+2
marksheet, ID, reservation certificates if applicable).

5. Seat Allotment: Seat allocation occurs based on your NEET rank and
choices, published on the CEE website.

6. College Reporting: Download the allotment letter and report to GMC
Konni with all original documents and fees within the given deadline.

7. Final Formalities: Complete fee payment, sign undertakings/bonds,
and attend orientation to join the program.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: Modern, equipped with audio-visual aids for interactive
learning.

e Laboratories: State-of-the-art labs for various medical disciplines
providing practical experience.

e Library: A large, well-stocked library with textbooks, journals, and
digital resources, featuring a reading room.

e Teaching Hospital: A 300-500 bed facility with modern tech, modular
OTs, ICUs, and 24/7 emergency care, providing diverse clinical
exposure.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights


--- Page 467 ---
e Awareness Campaigns: The institution actively participates in global
health weeks, including World Antimicrobial Resistance Awareness
Week (November 2024), World Glaucoma Week (March 2024), and
World Anemia Prevention Day.

e Departmental Publications: Faculty members have _ published
research on anatomical variations, specifically a meta-analysis
regarding the testicular artery and vein, proposing new classifications
with clinical implications.

e Academic Excellence: The 2023 batch achieved a notable milestone
by recording a 100% pass rate in their first year, a first for the
institution.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Capacity: Currently operating as a 500-bed multi-specialty hospital
(initially inaugurated with 300 beds and expanded to meet NMC
requirements).

e Surgical Suites: Equipped with Modular Operation Theatres designed
for infection control and high-efficiency surgical workflows.

e Critical Care: Specialized Intensive Care Units (ICUs) and a
dedicated Post-Operative Ward to manage high-risk patients.

e Emergency & Trauma: Features a 24/7 Emergency and Casualty
department capable of handling large-scale trauma and acute
medical cases.

e Specialized Units: The facility includes a Central Sterile Services
Department (CSSD), a PAC (Pre-Anesthetic Check-up) clinic, and
diagnostic services across General Medicine, General Surgery,
Pediatrics, and OBG.


--- Page 468 ---
e Clinical Skill Lab: A dedicated facility where students practice medical
procedures on high-fidelity mannequins. This allows them to master
skills like IV cannulation, CPR, and suturing in a_ controlled
environment before moving to real patient care.

e Patient Inflow: By serving over 3.5 million local residents who
previously had to travel over 100km to Kottayam or
Thiruvananthapuram, the hospital ensures a steady and varied "case
mix" for undergraduate learning.

Campus Life

e Sports: The 50-acre campus includes a gymnasium and facilities for
volleyball, badminton, and cricket. Students also participate in the
inter-medical college sports meets organized by KUHS (Kerala
University of Health Sciences).

e Student Union: A very active Union organizes frequent events, from
"Fresher’s Day" to social awareness rallies and blood donation
camps.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Room Layout: Most rooms are triple-sharing, designed to be spacious
and _ well-ventilated to handle the hilly, humid climate of
Pathanamthitta.

e Modern Amenities: Unlike many older government institutions, the
hostels here include elevators (lifts), 24/7 security personnel, and
CCTV surveillance in common areas.


--- Page 469 ---
e Proximity: The hostel is conveniently located just a 3-minute walk
from the academic block and hospital.

e Management: The mess is student-managed or run by private
catering services under student supervision, ensuring that the menu
reflects current batch preferences.

Safety & Support Systems

e Hostel Surveillance: The modern 10-story hostel blocks are equipped
with CCTV surveillance in common areas and mandatory entry/exit
logs.

e Ragging Prevention Committee: An active Anti-Ragging Committee is
in place to ensure a zero-tolerance policy. It consists of faculty
members who conduct regular checks and provide a clear reporting
mechanism for juniors.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles issues
related to gender-based discrimination or harassment, ensuring a
safe workspace and learning environment for female students and
staff.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Clinical Exposure: Interns gain significant hands-on experience due
to the hospital's high patient volume. The facility serves as the
primary tertiary care center for the Pathanamthitta district, ensuring
exposure to a diverse range of medical and surgical cases.


--- Page 470 ---
e Stipend: As per 2026 state guidelines for Kerala government medical
colleges, interns receive a monthly stipend ranging from %20,000 to
27,000.

e Placement Structure: Like most Indian medical colleges, there are no
"campus placements". Graduates typically transition into the Kerala
Health Services, join private multispecialty hospitals, or pursue
postgraduate (PG) studies via NEET-PG.

Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures

e MBBS students undergoing their one-year compulsory rotating
residential internship (CRRI) receive a flat monthly stipend.

e Monthly Stipend: 27,300

e Nature: Fixed amount for the duration of the 12-month internship.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)

e Ragging Prevention Committee: An active committee monitors the
campus. Any student found guilty faces immediate suspension and a
potential criminal record under the Kerala Prohibition of Ragging Act.

e Curfew: Students are generally required to be inside the hostel by
9:30 PM. Biometric attendance or physical roll calls are conducted
nightly.

Government Medical College, Konni -Student & Parent
Review
STUDENT REVIEW
The smaller batch size of 100 ensures every student receives
personalized mentorship and direct attention from the highly qualified
faculty. The academic block is praised for its spacious smart
classrooms, well-equipped departmental labs, and a multi-floor digital
library.Being the base hospital for Sabarimala pilgrims provides
students with unmatched, high-intensity training in emergency
medicine and trauma care.
PARENT REVIEW
Parents consistently praise the affordable government fee structure
(approx. %25,000-%35,000 per year), which provides high-quality
education at a fraction of private college costs. Many parents
highlight the 10-story modern hostel’s safety features, including
full-time security personnel, biometric attendance, and CCTV
surveillance.

travelers from the Kollam or Tamil Nadu side.
By Air

110 km away. You can hire a taxi or take a KSRTC bus from the
Thiruvananthapuram central terminal toward Pathanamthitta.

LOGO
#OVERVIEW
*Medical College History & Introduction
Government Medical College Thrissur, established in 1982 is one of the
leading centers in medical education in Kerala, India. Spread over an area
of more than 250 acres, it is located in the serene surroundings of
Mulagunnathukavu (M.G Kavu) 14 km from Thrissur.On April 1, 1982,
Kerala Governor Mrs. Jyoti Venkatachellam inaugurated the college. The
foundation stone of the proposed college building was laid on April 30,
1982, at Mulungathukkav. The medical college initially functioned on the
campus of the Veterinary College in Mannuthy.By March 1983, the
institution shifted to its permanent location at Mulungathukkav. The first
batch of 74 students joined in April 1982 and completed the course in May
1987. The college received permanent accreditation from the IMC in 1991
and from the WHO in 1993. The Kerala University of Health Sciences
(KUHS) began functioning in the campus in 2009.It continues to be the
premier medical institution in this part of the state, delivering health care to


--- Page 478 ---
three districts of Kerala and to patients in the neighbouring districts of Tamil
Nadu.
The vision of Government Medical College, Thrissur is to provide
world-class medical education and mould students as experts in the
medical profession, thereby delivering holistic healthcare services to the
community. Its mission is to produce competent medical graduates who
can function effectively within the healthcare system by striving for
academic excellence, developing self-reliant professionals with strong
social commitment, functioning as a premier healthcare provider for central
Kerala, delivering competency-based training to create skilled and
compassionate Indian Medical Graduates, and contributing to medical
advancement through research and evidence-based practices.
* General Information

e Year Of Establishment : 1982

e Location : Thrissur, Kerala

e Type : Government Medical College

e Affiliation : Kerala University of Health Sciences

e Approved by : National Medical Commission (NMC)

e Hospital Attached : Government Medical College Thrissur
#HOSPITAL STATISTICS

e Total Beds : 1400+

e Total ICU Beds : 75+

e Total Operation Theaters : 19 (13 Major + 6 Minor)

e Total Outpatient :~1200+

#COURSES & SEATS
*Courses Offered

e MBBS

e PG-MD/MS
*MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Duration : 5.5 Years (4.5 Years Academic Study + 1 Year
Compulsory Rotatory Internship).

e Admission Criteria : Admission is strictly based on qualification in
the NEET-UG (National Eligibility cum Entrance Test) conducted at
the national level, followed by state counselling conducted by the
Commissioner for Entrance Examinations (CEE), Kerala as per
Government of Kerala norms.

e Annual Intake : 175 MBBS seats.

e Assessment / Exam Format : The MBBS assessment system at
Government Medical College Thrissur follows the regulations of the
National Medical Commission (NMC) and the Kerala University of
Health Sciences (KUHS), Thrissur. It includes continuous internal
assessment along with final university examinations. Students are
evaluated through internal tests, practical examinations, viva voce,
assignments, and clinical assessments such as case presentations


--- Page 480 ---
and logbook-based skill evaluations. At the end of each professional
phase, university examinations are conducted, consisting of theory
papers, practical/clinical exams, and viva voce to assess academic
knowledge and clinical competencies. Students are also required to
maintain the prescribed attendance in both theory classes and clinical
postings to be eligible for university examinations.

#ADMISSION PROCEDURE

*Admission Procedure (MBBS)

e Step 1: NEET-UG Entrance Examination


--- Page 482 ---
o Attempt the Exam: Register for and appear in the national
NEET-UG medical exam conducted by the National Testing
Agency (NTA).

o Acquire Qualification Score: Score above the declared national
qualifying percentile (50th percentile for General, 40th
percentile for SC/ST/OBC).

e Step 2: Counselling Portal Selection & Registration

o Determine your quota pathway and register on the respective
centralized online portal when application windows open:

o For State Quota (85% of Seats): Register on the CEE Kerala
Portal through the KEAM Candidate Portal. Enter your
personal, academic, and NEET roll details.

o For All India Quota (15% of Seats): Register on the Medical
Counselling Committee Portal.

e Step 3: Document Uploading & Registration

o Upload Certificates: Digitally upload your signature, photograph,
Class 10/12 certificates, and categorical proofs (such as
Domicile, Non-Creamy Layer, or EWS credentials).

o Complete Registration: Submit the profile form online to be
included in the official CEE or MCC counseling lists.

o Save Confirmation: Download and print the Application
Acknowledgment Page for subsequent verification rounds.

e Step 4: Web Option Entry & Choice Locking

o Access Option Window: Log into your candidate portal profile
once the Centralized Allotment Process (CAP) choice-filling
window goes live


--- Page 483 ---
o Set Priority: Manually list your preferred colleges. Place
Government Medical College Thrissur at your top priority level
to optimize selection probabilities against your rank.

o Lock Choices: Review and electronically lock your choice
selections before the standard round deadline closes.

e Step 5: Seat Allotment Publication

o Check Merit Allocation: View the web-allotment results
published by CEE or MCC based on your national rank,
category reservations, and structural seat vacancies.

© Download Allotment Memo: If a seat is granted at the institution,
generate and download your formal Allotment Memo and
candidate data profile sheet from the site.

e Step 6: Physical Reporting & Document Verification

o Report On-Campus: Travel in person to the Academic Block at
GMC Thrissur within the concrete timeline dates outlined on
your allotment memo.

o Credential Evaluation: Present all physical original
documents—including your NEET admit card, 10+2 mark
sheets, Transfer Certificate (TC), Conduct Certificate, and
Medical Fitness/Vaccination forms—to the _ institutional
verification desk.

e Step 7: Service Bond Execution

o Sign State Bond: Confirm registration by executing the
mandatory Kerala Government Service Bond on 2200 local
stamp paper along with your valid legal sureties. This legal
document commits you to serve the state healthcare sector for


--- Page 484 ---
a specified duration following graduation. Your MBBS seat
enrollment is then officially certified.
* Admission Procedure for MD/MS (Postgraduate)
e Step 1: NEET-PG Entrance Qualification

o Appear for NEET-PG: Candidates must register for and take the
National Eligibility cum Entrance Test for Postgraduates
(NEET-PG) conducted by the National Board of Examinations
(NBE).

o Meet the Cutoff: Secure scores at or above the national
qualifying percentile according to category parameters.

e Step 2: Online Counselling Registration

o Select Quota Pathway: Based on rank eligibility, candidates
must register on the appropriate central gateway when windows
open:

ua For State Quota (50%): Create an account on the CEE
Kerala Portal under the "PG Medical" portal.
a For All India Quota (50%): Register on the MCC Portal.

o State Merit List: CEE Kerala filters registered applications to
publish a designated State Merit List. Only applicants listed on
this merit index can advance to the options phase.

e Step 3: Document Uploading (State Portal)

o Digital Submission: Upload clear PDF scans of mandatory
eligibility certifications to your CEE candidate portal page.

o Required Uploads: Academic parameters, MBBS
degree/provisional passes, Compulsory Rotatory Medical
Internship (CRMI) certificates, Nativity verification documents


--- Page 485 ---
(proving Kerala origin), and Category/Non-Creamy Layer
proofs.
e Step 4: Web Option Registration & Choice Locking

o Option Entry: Log into your respective counseling profile (CEE
or MCC) during active Choice Filling schedules.

o Prioritize Preference: Manually choose clinical/non-clinical
specialties and place Government Medical College Thrissur
alongside your chosen specialized branch (e.g., MD General
Medicine, MS Orthopedics) at the highest priority tier.

o Lock Choices: Finalize, save, and lock preference arrays prior
to the session deadline.

e Step 5: Seat Allotment Publication

o Check Results: Review the sequential seat allotments (Round
1, Round 2, Mop-Up) declared on the web portals based on
NEET-PG rank matrices, choice configurations, and reservation
criteria.

o Download Memo: If you are matched to a seat at GMC Thrissur,
download your official Allotment Memo and candidate Data
Sheet.

e Step 6: Physical Reporting & Document Verification

o Report to College: Travel in person to the Academic Block /
Principal's Office at GMC Thrissur within the designated joining
window noted on your allotment memo.

o Submit Credentials: Hand over all original physical documents
to the verifying board. The required documents include:

= CEE/MCC Allotment Memo & Candidate Data Sheet
m NEET-PG Scorecard & Admit Card


--- Page 486 ---
a SSLC Certificate (DOB proof) & 10+2 Certificates

= MBBS Degree Certificate & Semester-wise Mark Sheets

= CRRI/CRMI Internship Completion Certificate

mu Permanent Medical Council Registration (TCMC / State
Council / NMC)

a Transfer Certificate (TC) & Conduct Certificate from the
last institution

mu Physical Fitness Certificate & Vaccination Certificates
(Hepatitis A & B, MMR, Varicella)

e Step 7: Compulsory Bond Execution
o Sign State Bond: Candidates must sign two distinct indemnity
service bonds on %200 Kerala stamp papers with two valid
sureties:

m Bond 1 (Compulsory. Service): An official declaration
pledging to serve the Government of Kerala for a
minimum duration of 1 year right after graduating.

m Bond 2 (Liquidated Damages): A legal undertaking
agreeing to forfeit a heavy penalty fee in liquidated
damages if the course is discontinued or abandoned
mid-way.

Infrastructure & Facilities
e Central Library:


--- Page 499 ---
o The Central Library is attached to the Govt. Medical College,
Thrissur is designed to provide health and scientific information
to medical professionals, faculties, graduate and post graduate
students and medical researchers of the institution.

o The Central library contains more than 23749 books and 59
periodicals.

o The Central Library has access to ONOS and Access Medicine,
with hundreds of online journals and e-books, provided by
DME, Kerala.

o The library is also a member of ERMED consortium of National
Medical Library (NML). The Library is linked to the National
Knowledge Network and provides access to its patrons a wide
range of electronic resources, print and digital journal
collections and print reference books.

e DHR-ICMR MRU: Government of India approved the scheme for
‘Establishment of Multi -Disciplinary Research Units (MRUs) in the
Government Medical Colleges/Research Institutions’ as a path-
breaking initiative to develop or strengthen the health research
infrastructure in the country.

e Sports & Recreation: A physical education department oversees
comprehensive indoor and outdoor sports facilities, including a cricket
ground, football court, basketball courts, an indoor stadium, and a
well-equipped gymnasium.


--- Page 500 ---
H8 | Roktoanaastina [Noe
Pe [seinen Same
e Lecture Halls: Large, well-ventilated lecture rooms equipped with
smart classroom technology (audio-visual aids) for effective teaching.
e Laboratories: State-of-the-art labs for pre-clinical subjects (Anatomy,
Physiology, Biochemistry), a dedicated Skill Lab for practical training,
and various specialized departmental labs.
e Auditorium & Seminar Halls: An auditorium for youth festivals and a
large academic complex with a convocation hall and seminar halls for
academic events and conferences.


--- Page 501 ---
Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e National Rankings (2025): GMC Thrissur was ranked 63rd out of
522 medical colleges in India and 5th overall in Kerala for 2025.

e KUHS Ranks: In the January 2025 Kerala University of Health
Sciences (KUHS) MD examinations, students from the Department of
Forensic Medicine secured the 1st and 3rd university ranks.

e Departmental Awards: The Dermatology department has earned
over 16 national and 23 state awards, including prestigious IADVL
Oration awards for senior faculty in recent years.

e Indigenous Medical Tech: The college is involved in state-level
efforts to boost indigenous medical technologies through grants from
the Indian Council of Medical Research (ICMR).

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Total Bed Capacity: Approximately 1,706 beds (one of the highest in
Kerala), ensuring students encounter a vast array of clinical cases.

e Departments: There are 34 academic departments, covering all
major medical and surgical specialties and super-specialties such as
Cardiology, Neurosurgery, Oncology, and Nephrology.

e Intensive Care Units (ICUs): Fully functional, well-equipped 50 +
ICUs for various specialties are available, including Medical ICU,
Surgical ICU, Pediatric ICU, and a 42-bedded Neonatal ICU with
advanced Level Ill care facilities (e.g., high-frequency ventilation).

e Emergency & Trauma Care: A 24x7 Casualty and Trauma Care unit
provides immediate and continuous emergency services, supported
by resident doctors, nursing staff, and a functional blood bank.


--- Page 502 ---
e Patient inflow (OPD/IPD): Government Medical College, Thrissur
records an average OPD footfall of around 5,000—7,000 patients per
day. The hospital manages approximately 1,200—1,500 inpatient
admissions per month, providing strong clinical exposure.(For the
most current, real-time daily statistics, patients and staff can check
the "Patient Statistics" section on the official GMC Thrissur website. )

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments: Government Medical
College, Thrissur offers a wide range of specialty departments
including General Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, Obstetrics &
Gynecology, Orthopedics, Psychiatry, Dermatology, ENT,
Ophthalmology, and all pre-clinical and para-clinical subjects. It also
houses major super-specialty departments such as Cardiology,
Neurology, Neurosurgery, Nephrology, Urology, Gastroenterology,
Oncology, Endocrinology, Pulmonology, Plastic Surgery, Pediatric
Surgery, and Critical Care Medicine.

Campus Life

e Cultural Hub: Famous for its energetic arts fests and being a top
contender in university-level cultural competitions.

e Social Service: Highly active student-led charity wings like
Punarjani, which provides medicine and aid to poor patients.


--- Page 503 ---
e Atmosphere: Described as "serene and apolitical," offering a
balance of high-intensity medical study and a vibrant social life in the
"Triangle" and "Quadrangle" hangout spots.

Hostel & Mess Facilities
The college provides separate hostel facilities for male and female students
within or near the campus. Hostels offer basic amenities, study-friendly
environments, and mess facilities serving regular meals to students, with
administrative supervision to ensure safety and discipline.
Hostel Category Capacity Room Count
(Beds)

Men/Ladies
GMC Thrissur provides affordable, student-managed mess facilities within
the hostel premises, offering hygienic vegetarian and non-vegetarian meals
with input on the menu provided by the residents.
Safety & Support Systems
1. Student Safety & Anti-Ragging Measures
The college follows a Zero Tolerance Policy toward ragging, as mandated
by the Supreme Court and NMC guidelines.


--- Page 504 ---
e Anti-Ragging Committee: Monitored by the Principal and Vice
Principal.lt includes HODs, hostel wardens, local police
representatives (Sub Inspector), media, and student representatives.

e Anti-Ragging Squads: Faculty and student squads conduct surprise
inspections, particularly in sensitive areas and hostels.

e Hostel Security: Students must submit a mandatory anti-ragging
affidavit (signed by parents) to secure accommodation. Hostels have
dedicated wardens.

2. Grievance & Redressal Systems

e Grievance Redressal Committee: A dedicated platform for
students, faculty, and women to report issues and seek resolution.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically for addressing
complaints related to women's safety and harassment.

e Academic Monitoring Committee (AMC): Mentors students for both
academic performance and personality development, ensuring a
support system is in place for those facing difficulties.

3. Student Welfare & Health Support

e Mentorship Program: Faculty members are assigned to students to
provide academic and personal guidance.

e Screening & Counseling Center: Located within the Community
Medicine department, providing adolescent guidance and mental
health counseling.

e PTA (Parent Teacher Association): Facilitates communication
between parents and the institution to monitor student welfare.


--- Page 505 ---
Internship placement quality — quick summary

e The college is known for heavy patient inflow, providing interns with
significant hands-on experience in managing both common and
complex clinical scenarios.

e Interns undergo mandatory 12-month rotations across major and
minor departments, including General Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics,
and Orthopedics.

e The college has a high success rate for further studies, with over 95%
of graduates qualifying for higher education through exams like NEET
PG.

College rules & discipline- (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)
1. Anti-Ragging System


--- Page 506 ---
The college enforces a strict anti-ragging policy in accordance with the
Supreme Court of India and National Medical Commission (NMC)
regulations.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: Led by the Principal (Dr. Ashokan N.) and
Vice Principal (Dr. Sanal Kumar K.B.), this committee includes HODs,
hostel wardens, administrative officers, student union representatives
(Chairperson and General Secretary), and parent representatives.

e Monitoring: The committee is responsible for monitoring anti-ragging
activities and awarding punishments to those found guilty.

e Affidavits: Every student and parent must submit a mandatory
anti-ragging undertaking at the time of admission.

2. Grievance Redressal & Support
The institution has established several bodies to ensure student and faculty
welfare:

e Grievance Redressal Committee: Provides a formal platform for
students and faculty to voice complaints and seek resolutions.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles matters
related to sexual harassment and women's safety.Student Support
and Guidance Cell: Aimed at the psychological and academic
well-being of the students.

e Academic Monitoring Committee (AMC): Ensures teaching
standards are met and monitors student attendance and performance
to intervene where necessary.


--- Page 507 ---
3. Hostel Rules & Discipline
The hostel administration is led by the Principal, with specific wardens for
different sections

e Key Regulations:

o Right of Admission: Accommodation is not a right; the
administration can refuse entry to any student known for
disciplinary violations or who disturbs the "peace and
tranquility" of the hostel.

© Strict Obedience: Residents must strictly follow all current rules
and those enforced from time to time.

o Room Allotment: Rooms are re-allotted every year by the
Assistant Warden based on availability.

o Continuous Stay: Once admitted, a student remains a resident
for the year unless debarred on disciplinary grounds.

e Application Process: Students must apply for room allotment via
email with specific subject lines (e.g., Application for MBBS hostel
room allotment — Name — Batch) and submit physical forms once
classes commence.

Government Medical College,Thrissur - Student & Parent
Review

Student Review:

Students describe Government Medical College, Thrissur as a strong
academic institution with excellent clinical exposure, supported by a high


--- Page 508 ---
patient inflow and a wide range of specialties. Faculty members are
experienced, approachable, and actively involved in teaching through ward
rounds, case discussions, and clinical demonstrations.

Infrastructure is adequate for a government medical college, with
well-functioning hospital services and diagnostic facilities, though some
areas may feel crowded. Hostel and mess facilities are basic but sufficient,
and the overall campus environment is disciplined, safe, and focused on
professional development.

Overall: Government Medical College, Thrissur is a well-established
institution known for strong academics and excellent clinical exposure due
to high patient inflow. It offers a disciplined, supportive learning
environment that prepares students well for medical practice.

Parent review

Parents generally view Government Medical College, Thrissur as a reliable
and academically strong institution for medical education. They appreciate
the experienced faculty, structured teaching methods, and the college’s
long-standing reputation in Kerala. The high patient inflow is seen as a
major strength, as it ensures extensive clinical exposure and hands-on
training, helping students gain confidence and practical skills early in their
careers.

Parents also value the disciplined campus environment and the presence
of safety systems such as anti-ragging measures and grievance redressal
mechanisms. Hostel and mess facilities, though basic, are considered safe
and adequate for students’ daily needs. Overall, parents feel reassured
about their children’s academic progress, professional development, and


--- Page 509 ---
personal safety, making GMC Thrissur a trusted choice for medical
education.

Overall:Parents consider GMC Thrissur a reliable and academically sound
institution with experienced faculty and strong clinical training. They
appreciate the disciplined campus culture and feel confident about their
children’s safety and future.

Way to reach

By Air

The nearest airport is Cochin International Airport (COK) in Nedumbassery,
which is about 50-60 km away from the college.


--- Page 512 ---
e From the airport, you can hire a taxi (approx. 55 min journey) or take

a KSRTC or private bus towards Thrissur.
By Rail
The college is accessible via two main railway stations:

e Thrissur Railway Station (TCR) is a major station located about 9-14
km from the college. Public transport like buses, auto-rickshaws, and
taxis are readily available from here.

e Mulangunnathukavu Railway Station (MGK) is a local station that is
significantly closer, at approximately 4 km away from the campus

By Road
Thrissur is well-connected by national highways and local roads.

e From Thrissur City: The college is approximately 14 km from the
downtown area.

e Public Bus: Many KSRTC and _ private buses (e.g., those on the
Kuttippuram-Thrissur route or the Thirumudikkunnu - Medical College
Thrissur route) run to the college and surrounding areas like
Mundoor.

e Driving: The college is accessible via the Kodungallur - Shornur
Road. Use a maps service like Google Maps for precise driving
directions from your location.

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Established in 1951, Government Medical College Thiruvananthapuram
(GMCT) is Kerala's oldest medical institution and was inaugurated by
India’s first Prime Minister, Jawaharlal Nehru. The college's history began
in 1948 when the Travancore government sanctioned a medical scheme
and appointed Dr. C.O. Karunakaran was the first principal and "father" of
the institution. The sprawling 139-acre campus has since developed into a
premier healthcare hub, housing pioneering centers such as the Sree
Avittom Thirunal (SAT) Hospital for women and children (1952), the
Regional Cancer Centre (1958), and Kerala's first government Dental
College (1959). A major milestone occurred in 2012 when the college
performed the first cadaver organ transplant in a Kerala government
hospital.


--- Page 519 ---
The college currently offers over 86 courses across medical, paramedical,
and pharmacy disciplines. The flagship MBBS program has an annual
intake of 250 students, while postgraduate offerings include MD and MS
degrees in 23 disciplines such as General Medicine, Paediatrics, and
Orthopaedics. For advanced specialisation, the institution provides DM and
M.Ch super-specialty programs in areas like Cardiology, Neurology, and
Plastic Surgery. Allied healthcare education is extensive, featuring B.Sc.
and M.Sc. programs in Nursing, Medical Lab Technology (MLT), and
Optometry, alongside various diploma courses in Pharmacy, Dental
Mechanics, and Operation Theatre Technology.

Vision

The institution's vision is to remain a pioneering leader in medical science
and public health. It strives to be a premier centre of excellence that trains
future healthcare professionals who are dedicated to humanitarian service
and lifelong learning. The college aims to materialise a high-quality medical
education hub. supported by advanced research initiatives and
sophisticated technology.

Mission

The mission of the college is to provide world-class medical education and
drive impactful research while delivering compassionate healthcare. Key
pillars of this mission include


--- Page 520 ---
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Government Medical College,
Thiruvananthapuram (also known as Trivandrum Medical College).

e Location: Medical College Junction, Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala -
695011.

e Year of Establishment: 1951.

e Type of College: Public/Government Medical College.

e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur.

e Counselling Authority: Medical Counselling Committee (MCC) for
15% All India Quota and Office of the Commissioner for Entrance
Examinations (CEE), Kerala for 85% State Quota.

e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC).

e MBBS Intake: 250 seats annually.

e Course Duration: 5.5 years (including 4.5 years of academic study
and 1 year of compulsory rotating medical internship).

e Hospital Type: Tertiary care multi-specialty teaching hospital.

Official contact details(2025)

e Address: Trivandrum Medical College, Medical College PO,
Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala - 695011, India.

e Phone:

o Principal's Office: 0471-2444270 or 0471-2528386.
o Emergency/General Enquiry: 0471-2528300.
e Email:
o Official: principal@tmc.kerala.gov.in.
o Alternative: principalmct@gmail.com.


--- Page 521 ---
e Website: https://tmc.kerala.gov.in/
Teaching Hospital

e HospitalName: Medical College Hospital (MCh),
Thiruvananthapuram

e Phone: 0471-2528300 (Enquiry) or 0471-2443095

e Emergency Contact: 0471-2528300 (MCH Casualty) or
047 1-2528327 (SAT Casualty)

e Hospital Website: https://tmc.kerala.gov.in/

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: Approximately 3,250+ beds (including MCH
and specialized units like SAT Hospital).

e Total ICU Beds: Over 150+ specialized ICU beds, recently expanded
with a new Multi-Specialty Block (MSB) featuring 102 ICU beds with
ventilator facilities.

e Total Operation Theatres: Over 24 major theatres, including 6
modular OTs in the super-specialty block and 14 OTs in the newly
inaugurated Surgical/OT block.

e Total Outpatients: Manages an average of 6,000+ daily
consultations, totaling approximately 7.5 million outpatient visits
annually.

e Emergency Services: Operated 24/7 as a National Centre of
Excellence for emergency medicine and trauma care, featuring a
scientific triage system, stroke hotlines, and chest pain clinics.


--- Page 522 ---
e Hospital Accreditation: Affiliated hospital units are NMC recognized
for medical training; the Emergency Medicine department is a
federally recognized Centre of Excellence.

e Clinical Exposure: Extremely high clinical volume with over 80,000
annual admissions and an average of 55 major surgeries per day,
providing students with hands-on experience in complex trauma,
organ transplants, and maternal care.

MBBS (Course) — Core Details
Total Course Duration: 5.5 years (comprising 4.5 years of academic study
and 1 year of mandatory rotating internship).
Total Annual Intake:250 Seats
e State Quota (85%): 213 Seats
e All India Quota (15%): 37 Seats
Assessment / exam format:The assessment format for the MBBS
program at Government Medical College, Thiruvananthapuram, follows the
Competency-Based Medical Education (CBME) guidelines mandated by
the National Medical Commission (NMC) and implemented by the Kerala
University of Health Sciences (KUHS).

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Qualify NEET-UG 2026

e Appear for the NEET-UG exam and secure the required qualifying

marks.


--- Page 524 ---
e Ensure you have 50% marks in Physics, Chemistry, and Biology in
12th grade (40% for SC/ST/OBC).
2. Register for Counselling
e State Quota (85%): Register online via the CEE Kerala (KEAM)
portal.
e All India Quota (15%): Register via the MCC website.
3. Option Entry (Choice Filling)
e Log in to the portal during the "Option Entry" window.
e Select Government Medical College, Thiruvananthapuram as your
first preference.
e Lock your choices before the deadline.
4. Seat Allotment
e Check the allotment results on the portal.
e lf selected, download your Allotment Memo (Seat Allotment Letter).
5. Reporting & Document Verification
e Visit the college office in person with original documents:
o NEET Scorecard & Allotment Memo.
o 10th & 12th Certificates.
o Transfer (TC) & Conduct Certificates.
o Nativity & Community Certificates.
6. Fee Payment & Admission
e Pay the annual tuition fee (approx. %23,000-%32,000) and
hostel/other fees.
e Complete the medical fitness check and sign the required bond to
officially join the course.
