Academic Infrastructure
e Academic Block: A dedicated building that houses the college's
administrative offices, various departments, and lecture halls.
e Central Library: Located in the administrative wing, it contains over
11,000 books, academic journals, and a Learning Resource Center
(LRC) equipped with internet-enabled computers for digital research.


--- Page 551 ---
e Lecture Halls & Auditoriums: The campus features several major

venues for academic events and training:
o C.O. Karunakaran Memorial Hall.
o Silver Jubilee Auditorium.
o “Old Auditorium”.

e Multi-Disciplinary Research Unit (MRU): An ICMR-supported platform
that includes viral research labs, diagnostic facilities, and a Zebra fish
research facility, the first of its kind in Kerala.

e Departmental Laboratories: Every academic department, such as
Anatomy, Biochemistry, and Microbiology, is equipped with
specialized labs for student training.

e Anatomy Department: Features a premier center for anatomical
education with a dissection-based teaching focus and a cadaver
embalming facility.

e Animal House & Central Workshop: Dedicated facilities for medical
research and maintenance of advanced medical equipment.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Community Events: The Mega Pinkathon, a major health awareness
initiative, was inaugurated by the Chief Minister on January 8, 2026.

e Specialized Centers: Establishment of a Breast Milk Bank, a Skin
Bank, and a Urodynamic Study Center.

e National Ranking: Ranked #42 in India (NIRF 2024) and #6 among
government medical colleges nationally

e Pioneering Departments: First in Kerala to establish specialized
wings for Medical Genetics, Fetal Medicine, and Geriatrics.


--- Page 552 ---
Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure
ICU Beds & Operation Theatres

e Total Capacity: The main hospital and specialty blocks
combined offer over 3,250 beds.

e ICU Infrastructure:

o The Multi-Specialty Block (MSB) features 102 ICU beds
equipped with ventilators and 44 high-care beds.
o The Super Specialty Block (SSB) includes 40 ICU beds
and 25 high-care beds.
o A newly integrated Operation Theatre (OT) block adds 16
intensive care units.
Patient Inflow (OPD/IPD)

e Outpatient Department (OPD):. The hospital manages a
staggering 7.5 million outpatient consultations annually,
averaging over 5,600 visits per day.

e Inpatient Department (IPD): Approximately 80,000 patients are
admitted each year, with a consistent bed occupancy rate of
90-95%.

Specialty & Super-Specialty Departments

e Specialties: Includes 22 core disciplines such as General
Medicine, General Surgery, Orthopedics, Pediatrics, and
Obstetrics & Gynecology.

e Super-Specialties: Advanced departments include Cardiology,
Neurology, Nephrology, Gastroenterology, Urology,
Neurosurgery, and Cardiovascular & Thoracic Surgery.

e Centers of Excellence: Designated as a Center of Excellence
for Rare Diseases (SAT Hospital) and Emergency Medicine.


--- Page 553 ---
Blood Bank, Emergency & Trauma Care

e Blood Bank: A central Medical College Hospital Blood Bank
provides 24/7 services, supporting major procedures like organ
transplants and trauma cases.

e Emergency Medicine: Recently upgraded to a National Centre
of Excellence, this department provides rapid triage,
stabilization, and life-saving treatment for acute injuries.

e Trauma Care: A dedicated Trauma Care Division (built for ¥33
crore) includes its own OTs, ICU, and advanced imaging
(CT/MRI) to handle severe multi-trauma cases.

Campus Life
Sports & Recreation
The large campus grounds facilitate various sports and recreational
activities:
e Outdoor Sports: Facilities for cricket, football, hockey, basketball, and
volleyball are available, along with a 400-meter track.
e Indoor Games: Provisions for indoor games like table tennis and
badminton are also available.
Cultural & Academic Events
e Clubs and Societies: Active clubs include those for dance, music,
literature, quiz, and more, offering continuous engagement
opportunities.
Hostel & Mess Facilities


--- Page 554 ---
e Availability: Hostels are available for both male and female students,
with some located within the campus and others nearby.

e Amenities: Basic facilities include a 24/7 water and electricity supply,
study rooms, common TV halls, and a library or reading room. Wi-Fi
is available in common areas or can be arranged upon request in
some blocks.

e The mess facilities are run and managed by student representatives,
which helps maintain quality and affordability.

Safety & Support Systems

e Anti-Ragging Cell: A robust anti-ragging mechanism is in place,
featuring a committee of faculty and student representatives that
conducts regular vigil rounds in hostels and canteens.

e Mental Health Support: A dedicated Counseling Cell operates in
coordination with the Department of Psychiatry to provide
psychological support to students. Awareness programs on mental
health are regularly organized.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Placement Assistance: As a government medical institution, there are
no formal campus placements for MBBS graduates. Most students
utilize the internship year to prepare for NEET PG or pursue roles in
government health services or private hospitals independently.

e Post-Graduate Success: Graduates often find employment at
prestigious institutions like AIIMS, or private chains such as Apollo
and Aster, due to the recognized quality of training at GMC


--- Page 555 ---
Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures

As of 2026, the stipend for medical trainees at Government Medical
College (GMC), Thiruvananthapuram, is determined by the Kerala State
Government

e MBBS Interns (House Surgeons): ¥27,300 per month. Some records
indicate a base of €25,000 with additional increments or variations
depending on the specific posting.

e Postgraduate Residents (MD/MS):

o 1st Year: 57,876 per month.

o 2nd Year: $58,968 per month.

o 3rd Year: 60,060 per month.
College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A high-level committee comprising the
Principal, senior faculty, and local police representatives monitors the
campus.Students can report incidents via the NMC Anti-Ragging
Portal or the 24/7 National Anti-Ragging Helpline (1800-180-5522).

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles cases of
gender-based discrimination or sexual harassment, ensuring a safe
environment for female students and staff.

Student Review


--- Page 556 ---
Students consistently rate the clinical training as the college's
greatest strength, citing the massive daily patient volume as "unmatched"
for hands-on learning.The teaching staff are respected as top-tier clinicians
who provide high-quality medical education, though the curriculum is
described as extremely "hectic" and "rigorous."The student-run mess is a
major highlight, frequently praised for serving delicious, hygienic, and very
affordable Kerala-style meals.Life outside academics is active, with
high-energy festivals like "Euphoria" and "Medex" fostering strong bonds
between seniors and juniors.Students appreciate safety features like the
"Sky Walk" bridge, which allows secure travel between the hostel and
hospital during late-night duties.

Overall:GMC Thiruvananthapuram offers an unparalleled clinical education
with exceptional hands-on training and affordable, high-quality food, though
students must navigate a grueling workload and basic, often congested
hostel facilities.

Parent Review

GMC Thiruvananthapuram as the pinnacle of medical education in Kerala.
Graduating from here is seen as a guarantee of high clinical competence
and provides a significant advantage for future PG entrance exams and
career placements.The extremely low government fee structure is a major
highlight for parents, offering a world-class education at a fraction of the
cost of private medical colleges.There is high satisfaction with safety
measures like the "Sky Walk" bridge and improved CCTV surveillance,
which provide peace of mind for parents of students working late-night
clinical rotations.While the food quality is praised, parents frequently note


--- Page 557 ---
that hostel accommodation is "basic" and "congested." Many wish for more
modernized living facilities and fewer students per room in the older blocks.
Overall:GMC Thiruvananthapuram as the pinnacle of medical prestige and
financial value for its elite clinical training and 2026 safety upgrades, even
while acknowledging the extreme physical strain and basic living conditions
their children must endure.

super-specialty) training.

Way to reach

e Bus: Numerous Kerala State Road Transport Corporation (KSRTC)
buses operate between the Thiruvananthapuram Central Bus Station
(Thampanoor) and the Medical College area, as well as from other
city points like Pattom.

e Train: The nearest major railway station is Thiruvananthapuram
Central (TVC). From the station, you can take a taxi, auto-rickshaw,
or bus to the Medical College campus (approx. 6-7 km distance).

e Air: The nearest airport is Thiruvananthapuram International Airport
(TRV). A taxi ride from the airport to the college takes around 6
minutes and is the fastest option.

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Government Medical College (GMC), Wayanad, is a newly established
government medical institution located in Mananthavady, Wayanad district,
Kerala. It is affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur. The college was founded to enhance medical education and
healthcare access in the hilly and tribal-majority region of Wayanad,
fulfilling a long-standing need for such an institution in the district. The
establishment of a Government Medical College in Wayanad has been a
significant public and political goal for many years. The project gained final
momentum in 2025.
Vision and Mission
To be recognized as a leading institution for excellence in medical
education and research, fostering intellectual and socially committed
healthcare professionals.To provide high-quality, professional medical
education with a global outlook.


--- Page 567 ---
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Government Medical College, Wayanad
(Mananthavady)

e Location: Mananthavady, Wayanad District, Kerala - 670645

e Year of Establishment: 2025 (Established by converting the existing
Wayanad District Hospital)

e Type of College: Government / Public

e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur

e Counselling Authority: Commissioner of Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala

e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC)

e MBBS Intake: 50 students per year (as of the 2025 approval)

e Course Duration: 5.5 years (4.5 years of curriculum + 1 year of
rotating internship)

e Hospital Type: Teaching Hospital (formerly District Hospital,
Mananthavady) with a capacity of approximately 300 beds.

Official contact details(2025)

Kerala - 670645.

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)
e Total Hospital Beds: Approximately 500 beds.


--- Page 569 ---
e Total ICU Beds: The facility includes a specialized Pediatric ICU and

Specific total ICU bed count for the entire facility is currently being
expanded under the medical college upgrade).

e Total Operation Theatres: The facility is designed to house
approximately 10 operation theatres as part of its multi-phase
upgrade into a teaching hospital.

e Total Outpatients: The hospital handles a high volume of patients,
serving as the primary government healthcare hub for the district,
including specialized clinics for sickle cell anemia.

e Emergency Services: 24/7 Casualty and Emergency department
available. Includes a blood bank, emergency room, and ambulance
services.

e Hospital Accreditation: The institution is working toward National
Quality Assurance Standards (NQAS) and follows state healthcare
quality protocols.

e Clinical Exposure: Students receive extensive clinical exposure to a
wide variety of cases, including tropical medicine, tribal health
challenges, and maternal care, alongside specialized services like the
dedicated Hemoglobinopathy Research and Care Centre.

MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Duration: 5.5 years (4.5 years of academic study + 1 year of
compulsory rotating medical internship).

e Annual Intake: 50 seats.


--- Page 570 ---
e Admission Process: Admission is based on the rank secured in the
National Eligibility cum Entrance Test (NEET-UG) exam.

e All India Quota (AIQ): 15% of the seats are filled through central
counseling by the Medical Counselling Committee (MCC).

e State Quota: The remaining 85% of seats are filled through
state-level counseling conducted by the Commissioner for Entrance
Examinations (CEE), Kerala.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
Phase 1: Eligibility & Registration

1. NEET UG Qualification: You must appear for and qualify the NEET
UG 2026 exam conducted by the NTA.

2. KEAM Registration: Even though admission is via NEET, you must
register on the official CEE Kerala website.

3. Score Submission: Once NEET results are declared (usually June),
you must log back into the CEE portal to submit your NEET roll
number and score.

Phase 2: Centralized Allotment Process (CAP)

The allotment is divided into two main quotas:

e 85% State Quota: Managed by CEE Kerala for students with Kerala
nativity.

e 15% All India Quota (AlQ): Managed by the Medical Counselling
Committee (MCC) for students from all over India.

The Step-by-Step Allotment:

e Option Entry: You will be given a window to "fill choices." You must
select Government Medical College, Wayanad and place it in your
order of preference.

e Trial & First Allotment: CEE will release a trial allotment followed by
the first official list.

e Fee Payment: If allotted a seat, you must pay the required tuition fee
(approx. %31,715) to CEE Kerala via online payment or designated
post offices to "freeze" your seat.


--- Page 572 ---
Phase 3: Physical Reporting & Verification
After the allotment and fee payment, you must physically report to the GMC
Wayanad campus in Mananthavady.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: The campus features modern, air-conditioned "smart"
classrooms equipped with advanced audio-visual (AV) aids to
facilitate interactive learning.


--- Page 576 ---
e Laboratories: Department-specific laboratories are fully functional for
foundational subjects, including Anatomy, Physiology, and
Biochemistry.

e Dissection Hall: A dedicated dissection hall and demonstration rooms
are available for practical anatomical studies.

e Central Library: The institution houses a digital and physical library
with a_ significant collection of medical textbooks, international
journals, and high-speed Wi-Fi for research.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Historic Inaugural Batch: The college successfully admitted its first
batch of 50 MBBS students in October 2025. Notably, three Wayanad
natives, including a student from the Scheduled Tribe community,
were among those selected for this maiden batch.

e Kerala's First Sickle Cell Unit: The college established the state's first
dedicated unit for sickle cell disease, a condition prevalent in the
regional tribal population.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The hospital currently operates with approximately 300
to 500 beds. Under the 2025-2026 expansion plan funded by KIIFB,
it is being upgraded to a 700-bed super-specialty teaching facility.

e Specialized Units: Sickle Cell Unit: A specialized center dedicated to
Sickle Cell Anemia, which is prevalent among the local tribal
population.


--- Page 577 ---
o Modern Cath Lab: Fully functional for cardiac emergencies.
o Dialysis & ICU: Includes a 24/7 Emergency Casualty
department and a dedicated ICU complex.

e Academic Space: The clinical teaching facilities are integrated into a
new 2%45 crore multipurpose block, which houses smart classrooms
and advanced labs for pre-clinical training.

e Patient Inflow: As the main referral point for over 600,000 residents,
the hospital sees an average of 1,200—1,400 outpatients daily,
ensuring a high volume of cases for student observation.

e Early Clinical Exposure (ECE): Following the NMC’s
Competency-Based Medical Education (CBME) curriculum, students
are introduced to the hospital environment in their first year. They
participate as "passive observers" in the OPD and minor OT to
understand doctor-patient communication.

Campus Life

e Sports: Facilities for outdoor games like football and volleyball are
being developed on the grounds adjacent to the hospital and
academic blocks.

e Social Impact: Given its location, students often participate in
community health camps and tribal welfare programs, which form a
significant part of their social and professional life.


--- Page 578 ---
Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Accommodation Type: Separate hostel buildings are available for
boys and girls.

e Room Details: Generally, rooms are shared by three students, with
single occupancy sometimes offered to interns at an additional cost.
Each student is provided with essential furniture, including a cot,
study table, chair, and a cupboard or wardrobe.

e Amenities: The hostels offer several modern amenities, such as Wi-Fi
connectivity in common areas and study halls, 24-hour electricity with
generator backup, and 24/7 access to purified drinking water.
Laundry services and separate gyms are also available for boys and
girls.

Safety & Support Systems

e Anti-Ragging Committee: The institution has an active Anti-Ragging
Committee and Squad to prevent and address any incidents of
ragging, with a zero-tolerance policy. Students are informed about
their rights during induction programs and can report incidents to
committee members.

e Grievance Redressal Committee: A Grievance Redressal Committee
is in place to investigate and take action on issues related to safety
and security, as well as other student concerns.


--- Page 579 ---
College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)

e The college has a dedicated Anti-Ragging Committee chaired by the
Principal and an Anti-Ragging Squad that conducts surprise raids,
especially in hostels.

e Institutional rules & hostel regulations: the college
prospectus/admission download pages include the institution’s rules
and hostel regulations (disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance
rules). Read the prospectus carefully before admission.

Government Medical College, Wayanad Student & Parent
Review

Student Review

The campus is praised for its calm and "ideal" environment for focused
study, set against the scenic backdrop of Wayanad.Students report "good
classrooms" and "well-equipped laboratories" in the new academic blocks.
The recently completed multipurpose block has significantly improved
administrative and classroom facilities. Being the only tertiary healthcare
center in the district ensures a steady inflow of patients, providing students
with ample opportunities to learn from real medical cases. Staff are
described as "cooperative" and "highly qualified," often providing more
personalized attention due to the initial smaller batch sizes.

Parent Review

Significantly low tuition fees compared to private medical colleges, which
allows for medical education without high financial debt.The campus is
frequently described as having a "calm and ideal environment" for learning,
which is a priority for many families.Parents report that the teaching staff
are highly qualified, approachable, and provide personalized attention due


--- Page 580 ---
to the moderate student intake.The integration with the District Hospital
provides students with essential hands-on experience through real medical
cases.

Way To Reach

e By Road: The college is located in the Mananthavady area. KSRTC
and private buses frequently operate from nearby towns like Kalpetta
(about 35 km away) to Mananthavady.

e By Train: The nearest railway station is Kozhikode (CLT). From there,
you can take a bus or taxi, which takes approximately 3 hours to
reach Mananthavady via the scenic mountain passes (Wayanad
Churam).

e By Air: The closest airport is Kozhikode (Calicut) International Airport
(CCJ). Taxis or buses are available from the airport to Wayanad, a
distance of about 100 km

FAQ Section (General)

1. When was the college established?

JUBILEE MISSION MEDICAL COLLEGE & RESEARCH
INSTITUTE (JMMCRI)
Basic College Profile
● Jubilee Mission Hospital (as hospital) established in 1952.
● Jubilee Mission Medical College established in 2003.
● Institution Type:Private Self-Financing Medical College
● Minority Status: Christian-minority institution.
● Campus:Thecollege+hospital+relatedinfrastructurearelocatedin
Thrissur city.
● Motto / ethos: “Service with Love” — emphasizes patient care
irrespective of caste/creed, with special concessions for the poor.
● Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/NRI)
● Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences, National Medical
Commission.
● Religious Affiliation: Roman Catholic.
● Recognised by National Medical Commission (NMC)
● Address:
P.B.
No.
737,
Fathima
Nagar,
Mahatma
Nagar,
Nellikunnu,Thrissur – 680005, Kerala, India
● Official Website: https://jmmcri.org/profile.html
● Contact: 91 487 246 4346, 91 487 246 4347
● Total Beds:1500 - 1600
● Total ICU Beds:300
● Total Operation Theatres: 22.
● Total Outpatients:- 13,50,000 per year.

MBBS (Course) — Core Details
● Program length: 5.5 years total (4.5 years academic + 1 year
internship) — CBME aligned.
● Annual Intake : 150 (Historically 100 MBBS seats; NMC / KUHS
approvals to increase seats reports indicate +50seatsfor2025–26
giving 150)
● Assessment
/
exam

(theory/practical/clinical), University (KUHS) professional exams
including

and
competency/OSCE style elements in line with CBME. Check the
college prospectus/university rules for exact pass marks and IA
weightage.

allied health sciences), under its allied health wing.
● Postgraduate (MD/MS) — yes, postgraduate courses (clinical /
non-clinical) are offered.
Fee Structure (2025–26, Tuition + Academic Fees)
MBBS
● For Indian students / merit-quota: ₹ 8,16,038 per annum.
● For NRI quota MBBS: ₹ 21,65,720 per annum.
● Over full 5-year course (tuition), total ~ ₹ 40.8 lakhs.
● Hostel & Mess fees: ₹46,000 -₹54,000(differentroomcategories/
years may vary).
● Special fees & Caution deposit: ₹ 73,708
Note: Fees may change next academic year
Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Qualify Entrance Exam
● You must appear in and qualify NEET‑UG (with required
percentile/marks).


--- Page 589 ---
● Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English)must
meet eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40%
for reserved (SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.
2. Register for State-Level Counselling
● AdmissionsinKerala(statequota/self-financing/management
/ minority / NRI) for MBBS at JMMCRI are processed via
Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE)
through centralized counselling/web-based allotment.
● YouneedtoregisterontheofficialCEEportal,submitrequired
credentials (NEET result,academicrecords,domicile/caste/
reservation proofs if applicable).
3. Option Filling / Choice Preference
● Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) +
colleges (e.g.JMMCRI)+quotaoptions(state-quota,minority,
NRI) — as per your eligibility & preference.
● Lockyourchoicesbeforethedeadline.Option-fillingandlocking
is mandatory to participate in seat allotment.
4. Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority
● Based on your NEET rank, reservationcategory,preferences,
and seat availability, the counselling authority does seat
allotment.
● If a seat is allotted to you at JMMCRI, you get an allotment
memo / letter.
5. Reporting to College & Document Verification
● Report to JMMCRI within deadline with original certificates:
NEET scorecard, 10th/12thmarksheets&passingcertificates,


--- Page 590 ---
transfer/conductcertificate,domicile/caste/reservationproof
(if applicable), ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
● Paytherequiredtuitionfee(andotherfeeslikeadmissionfee,
etc.) to confirm admission.
6. Join the Course
● Once verification and fee payment is done — youjoinMBBS
1st year at JMMCRI with all admitted students.

infrastructure.

Internship placement quality — quick summary
● In-house placement for interns isstrong:final-yearstudentsand
freshgraduatesnormallygettheirinternshippostinginsidetheparent
teachinghospital(themandatory12-monthrotatoryinternshipoccurs


--- Page 614 ---
attheteachinghospital).Thatgivesdirectaccesstowards,OT,ICU
and specialty clinics.
● After internship many graduates either take jobs at the parent

listings indicate a high placement/PG continuation rate but exact
percentvariesbyyearandcourse;verifywiththecollege’splacement
office or alumni groups.
Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures
The college publishes stipend declarations. Two common components
appear in official/administrative documents:
● MBBS interns (typical / recent figures):
○ State Government stipend(where applicable):₹25,000/
month(listed in the college stipend declaration table).
○ College stipend / top-up:₹15,000 / monthshown inthe
college’s stipend table (financial year 2024–25 document).
○ Practically, thetake-homecan differ depending onwhether the
intern is paid by the state scheme, by the college (or both), and
on the financial year / policy updates — always check the
current academic year declaration.
● PG students / Residents (typical recent figures):
○ 1st year MD/MS:~₹53,000 / month(some official tablesand
college listings show ~₹53k–55k for 1st–3rd year PGs).


--- Page 615 ---
○ Senior PG / DM figures are higher per published tables. Exact
numbers are published annually by the institution/health
department.

● Anti-ragging committee / detailed contacts: JMMCRIhas a listed
Anti-Ragging Committee with names & phone numbers (published on
their site) — the college enforces anti-ragging policies per Supreme
Court / UGC / state rules.
● Institutional rules & hostel regulations: the college
prospectus/admission download pages include the institution’s rules
and hostel regulations (disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance
rules). Read the prospectus carefully before admission.
Jubilee Mission Medical College – Student & Parent
Review
Student Review
Students appreciate the strong academics, excellent patient exposure, and
supportivefacultyatJubileeMissionMedicalCollege.Thebusyteachinghospital
provides hands-on learning opportunities and helps build clinical confidence.
However,studentsalsomentionthatthecampusiscompact,rulesarestrict,and
hostel/mess facilities are average. Campus lifeismoreacademic-focusedwith
limited cultural or recreational activities.


--- Page 616 ---
Overall: Great for academics and clinical training, moderate hostel life, and
limited campus freedom.
Parent Review
Parents value the disciplined environment, safe campus, and the institution’s
reputation for quality medical education. They appreciate the strong hospital
backingandthestructuredacademicsystem.Someparentsfeelthatthecollege
couldoffermorerecreationalspaceandamoreflexiblehostelenvironmentbut
overall believe their children receive solid medical training.
Overall:Adependableandacademicallystronginstitutionwithgoodsafetyand
discipline for students.

● Academics:⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (Excellent)
● Clinical Exposure:⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (Outstanding)
● Faculty Quality:⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (Very Good)

GetMyAdmission – Professional Review of Jubilee
Mission Medical College
At GetMyAdmission, we assess medical institutions across India based on
academics,clinicalexposure,infrastructure,andstudentsupport.JubileeMission
Medical College, Thrissur, remains one of Kerala’s respected options for both
MBBS and PG training.
Student Perspective
Students highlight:
● Excellentclinical exposuredue to the high patientinflow at the parent
hospital.
● Adisciplined academic systemwith structured postings,regular
evaluations, and supportive faculty.
● Goodacademic infrastructure, including skill labsand modern lecture
halls.
● Safe, comfortable hostelswith reliable mess facilities.
Parent Perspective
Parents appreciate:
● The hospital’sstrong reputationand service-orientedapproach.
● Asafe, well-disciplined campuswith approachableadministration.
● Reasonable fee structurecompared to similar privateinstitutions.
● Effectiveinternship training, helping students gain confidence and clinical
skills.


--- Page 618 ---
Overall Assessment
Jubilee Mission Medical College offers strong academics, robust clinical
exposure, and a disciplined campus atmosphere. With consistent educational
performance and trusted hospital support, it remains a dependable choice for
both MBBS and MD/MS aspirants in Kerala.
GMA Rating & Verdict
● GMA Overall Rating: ★★★★☆ (4.3/5)
● Academics:★★★★★

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Karuna Medical College is a self-financing medical institution located in
Vilayodi, Chittur, Palakkad, Kerala, India. Established in 2006, the college
has since graduated over TWELVE BATCHES of MBBS students, with its
alumni holding prominent positions in the medical field. The college is
affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences and is equipped with
more than 600 bedded teaching hospitals. The campus is situated in the
heart of Palakkad, offering a dynamic environment for students.
Karuna Medical College Hospital is a 600+bed facility equipped with
state-of-the-art infrastructure and staffed by a team of highly qualified and
experienced healthcare professionals. Affiliated with Karuna Institute of
Medical Sciences, the hospital is located on the Karuna Medical College
campus, ensuring seamless integration of academic and clinical training.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management /

minority / NRI) for MBBS at AIMS are processed via Commissioner


--- Page 627 ---
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE)through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste
/reservation proofs if applicable).

3. Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) +colleges
(e.g. AIMS) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your
eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4. Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e If aseat is allotted to you at AIMS, you get an allotment memo / letter.

5. Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to AIMS within deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee, etc.)
to confirm admission.

6. Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBB/st year at
AIMS with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Theatres & Halls: Features five spacious digital classrooms
equipped with modern audio-visual aids, including LED projectors,
interactive touch panels, and high-resolution documentary cameras.

e Laboratories & Skill Centres: Specialized labs for Anatomy,
Physiology, Pathology, and Microbiology. The campus also includes
advanced simulation labs and skill centers for early clinical exposure.


--- Page 632 ---
e Teaching Hospital: A 600+ bed multispecialty hospital serving as the
primary training ground for hands-on clinical experience in
departments like Cardiology, Neurology, and Nephrology.

e Examination Hall: A dedicated 900 sq. m hall with a seating capacity
for 250 students.

HOSTEL FACILITIES

e Room Sharing: Rooms are available in single and double occupancy
formats, as well as three-person sharing, all with basic furniture like
beds, tables, chairs, and wardrobes.

e Utilities: Hostels are equipped with a 24-hour electricity supply (with
generator backup) and a continuous supply of hot and cold water.
Drinking water filters are available on each floor.

e Mess & Food: Mess facilities provide healthy and varied meals,
including both vegetarian and non-vegetarian options. The mess is
often run by students under a common dividing system.

e Security: Round-the-clock security personnel and wardens ensure a
safe and disciplined environment.

Hostel Safety & Discipline

e Curfew & Roll Call: Students must return to the hostel by a
designated time (typically 7:00 PM), with daily roll calls conducted at
approximately 7:30 AM and 8:00 PM.

e Separation of Facilities: The campus features completely separate
hostels for male and female students to ensure privacy and safety.


--- Page 633 ---
Emergency & Health Support

e 24/7 Medical Care: Being attached to a 600+ bed multispecialty
hospital, students have immediate access to 24-hour emergency
and trauma care services.

e Safety Audits: In compliance with Kerala state directives, the
institution participates in periodic security, fire, and electrical
audits to maintain infrastructure safety.

Student Support Systems

e SSGP (Student Support & Guidance Programme): A mandatory
KUHS initiative that provides counseling for stress management and
academic pressure.

e Mentorship: Small student groups are assigned to faculty mentors
who track academic progress and provide personal guidance.

e Financial Aid: Access to the Vivek Medical Students’ Scholarship
(VMS) for low-income students and various state-level minority
scholarships.

e Grievance & Safety: Active Anti-Ragging Committees and a
dedicated Grievance Redressal Cell to address student complaints
quickly.

e Healthcare: 24/7 access to medical care and emergency services
through the attached teaching hospital.


--- Page 634 ---
MBBS Internship (Compulsory One-Year Rotatory
Internship)

e The internship is a mandatory 12-month clinical training students
must complete after finishing their 4.5 years of academic MBBS
studies.

e Without completing this internship, a student is not eligible to be
awarded an MBBS degree or gain full registration with the medical
council.

Karuna Medical College Student Parent Review

Student Review
Consistently rated as the strongest aspect (approx. 4.5/5). Teachers are
described as highly qualified, approachable, and helpful in clearing doubts. The
attached 600+ bed hospital provides good patient flow, ensuring students get
adequate hands-on experience during clinical postings.Facilities are considered
average. Rooms are typically shared by three students. Common complaints
include the lack of air conditioning during summer, spicy food, and shared
washrooms.Described as calm and pollution-free but relatively quiet. First-year
students often have restricted access to recreational facilities like the gym and
certain sports events.Situated in a semi-rural area (Vilayodi), it is about 6km from
the nearest town, which some students find inconvenient for shopping or
entertainment.


--- Page 635 ---
Parent Review
Parents generally express high confidence in the teaching standards. The faculty
is frequently described as dedicated, highly qualified, and supportive of student
learning.Many parents are pleased with the hands-on clinical exposure
provided by the 600+ bed teaching hospital, noting that it prepares students well
for real-world practice.The calm, pollution-free, and eco-friendly campus
environment is often cited as a positive for focused study. The separate, secure
hostels with 24/7 security also provide peace of mind to parents regarding
student safety.A common critique involves the average quality of hostel food
and amenities. Some feedback highlights that while minimum requirements are
met, the overall infrastructure may lag behind high-end private
institutions.Parents often note the remote location as a challenge. Being roughly
6km from the nearest town means limited nearby shopping or entertainment, and
public transportation can be poor.

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Kerala Medical College (KMC), Mangode, located at Cherpulasserry in
Palakkad district, Kerala, was established in 2011 with a vision to provide
high-quality medical education and comprehensive healthcare
services. Since its inception, the college has grown rapidly to become one
of the leading private medical institutions in Southern India.
Affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and
approved by the National Medical Commission (NMC), KMC Mangode
ensures that its curriculum, teaching standards, and clinical training meet
national regulatory standards. Managed by a private educational trust,
the college operates as a self-financing institution with a strong focus on
academic excellence, clinical skills, and research opportunities.
The attached multi-specialty teaching hospital is equipped with modern
diagnostic and surgical facilities, outpatient and inpatient care units, and
provides students with hands-on clinical exposure across various
specialties. The institution emphasizes professionalism, teamwork,


--- Page 641 ---
integrity, and patient-centered care, ensuring students gain both
theoretical knowledge and practical skills.
In just over a decade, Kerala Medical College has earned recognition for its
academic standards, clinical training, and quality healthcare services,
making it a preferred choice for students seeking medical education in
Kerala.

Kerala Medical College- Student & Parent Review

Student Review:

Students generally describe Kerala Medical College, Mangode as a calm
and academically focused institution suitable for serious medical study. The
teaching staff are considered approachable and supportive, and the
academic structure follows NMC guidelines with regular assessments and
Clinical postings.

Clinical exposure is moderate, with patient flow improving in higher
semesters, allowing students to gain practical experience over time. The
campus infrastructure is modern and well-maintained, and hostel facilities
are adequate with acceptable mess services. Campus life is quiet, with
limited but meaningful cultural and extracurricular activities. Overall,
students view KMC Mangode as a good option among private medical
colleges in Kerala for a disciplined and study-oriented environment.

Overall :Students find Kerala Medical College, Mangode to be a
disciplined, academically focused institution with supportive faculty and
decent infrastructure. Clinical exposure improves over time, making it a
satisfactory choice among private medical colleges in Kerala.


--- Page 652 ---
Parent review:
Parents generally regard Kerala Medical College, Mangode as a safe,
disciplined, and academically reliable institution for medical education.
They appreciate the structured curriculum, qualified faculty, and regular
academic monitoring that help ensure consistent student progress. The
presence of an attached teaching hospital reassures parents about their
child’s clinical training and practical exposure.
They also value the secure campus environment, with hostel supervision,
controlled access, and basic safety measures in place. Hostel and mess
facilities are considered satisfactory, providing a comfortable living
environment away from home. Although the fee structure is higher than
government colleges, many parents feel it is justified by the infrastructure,
teaching standards, and overall academic stability offered by the institution.
Overall : Parents consider Kerala Medical College, Mangode a safe and

Medical College History & Introduction
KMCT Medical College was established in the year 2008 with an intake of
100 MBBS seats approved by the Medical Council of India. The College is
affiliated with Kerala University of Health Sciences. The Central
Government had accorded recognition for the MBBS course in the year
2013. Postgraduate courses were started in the academic year 2015-16 in
Orthopaedics & Pharmacology and in the academic year 2020-21
postgraduate courses were started in other specialities (Microbiology,
Community Medicine, General Medicine, General Surgery, Obstetrics &
Gynaecology, Paediatrics, ENT, Ophthalmology, Dermatology,
Anaesthesiology, Psychiatry, Radiology & Pulmonary Medicine). From the
academic year 2024-25, the intake of students in MBBS course was
increased from 150 to 250 by the approval of Central Government.The
Medical College is attached to KMCT Medical College Hospital, which is a
tertiary level multispecialty hospital with more than 1200 beds.
The vision of the college is to be one among the top medical institutions in
the world in every aspect of healthcare, education and research. And its
mission is to provide ethical, cost effective and state of the art healthcare
services to remedy illness and improve patient care through compassionate
healing and advanced research;Create holistic development opportunities


--- Page 660 ---
for students through interdisciplinary comprehensive and_ progressive
academic programs;Cultivate an environment which is collaborative, open
to exchange of ideas and innovative in approach.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at SNIMS are processed via Commissioner
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference


--- Page 663 ---
e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. KMCT) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per
your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e If a seat is allotted to you at KMCT, you get an allotment memo /
letter.

5.Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to KMCTwithin deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.

6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at KMCT with all admitted students.

Infrastructure & Facilities
Central Library
e The central library is housed in a 2400 sqm area with air-conditioning
and is well protected with fire alarms and other safety measures with


--- Page 678 ---
a seating capacity for 150 students. The library comprises more than
12250 books.

e All major medical journals and e-journals are subscribed in the library
for the students.

e Along with this, each department has its own small library specifically
for that particular discipline.

e The Library is fully automated with software developed in-house with
the OPAC (KOHA) facility.

e Reprographic Facility. Internet Facility. Database Search through
Ebsco Medline. Document Delivery Service. Provision for Separate
Reading rooms for students and faculty members.

e Open for extended hours to support study and research.

e Wi-Fi access and separate reading rooms.

Lecture Halls & Classrooms

The college has a total of six lecture halls used by different departments.
Among the lecture halls, four of them can accommodate more than 180
students each and one can accommodate more than 200 students. They
are spacious, air-conditioned and fitted with all modern amenities like
microphones and overhead projectors.

Museums

The college has six museums in the campus for the Preclinical and
Paraclinical departments of Anatomy, Forensic Medicine, Community
Medicine, Pharmacology, Microbiology and Pathology. A wide range of
specimens, models, charts etc., are exhibited in these museums enabling
the students to get first-hand information about the subjects that they are
dealing with.


--- Page 679 ---
Lab
Pre Clinical and Para Clinical departments have their own practical labs
and research labs with a facility to seat more than 90 students at a time.
Demonstration Rooms
Most departments have dedicated demonstration rooms (70-125
seating), fitted with overhead projectors and audio-visual aids to
enhance learning.
Recreation
The Campus has a number of options for recreation for the students. There
are facilities to play games like Football, Volley Ball, Table Tennis,
Badminton to take away their stress after classes and examinations. In
addition to this, the College conducts regular art festivals, popular music
bands are also invited to the campus.
Cafeteria
There are four canteens in the Medical College. Two canteens in the
campus, one in the hospital and the fourth one inside the College. A
variety of snacks, savouries, meals and beverages are available here. It is
our commitment to give you the best.
Campus Safety & Security
e Anti-Ragging & DisciplineThe college has a formal Anti-Ragging
Committee and Squad to enforce strict anti-ragging rules and support
affected students.Ragging is strictly prohibited on campus and in
hostels, and students are required to submit anti-ragging
undertakings.Complaints can be made to the committee or through
dedicated helplines.


--- Page 680 ---
e Women's Cell: A fully functional unit focused on the empowerment
and safety of female students and employees, providing guidance
and grievance support.

e Mental Health Counselling: An expert team is available to help
students manage academic and personal pressures in a safe,
confidential environment.

e 24/7 Monitoring: KMCT Medical College maintains around-the-clock
security personnel and CCTV surveillance to monitor entry points and
common areas.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e KMCT Medical College provides separate hostel facilities for boys
and girls within or near the campus, ensuring a safe and comfortable
stay for students.

e Hostels are supervised by wardens and support staff, with controlled
entry timings and basic security measures in place.

e Rooms are adequately furnished and include essential amenities
such as beds, study tables, cupboards, and common washroom
facilities.

e The hostel mess serves regular meals with a focus on hygiene and
nutritional balance.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e KMCT Medical College has been Accredited with A in the first cycle

of accreditation by NAAC.


--- Page 681 ---
e The college regularly conducts academic conferences, CME
programs, workshops, seminars, and guest lectures across various
medical specialties.

e Cultural festivals, sports meets, and intercollegiate competitions are
also organized, encouraging holistic student development.

e The college promotes undergraduate and postgraduate research
activities through ICMR projects, departmental research programs,
and conference presentations

e Faculty and students publish research articles in indexed national and
international journals, supporting a growing research culture within
the institution.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The main KMCT Medical College Hospital is a
tertiary-level multi-specialty facility with 1,200 beds (including 200
ICU beds) spread across 7 buildings.

e High Patient Inflow: Being a tertiary care center located ~25km from
the main city, it caters to a massive rural and semi-urban population,
ensuring a diverse case mix for students.

e Specialized Units: The hospital features a NABH-accredited Super
Specialty Centre offering 48 fields of specialization, including
Cardiology (with Cath Lab), Neurology, Nephrology (24/7 Dialysis),
and Urology.

e Skill Lab: A state-of-the-art 360° Skill Lab allows students to practice
complex procedures (like intubation, catheterization, and suturing) on
high-fidelity simulators before performing them on patients.


--- Page 682 ---
MBBS Internship (Compulsory One-Year Rotatory Internship)

e The internship is a mandatory 12-month clinical training students
must complete after finishing their 4.5 years of academic MBBS
studies.

e Without completing this internship, a student is not eligible to be
awarded an MBBS degree or gain full registration with the medical

College rules & discipline

Institutional rules & hostel regulations : the college prospectus/admission
download pages include the institution’s rules and hostel regulations
(disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance rules). Read the prospectus
carefully before admission.

KMCT Student & Parent Review

Student Review

Students at KMCT Medical College appreciate the steady clinical exposure
provided by the attached teaching hospital, which ensures consistent
patient inflow across major departments. The wide range of specialties
allows students to gain practical experience during clinical postings and
internships. Faculty members are generally regarded as supportive and
approachable, particularly in guiding students through case discussions
and exam preparation. The campus environment is calm and disciplined,
helping students maintain academic focus. Hostel facilities are comfortable
with basic amenities, and the mess food is considered satisfactory by most
students. Some students feel the academic schedule can be demanding,
but they acknowledge that it strengthens clinical skills and exam readiness.


--- Page 683 ---
Overall, KMCT is viewed as a reliable private medical college in Kerala
offering balanced academics, practical training, and a supportive learning
atmosphere.

Overall : Students view KMCT Medical College as a dependable institution
with steady clinical exposure and a structured academic system.They
appreciate the supportive faculty, disciplined campus atmosphere, and
balanced focus on theory and practical training.

Parent Review

Parents generally express satisfaction with KMCT Medical College,
appreciating its structured academic system and disciplined campus
environment. They value the affiliation with Kerala University of Health
Sciences and the presence of a functioning teaching hospital, which
ensures consistent clinical exposure and practical learning opportunities.
Many parents feel reassured by the availability of experienced faculty
members who guide students academically and professionally. The
campus safety measures, hostel supervision, and basic amenities are also
seen as positive aspects contributing to student well-being.

Some parents note that the academic schedule can be rigorous, but they
recognize that this intensity helps students build strong clinical knowledge
and exam preparedness. Communication from the administration and
accessibility of hospital facilities further add to their confidence. Overall,
parents consider KMCT a dependable private medical college in Kerala
that offers balanced academics, practical training, and a secure
environment for medical education.


--- Page 684 ---
Overall: Parents consider KMCT Medical College a dependable institution
with structured academics and adequate clinical training. They appreciate
the safe campus environment, disciplined system, and supportive faculty
guidance for their children.

By Train:

Station, around 25-30 km away. From the station, students can take
buses, taxis, or auto-rickshaws to reach the college.

By Road:

KMCT Medical College is located at Manassery, Mukkam, Kozhikode

district. Regular KSRTC and private buses operate from Kozhikode city to


--- Page 687 ---

MMC
LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Malabar Medical College Hospital & Research Centre was established in
the year 2010 as the first private medical college in Kerala to have 150
seats at inception. After a decade of dedicated and untiring commitment for
grooming. the. best kind of medical professionals and creating many top
ranks for MBBS examinations, the institution is recognized as the first kind
of it in entire Kerala and has now been elevated to the status of a 200
seated private medical college. The necessary permissions from
Government of Kerala, National Medical Commission and Kerala University
of Health Sciences are all obtained for facilitating the additional intake
effective from academic year 2022 -23.
Malabar Medical College & Research Centre is managed by Sree Anjaneya
Medical Trust with the mission of providing upper crust medical education
and quality health care at affordable cost. The medical college was


--- Page 695 ---
established in the year 2010 and is affiliated to Kerala University of Health
Sciences.

It would be not exaggerating if we say that Malabar Medical College stands
among the top private medical colleges of the state when the past results of
the MBBS students in their university examinations and _ overall
performance of the institution in various activities including cultural, sports,
research of the students and faculties speaks volumes about the institution.
Few achievements worth mentioning in the University examinations are
given below.As one of the leading institutions offering Medical UG PG
Courses in Kerala, MMC continues to set high academic standards through
its comprehensive programs and consistent results.

Mission

Malabar Medical College Hospital & Research Centre is committed to
provide excellent infrastructure, renowned faculty and learning environment
to nurture new medical professionals with moral values and ethics with an
attitude to serve the community selflessly and with compassion.

The institution is obligated to house innovative medical research activity to
unfold the scientific truth beneficial for the human race.

Vision

Malabar Medical College Hospital & Research Centre is accomplished to
be recognized as an institution of eminence in India for providing excellent
medical education, medical care and medical research.


--- Page 696 ---

e Name of Institution: Malabar Medical College Hospital & Research

MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Total Duration: 5.5 years, consisting of 4.5 years of academic study
and a 1-year mandatory rotatory internship.

e Intake Capacity: 250 seats annually (increased from 200 starting in
the 2025-2026 academic year).

Internal Assessment (College Level):

e Continuous Evaluation: Regular unit tests, practical records, and
model exams.

e Eligibility: You must score at least 50% in Internals to sit for the final
University exams.

University Exams (End of Year)

e Theory: Written papers consisting of structured essays, short notes,
and MCQs.

e Practical/Clinical: | Real-world patient cases, OSCE/OSPE
(station-based tasks), and spotting.

e Viva Voce: Face-to-face oral examination with internal and external
examiners.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. Qualify NEET-UG: All candidates must appear for and secure the
minimum qualifying percentile in the NEET-UG entrance examination
conducted by the NTA.

2. State Registration: Candidates must register online on the official
Commissioner for Entrance Examinations (CEE), Kerala portal. This
applies to both Keralite (State Merit) and Non-Keralite
(Management/NRI) categories.

3. Option Registration (Choice Filling): During the counseling rounds,
log into the CEE candidate portal to select Malabar Medical College
as your preferred institution and arrange it in your priority list.

4. Seat Allotment: CEE Kerala releases the allotment list based on your
NEET rank, category, and preferences.

5. Fee Remittance: If allotted a seat, you must pay the first-year tuition
fee as directed by the CEE to confirm your acceptance.

6. Reporting to College: Visit the Malabar Medical College campus in
person with your Allotment Memo and original documents for final
verification and joining.

MBBS Seat Distribution (2025)
e Total Intake: 250 Seats
e Government/State Merit Quota (50%): 125 Seats
These are filled based on the Kerala State Rank list and include
reservations for various categories (SC, ST, SEBC, etc.).

e Management Quota (35%): 87-88 Seats

Open to candidates on the Kerala State merit list, typically at a
higher tuition fee than government seats.


--- Page 701 ---
e NRI Quota (15%): 37-38 Seats
Reserved for children/dependents of Non-Resident Indians;
these seats require specific NRI documentation during CEE
Kerala registration.

Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Theatres: The campus includes 6 gallery-type lecture halls.
Five are located in the medical college (four seating 180 and one
seating 350) and one in the hospital seating 200. These are equipped
with centralised air-conditioning, smart boards, and audio-visual aids.
e Central Library: A three-story facility housing approximately 11,500
books and periodicals. It features:
o A reading room for 140 students.
o A Digital Library with 40 internet-connected PCs.
o Online access to over 300 medical journals, 100 e-books, and
the MEDLINE Complete database.
o Operational hours: 8 AM to 12 AM (midnight).
e Examination Halls: Two dedicated examination halls covering 1,200
square metres, capable of accommodating up to 1,000 students.
e Specialised Labs: Each department has its own laboratory. Notable
ones include:
o Anatomy: Spacious dissection hall with a cadaver storage room
and an LCD projector for previews.
o Microbiology: Features a diagnostic wing and an academic wing
with practical halls and a dedicated museum.


--- Page 714 ---
o Hospital Labs: Modern facilities for Clinical Pathology,
Haematology, Biochemistry, and Microbiology.
Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Academic Rankings: The institution was ranked 9th among 28
medical colleges in Kerala (both government and private) based on
university examination results.

e Sports Excellence: The college held the KUHS University Sports
Championship for three consecutive years (2014-2017) and was the
Overall Runner Up in the 2022-2023 State Sports Meet.

e SIRO Certification: In 2022, the Sree Anjaneya Medical Trust
received DSIR (Department of Scientific and Industrial Research)
certification, officially becoming a Scientific and Industrial Research
Organization (SIRO).

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A 890-bed multispecialty teaching hospital serving the
urban and rural populations of North Malabar.

e Operating Theatres: Equipped with 10 major and 2 minor operating
theatres designed for diverse surgical procedures.

e Specialised Units:

o Cardiac Sciences: Features an ultramodern Cath Lab (the first
of its kind in North Kerala) and a 12-bed intensive care unit.

o Emergency Medicine: A 25-bed department with cardiac
monitoring, a mobile ICU, and 24/7 casualty services.

o Critical Care: Provides high-flow nasal oxygen, invasive
mechanical ventilation, and renal replacement therapy.


--- Page 715 ---
o Diagnostics: Includes advanced imaging such as a 1.5 Tesla
MRI, 64-slice CT scan, and a fully automated central laboratory.

e Patient Footfall: Students gain hands-on experience with a daily OPD
footfall of over 1,140 patients, offering a broad spectrum of clinical
cases.

e Early Clinical Exposure: The Malabar Medical College Hospital
follows the NMC-approved CBME (Competency-Based Medical
Education) curriculum, introducing clinical posting in wards starting
from the para-clinical stage (3rd semester).

e Simulation & Skills Lab: Features a dedicated Skill Lab with medical
manikins for practicing CPR, IV access, and life support (BLS/ACLS)
before treating real patients.

Campus Life

e REVEL: The massive annual arts and cultural fest where students
compete in music, dance, and theater.

e Sports Meet: A major highlight, given MMC's history as a KUHS
University Sports Champion. Expect intense inter-batch competitions.

e Celebrations: The campus goes all out for festivals like Onam (with
massive Pookalams and Sadhyas), Christmas, and Holi

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e We have separate hostel facilities for boys and girls for students
who are staying and continuing their studies on campus .

e The hostel can accommodate 900 students at present.

e Our well maintained Hostel mess provides quality food served for
the Hostel Inmates.


--- Page 716 ---
e Atatime, our mess dining hall can serve food for 350 students.

e There is a gym functional attached to the hostel with all modern
physical fitness work out facilities.

Safety & Support Systems

e Campus Surveillance: The institution maintains 24/7 security with
integrated CCTV monitoring and perimeter security to ensure a safe
environment for students and staff.

e Hostel Security: Residential areas have dedicated guards and strict
entry/exit protocols, including a 7:00 PM curfew for all inmates.

e Anti-Ragging Infrastructure: MMC strictly enforces a zero-tolerance
policy against ragging.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

1. Anti-ragging committee / detailed contacts: mmc has a listed
Anti-Ragging Committee with names & phone numbers (published on
their site) — the college enforces anti-ragging policies per Supreme
Court / UGC / state rules.

2. Institutional rules & hostel regulations: the college
prospectus/admission download pages include the institution’s rules
and hostel regulations (disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance
rules). Read the prospectus carefully before admission.

Student Reviews

e The hospital experiences a high patient load, providing students with
substantial practical experience compared to many other private
institutions.

e Lecture halls are equipped with modern amenities like centralised
air-conditioning, smart boards, and inverters.

e There is a strong emphasis on extracurriculars, with facilities for
football, basketball, volleyball, and an indoor badminton court.

Overall:Malabar Medical College is highly regarded as a top-tier private
institution in Kerala, offering exceptional academic results and high patient
clinical exposure, though students must adapt to a rigorous schedule and
the physically demanding hilly terrain of the campus.

Parent Reviews

e Parents appreciate the high pass rates (approx. 95%) and the
frequent internal exams that ensure students are constantly prepared
for university.

e Faculty Quality: Many parents are encouraged by the presence of
retired professors from Government Medical College, Kozhikode,
ensuring their children learn from the region's best educators.

e Safety and Discipline: The hostel is noted for having top-notch
security measures, providing peace of mind regarding student safety.

Overall:Malabar Medical College as a safe and academically prestigious
choice that ensures their children become skilled doctors through rigorous
discipline and excellent patient exposure, though they often remain critical

of the high-pressure environment and occasional administrative lapses in
the hospital wing.

(e~ M.0.S.C. MEDICAL COLLEGE HOSPITAL
LOGO

MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES

More than half a century ago, the philanthropist in and around Kolenchery,
under the auspices of the Malankara Orthodox Syrian Church, envisage a
noble initiative to care for the sick and the destitute which gave shape to
the founding of Malankara Orthodox Syrian Church Medical Mission
(MOSC Medical Mission). In addition to MOSC Medical College Hospital,
the Medical Mission runs top rated educational institutions namely MOSC
Medical College, MOSC College of Nursing and MOSC Institute of Allied
Health Sciences.

The MOSC Medical College Hospital started in 1970 with 100 patient beds
has now grown to a well Known 1100 beds multi specialty hospital with
state of the art investigative and therapeutic facilities. We have celebrated
our golden Jubilee of 50 successful years of the hospital in 2019 - 20. At
this juncture we thankfully remember the Founding fathers Late Mr. Chacko
Pillai (Founder Secretary), Dr. K.C. Mammen (Founder Director) and all
great people who lead or contribute to the growth of our institution.

MOSC Medical College and its associated institutes offer MBBS,
postgraduate degrees in clinical and non-clinical specialties (MD and MS),


--- Page 724 ---
a super-specialty DM in Neonatology, undergraduate and postgraduate
Nursing programs (B.Sc, Post Basic B.Sc, M.Sc, and Ph.D.), the Master of
Hospital Administration (MHA), and various PG Diplomas.
Vision: The department aims to be a center of excellence in providing
knowledge of anatomy and quality medical education and research.
Mission: We as a team hope to provide a firm foundation in learning
human anatomy and to emphasize the practical application of anatomical
knowledge in clinical settings and to foster professionalism, ethics, and
critical thinking skills in students.
Basic College Profile
e Name of Institution: Malankara Orthodox Syrian Church (MOSC)
Medical College.
e Location: Medical College Road, Kolenchery, Ernakulam District,
Kerala - 682311.
e Year of Establishment: 2002 (Hospital established in 1970).
e Type of College: Private (Christian Minority / Trust-run).
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur.
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner of Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala.
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC); formerly
Medical Council of India (MCI).
e MBBS Intake: 100 seats.
e Course Duration: 5.5 years (including 1 year of mandatory rotatory
internship).

e Hospital Type: Multi-specialty tertiary care teaching hospital with
1,100 beds.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling


--- Page 727 ---
e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management /
minority / NRl)for MBBS at AIMS are processed via Commissioner for
Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste
/reservation proofs if applicable).

3. Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. AIMS) + quota options (state-quota, minority, NRI) — as per
your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4. Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e If aseat is allotted to you at AIMS, you get an allotment memo / letter.

5. Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to AIMS within deadline with original certificates:NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates, transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof(if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee, etc.) to
confirm admission

6. Join the Course

e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBB1st year at

AIMS with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: Five spacious, air-conditioned lecture theatres
equipped with E-learning facilities and advanced audio-visual aids [8].

e Central Library: A multi-story facility housing over 16,000 books,
100+ national and international journals, and an E-Library section
with high-speed internet [8, 10].

e Laboratories: Specialized practical labs for each pre-clinical and
para-clinical department, including a Skills Lab for hands-on clinical
simulation [2, 10].

e Auditoriums: A large Main Auditorium and a separate Examination
Hall with a seating capacity for over 300 students [10].

e Museums: Well-maintained anatomical, pathological, and forensic
museums featuring a vast collection of specimens and models for
student study [10].

e Hostels: Separate, secure residential blocks for men and women
with attached mess halls and recreational areas located within the
MOSC Campus.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e Ongoing Medical Projects: Collaborative initiatives include the CBM
Community Ear Care Project for hearing restoration and the DRS
Project for monitoring drug-resistant Tuberculosis in Ernakulam.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Total Bed:1,100 beds.

e Outpatient:1,039 patients per day.

e Specialty Units: Includes the Kolenchery Heart Institute (KHI) for
advanced cardiac care and KIND (Kolenchery Institute of
Neurological Diseases), which was the first in Kerala to install a CT
scanner.

e Advanced Diagnostics: Features state-of-the-art technology including
a 64-slice CT scan, MRI, 4D Ultrasound, and a dedicated CathLab for
interventional procedures.

e Emergency Medicine: Operates one of Kerala's largest academic
Emergency Medicine facilities (20,000 sq. ft.) with a 48-bed capacity
and 24/7 point-of-care laboratory services.


--- Page 739 ---
e Surgical Facilities: Equipped with specialized operation theatres for
Cardiovascular and Thoracic Surgery (CVTS), including Heart-lung
machines and advanced laparoscopic units.

e Critical Care: Includes a specialized 42-bed Neuro ICU and a modern
Critical Care Unit (established in 2023) providing intensive life
support.

Campus Life

e Infrastructure: The campus features a modern basketball court, an
indoor stadium, and a high-quality football ground recognized as one
of the best in the zone.

e Games: Facilities for volleyball, tennis, throw ball, cricket, table
tennis, chess, and carom are available.

Hostel & Mess Facilities
1. Separate Hostels for Boys & Girls

e The college provides on-campus hostel accommodation for both male
and female students.

e Rooms are available in single, double & triple sharing formats.

2. Room & Furnishing

e Rooms typically include beds (without mattress), cupboards, study
tables, chairs, fans and lights.

e Some rooms may have basic furnishings, and cleanliness is
maintained regularly. Student reviews mention cleaning staff and
shared bathroom areas.

3. Mess & Dining
e Hostels are attached with mess facilities serving meals to students.


--- Page 740 ---
e Acafeteria is also available on campus for snacks/visitors.
Safety & Support Systems
1. Anti-Ragging Measures

e The college strictly prohibits ragging in any form on campus or
off-campus. Ragging is treated as a serious offence. Students and
parents must submit anti-ragging affidavits at admission time.

e There is a formal Anti-Ragging Committee comprising faculty, hostel
wardens, and legal advisors to address and act on any complaints
immediately.

2. Internal Committees for Discipline & Grievances

e A Grievance Redressal Cell exists where students can report issues
like harassment, misconduct, teaching problems, or other campus
concerns — via email or suggestion box.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

Internship quality at MOSC Medical College is considered high due to the
massive patient volume and advanced clinical infrastructure of the
1,100-bed hospital.

e Clinical Exposure: Interns rotate through high-volume departments
like Emergency Medicine and the Kolenchery Heart Institute, gaining
hands-on experience with complex cases.

e Stipend: Interns receive a competitive monthly stipend of
approximately 25,000 to ¥26,000 (as per KUHS and Kerala Govt.
norms).


--- Page 741 ---
e Workload: The schedule is demanding, particularly in the 24/7
Casualty and Critical Care units, which effectively prepares students
for PG residencies.

e Rural Posting: Mandatory rotations at Rural Health Centres provide
essential experience in community medicine and primary healthcare.

Stipend (MBBS interns & PG students) — authoritative
figures

MBBS Internship Stipend

Medical interns at MOSC Medical College receive a monthly stipend that
aligns with current Kerala state standards:

e Monthly Amount: 226,000 to 27,300.

e Authoritative Basis: The Kerala government enhanced the House
Surgeon stipend to %27,300 effective July 2024. Per NMC CRMI
Regulations 2021, private medical colleges must pay interns at par
with corresponding state government institutions.

Postgraduate (MD/MS) Stipend
Junior Residents (PG students) at MOSC are paid a structured monthly
stipend that increases annually:

e 1st Year PG: 257,876

e 2nd Year PG: 258,968

e 3rd Year PG: %60,060

e Authoritative Basis: These figures are explicitly declared by the
MOSC Medical College Stipend Portal for the 2025-26 financial year.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance redressal,
hostels)

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A dedicated panel, including the Principal,
local police officials, and faculty, monitors the campus 24/7.

e Separation of Freshers: First-year students are often housed in
separate hostel blocks or wings to prevent unauthorized interaction
with seniors.

e Reporting: Students can report incidents via the National
Anti-Ragging Helpline (1800-180-5522) or the college’s internal
portal.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles cases
related to sexual harassment and gender-based discrimination under
the POSH Act.

e Student Redressal Cell: Chaired by the Dean, this committee
addresses academic or infrastructural complaints.

e Online Portal: Grievances can be submitted through the MOSC
Medical College Official Website for documented tracking

e Curfew: Entry into hostels is strictly restricted after 9:00 PM (8:30 PM
for freshers), with mandatory attendance registers.

e Prohibited Items: Consumption of alcohol, tobacco, or illicit drugs
results in immediate suspension or expulsion.

e Dress Code: Students must wear clean white aprons and formal attire
during clinical hours and lectures.

e Mobile Usage: Use of mobile phones is strictly prohibited in lecture
halls and hospital wards

LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
MES Medical College, founded in 2004, has embarked on a remarkable
journey of delivering quality education and healthcare services. Though our
journey began with an annual intake of 100 students, we have since
expanded our reach and offerings. Our institution is complemented by a
600-bed hospital that provides a comprehensive range of medical and
surgical specialties, including major super specialties. From the very outset
of establishing our Teaching Hospital, we have remained committed to
extending, free medical care, diagnostic tests, medications, surgeries, and
related services to those in need.
In 2011, MES Medical College attained the status of a Post Graduate
Medical Institute, offering Post Graduate Degree and Diploma Courses in
all disciplines. Within the same campus, MES has also introduced Dental
and Nursing Colleges, providing Post Graduate Courses.
On average, we attend to approximately five lakh patients from diverse
backgrounds every year, demonstrating our unwavering dedication to
serving the community.


--- Page 750 ---
Vision:The MES Medical College is the end of an arduous trek of a once
beleaguered community from the womb of ignorance, illiteracy and
ignominy. Leaving aside the horrors of 1921, the partition of minds in 1947,
we hold our hands with the brethren of our fraternal communities and
march forward into a new dawn of scientific temper and secular ethos.
Mission:The mission of MES Medical College Hospital is to make available
the highest quality of health services and facilities for the community, to
give wellness to all, to relieve pain and restore health as speedily and
safely and as humanely as is possible regardless of age, gender or creed
with competent and innovative services as well as with human care and
respect and educate the people on prevention of illness and thus help them
be healthy always.
Basic College Profile
e Name of Institution: MES Medical College (also referred to as MES
Academy of Medical Sciences).
e Location: Malaparamba, Palachode Post, Perinthalmanna,
Malappuram District.
e Year of Establishment: 2004.
e Type of College: Private (Non-Government), Self-Financing Muslim
Minority Institution.
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur.
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala.
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC).
e MBBS Intake: 150 seats per year.


--- Page 751 ---
e Course Duration: 5.5 years (including a 1-year compulsory rotating
internship).
e Hospital Type: Multi-Super-Speciality Teaching Hospital with over
600 beds.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Mandatory Entrance Exam
e NEET-UG 2025: All candidates must qualify for the National
Eligibility-cum-Entrance Test (NEET-UG) with a valid percentile rank.
2. Counseling Authority
e CEE Kerala: The Commissioner for Entrance Examinations (CEE),
Kerala conducts the entire admission process via the KEAM (Kerala
Engineering Architecture Medical) portal.


--- Page 754 ---
3. Counseling Rounds & Choice Filling

e Option Registration: Once the merit list is published, candidates must
log into the KEAM Candidate Portal and register their "options"
(preferences) for colleges and courses.

e Registration: Aspiring candidates must register on the CEE portal,
typically in February-March, and upload their NEET results once
declared.

4. Special Quotas (Muslim Minority & NRI)

e Minority Seats: To claim one of the 75 reserved seats for the Muslim
community, candidates must indicate this during CEE registration and
provide a Community Certificate issued by a Revenue Authority.

e NRI Quota: 15% of seats (22 seats) are for NRI candidates. These
also require CEE registration and specific documents (Sponsor's
Passport/Visa, Relationship Certificate).

5. Post-Allotment Formalities

e Allotment Memo: If allotted a seat, candidates must download the
allotment memo from the CEE portal.

e Fee Payment: The tuition fee specified in the memo must be paid to
confirm the seat.

e Physical Reporting: Candidates must report to the college within the
scheduled dates with original documents for final verification and
admission.
