Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Halls: The college has 5 air-conditioned, soundproof lecture
theaters. Four are located in the medical college building and one in
the hospital.

o Capacity: Three halls accommodate 180 students each, while
the largest seats 250 students.
o Technology: Equipped with digital screens, LCD projectors,
OHPs, and modern audio-visual aids.

e Examination Halls: Two dedicated halls of 250 sq. meters each for
university and internal assessments.

e Departmental Labs: Each pre-clinical and para-clinical department
(such as Anatomy, Biochemistry, and Pathology) has its own
specialized labs and demo rooms for 75 students.


--- Page 769 ---
e Teaching Hospital: A 600+ bedded super-specialty hospital with 17
modern Operation Theatres and specialized ICUs (NICU, PICU,
MICU).

e Space & Capacity: A 2,400 sq. meter (approx. 10,000 sq. ft.)
air-conditioned digital library with a seating capacity for 500 students.

e Digital Access: Features high-speed internet (100 Mbps lease line),
40 internet nodes, and access to e-journals and online medical
literature.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e The campus includes NABL-accredited molecular labs and an
advanced ART (Assisted Reproductive Technology) facility.

e Students consistently secure top positions under KUHS, including
first ranks in MD Pathology and PG Diploma (DCH).

e Cultural Fests: Annual sports and cultural fests, alongside specialized
events. like Alzheimer's Day observances. in collaboration with the
Neurology department.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A 600+ bedded facility (some reports cite up to 750+
beds) with specialized units.

e Intensive Care Units (ICUs): Features dedicated Multidisciplinary
ICUs (MDICU), High Dependency Units (HDU), Neonatal ICUs
(NICU), and specialized Medical ICUs (MICU) equipped with
advanced vital sign monitoring.


--- Page 770 ---
e Diagnostics & Radiology: Fully digitized department offering MRI, CT
Scan, Ultrasound, Mammography, and a 24/7 NABL-accredited
Central Laboratory.

e Specialized Units: Houses one of the largest modern Dialysis Units in
the region, a Cath Lab, and a 24/7 blood bank with component
separation.

e Patient Inflow: The hospital attends to approximately 5 lakh patients
annually, with a daily outpatient (OPD) volume of over 1,150 patients,
providing diverse clinical cases for study.

e Super-Specialty Access: Students rotate through various
super-specialty departments, including Neurology (offering DM
courses), Cardiology, Nephrology, Urology, and Oncology.

Campus Life

e Athletics: The college is a powerhouse in the KUHS C-Zone, recently
clinching championships in Football and Women's Chess (2025).

e Facilities: Includes a_ full-sized football. field, basketball courts,
badminton courts, and an indoor games area for table tennis and
carroms.

e College Unions: The student union is highly active, organizing
massive annual arts fests and graduation ceremonies like Fozfade
and Hesoyam.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Accommodation: Rooms are available on a shared basis, typically

accommodating two or four students.


--- Page 771 ---
e Amenities: Each student is provided with essential furniture including
a bed, study table, chair, and cupboard/wardrobe. Some rooms may
have attached bathrooms, while others have _ well-maintained
common toilet facilities on each floor.

e Mandatory Mess: Availing the mess facility is generally mandatory for
all hostel residents, and food costs are a significant portion of the
annual hostel fee.

e Menu & Quality: The mess provides a diverse menu of healthy and
nutritious food, including both vegetarian and non-vegetarian options
that cater to various dietary preferences. The menu often follows a
fixed weekly schedule.

Safety & Support Systems

e Student Support & Guidance Programme: Dedicated to academic
success and emotional well-being, offering services like personal,
mental health, and adolescent health counseling.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A supervisory body that meets regularly to
review preventive measures and investigate any reported incidents.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Zero Tolerance: Ragging is strictly prohibited by law, defined as any
act causing physical or psychological harm, embarrassment, or fear.

e Enforcement: The college maintains an active Anti-Ragging
Committee and Squad that conducts regular rounds, including in
hostels.


--- Page 772 ---
e Administration: The Principal serves as the Chief Warden, with a
resident Deputy Warden managing daily affairs.
e Curfew & Roll Call: Residents must be present for daily roll calls.
Standard MES hostels often close gates around 9:30 PM.

and 30 minutes to reach by taxi or car.
By Rail
e The nearest railway station is Angadipuram Railway Station
(AAM), which is around 4 km from the college campus.
By Road
e The college is well-connected by road, with easy access via
public or private transportation.

twiggy’, Medical College

2 MEL" (FORMERLY KNOWN AS DM WAYANAD INSTITUTE OF MEDICAL SCIENCES)

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Dr. Moopen’s Medical College Hospital-formerly known as DMWIMS- was
founded by DM Education and Research Foundation, after analyzing the
needs and gaps in the health care facilities in the Wayanad area. It is the
first Medical College in Kerala established in a backward, hilly & tribal
district. It is also the first Medical College Hospital in North Kerala and one
among the very few Medical College Hospitals in the country established in
a rural area to receive NABH accreditation.
We are dedicated to transforming health through medical education,
healthcare and medical research. We offer quality healthcare at an
affordable cost. We are committed to providing high-quality medical
education and training. We aim to improve the healthcare infrastructure and
overall development of Wayanad.
Vision
To be one of the top medical institutions in India adopting global standards
in education, research and innovation moulding healthcare professionals to
serve the world with compassion and commitment, in harmony with nature.
Mission
To develop best-in-class academic and clinical infrastructure with talented
faculty and Administration to provide the required atmosphere for imbibing
knowledge.To create an ambience for holistic learning through constant


--- Page 780 ---
interaction between teachers and students with ready access to the
laboratories, libraries and patients.To keep meritocracy along with a
passion for taking up the noble medical profession with all its sacrifices as
the basis for selection of the students and aid in them ingesting this culture,
while on campus.
Basic College Profile
e Name of Institution: Dr. Moopen’s Medical College (formerly known
as DM Wayanad Institute of Medical Sciences - DM WIMS)
e Location: Naseera Nagar, Meppadi P.O., Wayanad, Kerala - 673577
e Year of Establishment: 2013
e Type of College: Private (Trust)
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala (via the KEAM portal)
e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC)

internship).

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: 798 beds are currently operational, with
long-term infrastructure capacity planned for up to 1,000 beds.

e Total ICU Beds: The hospital maintains multiple modern intensive
care units, including ICCU, MICU, SICU, PICU, and NICU.

e Total Operation Theatres: The facility is equipped with modular
operation theatres designed for complex surgical procedures.

e Total Outpatients: The hospital serves as a critical tertiary care hub
for the Wayanad district, managing a high daily volume of outpatients
from local and tribal communities.

e Emergency Services: Provides comprehensive 24/7 emergency and
trauma care with a dedicated helpline at +91 81118 81234.

e Hospital Accreditation: It is NABH-accredited, distinguished as the
first medical college hospital in North Kerala and one of the few rural
facilities in India to hold this quality certification.

e Clinical Exposure: Students gain significant hands-on experience
through a diverse patient pool including local tribal populations,

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1. Qualify Entrance Exam
e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).
e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English)must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general,40%for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.


--- Page 783 ---
2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing/management /
minority / NRI) for MBBS at AIMS are processed via Commissioner
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE)through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste
/reservation proofs if applicable).

3. Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) +colleges
(e.g. AIMS) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your
eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4. Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences, and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e If aseat is allotted to you at AIMS, you get an allotment memo / letter.

5. Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to AIMS within deadline with original certificates:‘NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates, transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof(if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.


--- Page 784 ---
6. Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBB1st year at
AIMS with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
Core Academic Facilities

e Academic Block: A multi-level facility housing departments for
Anatomy, Physiology, Pharmacology, and Microbiology. It includes
specialized seminar halls, eight student laboratories, and dedicated
common rooms for students.

e Lecture Halls: The campus contains four major lecture halls and two
large examination halls equipped for modern teaching.

e Central Library: An adequately stocked library featuring hard copies,
online resources, and subject-related research papers. It is fully
integrated with Wi-Fi to support digital learning.

e Laboratories: Equipped with state-of-the-art standards, the college
maintains departmental labs and a central ICMR-recognized research
lab.


--- Page 793 ---
Clinical & Research Infrastructure

e Teaching Hospital: A 700-bedded NABH-accredited hospital
(expandable to 1,000 beds) provides students with hands-on clinical
exposure in various specialties.

e Research & Innovation (R&l) Unit: Focuses on cutting-edge fields like
3D Bioprinting, tissue engineering, and cancer biology. It houses a
specialized R&l lab with advanced instrumentation for biomedical
research.

e IT Infrastructure: Features a comprehensive network of approximately
300 systems, extensive LAN/VLAN connectivity, and high-speed
internet to facilitate e-learning platforms like Moodle and Google
Classrooms.

Student Support & Campus Amenities

e Accommodation: Separate hostels for male and female students,
interns, and residents are located on-campus, with 100%
accommodation planned for faculty and residents.

e Learning Environment: The campus includes the Naseera Botanical
Garden, which features a wide range of medicinal plants for botanical
and medical study.

e Recreational Facilities: Includes a gym, football-cum-cricket ground,
and basketball courts to encourage physical fitness alongside
academic pursuits.


--- Page 794 ---
Key Hospital Infrastructure

e Bed Capacity: A 700-bedded NABH-accredited teaching hospital.
Plans are in place to upgrade this capacity to 1,000 beds, with 650
designated specifically as teaching beds.

e Specialized Units:

o Intensive Care: Includes 57 specialized ICU beds and
dedicated Neonatal Intensive Care Units (NICU).

o Operating Theatres: Modern surgical suites equipped for a wide
spectrum of procedures.

o Emergency & Outpatient: Features 24/7 emergency services
and extensive Outpatient Departments (OPD) covering multiple
clinical specialties.

e Support Services: Integrated 24-hour pharmacy, blood bank, and
advanced diagnostic imaging including PACS (Picture Archiving and
Communication System).

Technology & Diagnostic Infrastructure

e Laboratory Services: A fully automated and interfaced laboratory
department. It includes an ICMR-approved and NABL-accredited
BSL-2 Virology lab.

e BioNEST Incubator: A 11,000 sq. ft. facility supporting healthcare
technology innovation. It features a DSIR-recognized Biomedical
Research Lab, a clinical simulation lab, and a digital health database.

e IT Integration: The hospital is supported by a comprehensive Hospital
Information System (HIS) and Laboratory Information System (LIS) to
streamline patient management and data.


--- Page 795 ---
Hostel Amenities

e Room Features: Rooms are well-furnished with a personal cot, study
table and chair, wardrobe, and a bookshelf for each student. Most
rooms are triple-sharing, with single occupancy options available for
interns or at an additional cost.

e Hygiene & Maintenance: High levels of cleanliness are maintained,
with cleaning staff performing weekly cleaning of rooms and
washrooms.

e Utilities & Connectivity: Hostels offer a 24/7 electricity and water
supply, with a geyser/water heater in every bathroom. Free
high-speed Wi-Fi is available throughout the hostel and academic
blocks.

e Food & Dining: A hygienic mess facility provides nutritious vegetarian
and non-vegetarian food options.

e Security: The hostels are highly secure with 24-hour security
personnel and CCTV surveillance to ensure student safety.

Mens Hotel
The men’s hostel can accommodate around 236 students in about 160
rooms according to the official college hostel capacity data.

e Room Type: Mostly shared rooms (typically 3 students per room).

e Furnishings: Rooms usually include beds/cots, study tables, chairs,
cupboards/wardrobes.

e Bathrooms: Shared bathrooms’ with hot water (water
heaters/“geyser”’) available.

e Electricity & Water: 24-hour power and water supply.


--- Page 796 ---
e Wi-Fi: Hostel Wi-Fi/internet connectivity available.

e Hostel stay is typically mandatory for first-year MBBS students.

e Students often describe the hostel as spacious with good
infrastructure, though experiences with food and other services can
vary.

e Hostel and mess charges vary depending on the year and room type.

Women’s Hostel

The college has separate hostel accommodation for female students on
campus, distinct from the boys’ hostel.

The women’s hostel has more capacity than the men’s: it can
accommodate around 439 students in about 276 rooms.

e Shared rooms (usually 2-3 students per room).

e Furniture: Beds/cots, study tables, chairs, cupboards, shelving.

e 24x7 electricity and water supply, including hot water in
bathrooms.

e Wi-Fi/Internet connectivity.

e Mess facility with meals (veg & non-veg options).

e Security and CCTV monitoring across hostel premises.

e Laundry services and weekly cleaning support.

e Separate gym and recreational spaces available on campus (for both
boys and girls).

Mess & Food

e There is a hostel mess with meals provided, generally including both

vegetarian and non-vegetarian options.


--- Page 797 ---
e Mess food quality reviews vary among students, so experiences
differ.

Campus Safety & Security

e 24x7 Security Surveillance: The campus and hostels are monitored
with 24-hour CCTV cameras at key points to deter and record any
suspicious activity.

e Controlled Entry & Access: Access to the college campus is
regulated to ensure that only students, staff, patients, and authorized
visitors can enter with legitimate reasons.

e Hostel Wardens & Staff: Each hostel has designated wardens and
assistant wardens who routinely check on students, maintain
discipline, and act as the first point of contact in case of concerns.

Anti-Ragging Measures

e Anti-Ragging Committee & Squad: The college maintains a formal
anti-ragging committee with faculty members, administrative staff,
police representation, and student reps to prevent ragging on campus
and in hostels.

e Awareness & Enforcement: The committee runs awareness
campaigns, displays anti-ragging information, conducts surprise
inspections of hostels and common areas, and enforces strict
disciplinary actions as per regulatory guidelines.

Emergency Contacts: New students are provided important contact
numbers (including anti-ragging helplines) to report incidents quickly.


--- Page 798 ---
Student Support Systems

e Academic Support: Faculty mentoring, Medical Education Unit
(MEV), library & clinical training support.

e Safety & Welfare: Active Anti-Ragging Committee, helplines,
campus & hostel security.

e Health Services: 24x7 access to the on-campus teaching hospital
and emergency care.

e Counselling & Well-Being: Guidance for academic stress and
personal issues.

e Hostel Support: Wardens, disciplined hostel system, student welfare
monitoring.

e Student Activities: Sports, cultural programs, clubs, and community
activities.

e Financial Aid: Merit- and need-based scholarships.

MBBS Internship (Compulsory One-Year Rotatory Internship)

e The internship is a mandatory 12-month clinical training students
must complete after finishing their 4.5 years of academic MBBS
studies.

e Without completing this internship, a student is not eligible to be
awarded an MBBS degree or gain full registration with the medical
council.

GetMyAdmission — Professional Review of Dr.Moopens
Medical College
At GetMyAdmission, we evaluate medical colleges across India based on
academic strength, clinical exposure, infrastructure, faculty support, and
overall student experience. Dr. Moopen’s Medical College, Wayanad, has
steadily emerged as a strong private medical institution in Kerala,
especially noted for its hospital services and rural clinical exposure.
Student Perspective
Students commonly highlight:
e Good clinical exposure, as the attached hospital is a major tertiary
care center for Wayanad and surrounding rural regions.
e Supportive and approachable faculty, particularly in pre-clinical and
para-clinical departments.
e Well-planned academic schedule with regular internal assessments
and structured postings.


--- Page 802 ---
e Modern infrastructure, including well-equipped laboratories, lecture
halls, library, and skill labs.
e A peaceful, distraction-free campus environment, ideal for focused
medical studies.
Parent Perspective
Parents often appreciate:
e The hospital’s strong reputation and service to tribal and rural
populations, ensuring real-world clinical training.
e A safe, disciplined campus with controlled student environment and
good security.
e Good hostel facilities with acceptable living standards for both boys
and girls.
e Internship training that builds clinical confidence and hands-on skills,
especially in general medicine, surgery, and emergency care.
Overall Assessment
Dr. Moopen’s Medical College provides a balanced medical education with
emphasis on clinical learning and patient interaction. The college benefits
from being a key healthcare provider in Wayanad, giving students exposure
to a wide spectrum of cases. While its remote location may feel limiting to


--- Page 803 ---
some, it significantly enhances bedside learning and responsibility among
students.

MEDICAL COLLEGE

LOGO

Medical College History & Introduction

The Mount Zion Medical College Hospital was established in the year 2012
by The Charitable Educational and Welfare Society Reg No. Q373/84. The
College includes all the clinical Departments, such as Departments of
General Medicine, General Surgery, Orthopaedics, Obstetrics and
Gynaecology, Paediatrics, Ophthalmology, Oto-Rhino Laryngology ENT),
Anaesthesiology, Radio-diagnosis, Radio therapy, and Dentistry and non
clinical Departments such as Anatomy, Physiology, Biochemistry,
Pharmacology, Pathology, Microbiology, Forensic Medicine and Community
Medicine. A green, calm, quiet and serene area flourished in 32 acres. The
Medical College is about 8 kilometres away from Adoor and can be
reached by road from Adoor or Pathanapuram. The Medical College is
recognized by the Medical University and approved by the Government of
Kerala.

The institution’s Vision is to emerge as an excellent center for healing and
learning in all possible ways incorporating knowledge, experience,
automation and technology enhancing cure and patient satisfaction.And


--- Page 807 ---
mission is to provide comprehensive and innovate patient care with
dedication, commitment & cost effectiveness, by increased knowledge and
facilities which results in better patient outcome. “Trust upon us, we will
care for you” is the motto of Mount Zion Medical College.
Basic College Profile

e Institution Type : Private Self Financing Medical College

e Minority Status: Christian Minority Institution

e Campus : The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located

in Adoor Pathanamthitta.

e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)

e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences.

e Recognised by: National Medical Commission (NMC)

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e If aseat is allotted to you at Mount Zion Medical College , you get an
allotment memo / letter.

5.Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to Mount Zion Medical College within deadline with original
certificates: NEET scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing
certificates,transfer / conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation
proof (if applicable), ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Mount Zion Medical College with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Theatres : Multiple spacious, air-conditioned lecture
halls equipped with audiovisual teaching aids (projectors, smart
boards) to support effective classroom learning.
e Central Library : The Mount Zion Medical College has a full-fledged
library which functions from 8am to 4pm. The library is equipped with


--- Page 818 ---
various books including the journals, reference books as well as the
text books. The library subscribes to international and national
journals. The Library has separate sections of all the available titles
on almost all important branches of Medical sciences. E-Library
facilities have been introduced for the academic value addition for
students and the students can access.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Separate hostels for boys and girls are available on/near the college
campus.

e The hostel is under the supervision of resident wardens and a faculty
member. Students are forbidden to reside in unapproved lodgings

e Rooms are typically 2-sharing with attached bathrooms in most
blocks.

e Hostel accommodation is compulsory for all students.

e Basic furniture like beds, tables, cupboards is provided.

e Security, housekeeping, and maintenance services are present.

e Students have to make necessary entries in the "Movement Register"
before leaving the hostel for outing/shopping. All inmates are
expected to contact the Faculty Warden or Resident Warden for
redressal of any grievance during their stay in the hostel. Inmates are
bound to obey the directions of the warden.

Services & Security

e Specialized Departments: Comprehensive care in, General
Medicine, Pediatrics, Orthopaedics, and Obstetrics & Gynaecology.

e Emergency Care: A 24/7 Emergency and TraumaCareunit equipped
with advanced critical care facilities and ambulance services.

e Advanced Diagnostics: In-house laboratory and radiology services,
including interventional cardiology for procedures like pacemakers
and coronary artery interventions.

e Patient Support: Services include insurance assistance (KASP),
outpatient booking, and dedicated guest relations staff to assist with
the hospital experience.


--- Page 820 ---
e Hostel Security: Separate hostels for male and female students
feature 24 Security Personal to monitor access and safety.

e Campus Environment: The campus is a serene 32-acre area
designed with accessibility in mind, including wheelchair-accessible
entrances and parking.

e Safety Protocols: The hospital follows a quality policy committed to
ethical practices and patient safety, aiming for national and
international accreditation standards like NABH.

Student Support Systems

e Student Welfare Committee: A dedicated body that addresses
student concerns, provides resources for personal development, and
facilitates financial assistance or scholarships for those in need.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: Ensures a safe campus by implementing
strict policies and awareness campaigns to prevent bullying,
particularly for newcomers.

e Grievance Redressal Cell: Offers a formal platform for students to
voice issues related to academics, facilities,or campus life for prompt
resolution.

e Mentoring Programme: Students are paired with mentors who
provide guidance and affirmation to help them navigate career
transitions and personal growth.

e Foundation Program: Helps students from diverse backgrounds
transition into the MBBS curriculum with dedicated time for
self-directed learning.


--- Page 821 ---
e Student Corner: An online portal featuring educational role-plays
and medical scenarios created by students to enhance peer-to-peer
learning.

MBBS Internship (Compulsory One-Year Rotatory Internship)

e The internship is a mandatory 12-month clinical training students
must complete after finishing their 4.5 years of academic MBBS
studies.

e Without completing this internship, a student is not eligible to be
awarded an MBBS degree or gain full registration with the medical
council.

Mount Zion Medical College Student Parent Review
Student Review

Students describe Mount Zion Medical College as a disciplined and
academically focused institution with supportive and experienced faculty
members. The teaching approach emphasizes conceptual understanding,
clinical application, and ethical medical practice. Clinical exposure is
steadily improving, with students gaining hands-on experience through
OPD postings, ward rounds, and emergency duties.

The campus provides essential facilities including hostels, library
resources, and recreational spaces. Students appreciate the safe and
secure environment, regular academic monitoring, and mentorship support.
While infrastructure continues to develop, the overall student experience is
positive, especially for those seeking a structured and serious medical
education environment.


--- Page 822 ---
Overall : Mount Zion Medical College provides a disciplined academic
environment with supportive faculty and steadily improving clinical
exposure. Students value the structured learning system, safety, and focus
on professional development.
Parent Review
Parents regard Mount Zion Medical College as a well-structured institution
that prioritizes academic discipline, student safety, and professional
development. They appreciate the organized teaching system, qualified
faculty, and consistent academic monitoring that help students maintain
strong academic performance.
The campus environment is considered safe and supportive, with proper
hostel facilities, security measures, and student support services. Parents
also value the institution's focus on ethics, patient care, and character
building, which prepares students not only to succeed academically but
also to become responsible and compassionate medical professionals.
Overall: Parents appreciate Mount Zion Medical College for its disciplined
academic environment, safe campus, and supportive faculty. They value
the institution’s focus on student welfare, professionalism, and consistent
academic guidance.

GetMyAdmission Professional Review — Mount Zion Medical
College
At GetMyAdmission, we assess medical institutions across India based on
academics, clinical exposure, infrastructure, and student support. Mount
Zion Medical College is a private medical institution in Kerala that is still in
its developmental stage. While it offers MBBS education with basic facilities
and faculty support, its clinical exposure and hospital services are currently
limited compared to more established private and government medical
colleges.

Student Perspective
Students highlight:

e Limited clinical exposure due to low OPD and IPD patient inflow.

e Supportive faculty, but with shortages and frequent changes in some

departments.

e Basic academic infrastructure, including lecture halls and

laboratories, with scope for improvement.

e Quiet campus environment, but fewer academic and extracurricular

activities.


--- Page 824 ---
Parent Perspective
Parents appreciate:

e Relatively affordable fee structure compared to many private medical

colleges.

e Safe and disciplined campus environment.

e Ongoing development of hospital and academic facilities.

e Less crowded campus allowing closer faculty-student interaction.
Overall Assessment
Mount Zion Medical College currently provides basic medical education but
lacks strong clinical exposure and well-established hospital services.
Students must be self-driven and proactive to maximize learning
opportunities. It is more suitable for those prioritizing affordability and a
calm campus over high patient load and advanced clinical training.

Palakkad Institute of Medical

PIMS

LOGO:
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Established in 2014 under the V.N. Public Health and Educational Trust,
the Palakkad Institute of Medical Sciences (PIMS) was founded by the
visionary philanthropist and industrialist Dr. V.N. Venkitachalam. Located in
Walayar, near the Kerala-Tamil.Nadu border, the institution was built to
provide advanced, affordable healthcare to rural populations while fostering
academic excellence. It operates under the same leadership ethos as its
parent institution, Malabar Medical College (MMCHR), and is affiliated with
the Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the
National Medical Commission (NMC).
The institution offers a wide range of academic programs, primarily its
flagship MBBS course with an annual intake of 150 seats, as well as
Bachelor of Physiotherapy (BPT) and B.Sc. Nursing through its specialized
schools. Students gain hands-on clinical experience at the attached
300-bed multispecialty hospital, which provides 24-hour emergency


--- Page 832 ---
services and specialized care in departments such as _ cardiology,
neurology, and oncology. With modern infrastructure including digital
classrooms, simulation labs, and research-focused community medicine
programs, PIMS has rapidly become a key center for medical training and
public health service in the region.
Vision:We envision the Indian Medical Graduates to be effective public
health leaders,accountable the community at large, and proficient in their
Medical profession-providing holistic treatment to build a healthy nation .
Mission:To impact comprehensive training in preventive,promotive and
primary healthcare through field-based learning.We are committed to
fostering community oriented ethical practice to improve the health and well
being of people.
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Palakkad Institute of Medical Sciences (PIMS)

e Location: Walayar, Palakkad, Kerala 678624

e Year of Establishment: 2014

e Type of College: Private (Self-Financing)

Thrissur
e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala.

e MBBS Intake: 150 Seats

e Hospital Type: Multispecialty Teaching Hospital (300+ Beds).

MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Curriculum: Follows the latest Competency-Based Medical Education

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. Qualify NEET-UG 2026: You must appear for the NEET-UG exam
and secure the minimum qualifying percentile (50th for General, 40th
for SC/ST/OBC).

2. Register with CEE Kerala: Apply online through the Commissioner for
Entrance Examinations (CEE) Kerala website. This is mandatory for
both Kerala natives and non-Keralites seeking management/NRI
seats.

3. Option Entry (Choice Filling): When the "Option Registration" window
opens, log in to the CEE portal and select Palakkad Institute of
Medical Sciences as your preferred college.

4. Check Allotment: Monitor the CEE website for the seat allotment list.
If you are selected, download your Allotment Memo.

5. Fee Payment: Pay the required tuition fee to the CEE account as
specified in the allotment memo to confirm your intent to join.

6. Physical Reporting: Visit the PIMS campus in Walayar with your
original documents (NEET card, 10th/12th marks, Transfer
Certificate, etc.) to complete the verification and final admission.

Academic Infrastructure

e Lecture Theatres: The campus features four large, gallery-style
lecture halls, each with a seating capacity for 180+ students. They
are centrally air-conditioned and equipped with modern audio-visual
aids, including digital smart boards and high-definition projectors.

e Central Library: A massive facility spanning over 2,000 sq. meters,
providing:

o Separate reading sections for students and faculty.

e Pre-Clinical & Para-Clinical Labs: Specialized laboratories for
Anatomy, Physiology, Biochemistry, Pathology, Microbiology, and
Pharmacology. These are equipped with advanced microscopes,
chemical analyzers, and specialized diagnostic equipment.

e Dissection Hall: A large, well-ventilated hall in the Anatomy
department for cadaveric dissection, equipped with modern storage
tanks and embalming facilities.

e Departmental Museums: Each department (such as_ Forensic
Medicine, Anatomy, and Pathology) maintains a museum with a vast


--- Page 844 ---
collection of specimens, charts, and models for visual and self-paced
learning.
Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e AARAMBH 2026: The annual orientation and white coat ceremony for
the new 2026 MBBS batch, emphasizing the transition to the CBME
(Competency-Based Medical Education) curriculum.

e NMC Milestone: The institution successfully secured its annual seat
renewal from the National Medical Commission (NMC) for the
150-seat intake, maintaining high standards in faculty-to-student
ratios.

e KUHS' Research Projects: Several faculty members and
undergraduate students have been granted research funding from the
Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS) for projects focusing on
lifestyle diseases prevalent in the Palakkad region.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: The hospital currently operates with 300 to 450
multispecialty beds. Long-term development plans include a phased
expansion to a 700-bed capacity to meet increasing regional demand.

e Clinical Departments: Full-fledged departments are operational in
General Medicine, General Surgery, Pediatrics, Obstetrics &
Gynecology, Orthopedics, ENT, Ophthalmology, Psychiatry,
Dermatology, and specialized units like Cardiology, Neurology,
Urology, and Nephrology.

e Emergency & Critical Care: A 24/7 Casualty and Trauma Center is
equipped to handle medical and surgical emergencies. The hospital


--- Page 845 ---
also features specialized intensive care units, including Medical,
Surgical, and Neonatal ICUs.

e Early Clinical Exposure (ECE): In accordance with the 2026 CBME
curriculum, MBBS students begin clinical interactions in their first year
to integrate theoretical knowledge with patient care.

e Patient Footfall: The hospital’s strategic location on NH 544 ensures
a high volume of diverse cases, offering students extensive hands-on
experience in managing both routine and complex medical conditions

e Outpatient Department (OPD): The hospital manages an average
daily footfall of 800 to 1,000+ patients. The OPD operates across all
major clinical and super-specialty departments, providing
comprehensive care to the local community in Walayar and
neighboring districts of Tamil Nadu.

e Inpatient Department (IPD):

o Bed Occupancy: The hospital functions with a strength of 300 to
450 multispecialty beds.
Campus Life

e Sports Infrastructure: The campus promotes physical well-being with
facilities for outdoor sports like Football, Cricket, and Volleyball. There
are also dedicated courts for Basketball and Badminton.

e Indoor Games: Common rooms in the hostels provide facilities for
Table Tennis, Carrom, and Chess.

e Gymnasium: A well-equipped in-house gym is available for students
to maintain their fitness schedules
Scenic Location: Situated at the foothills of the Western Ghats in


--- Page 846 ---
Walayar, the campus provides a serene, pollution-free environment
conducive to focused study.

e Security: The entire 30-acre campus is under 24/7 CCTV surveillance
and is patrolled by a dedicated security team to ensure student
safety.

e Anti-Ragging Cell: PIMS maintains a strict Zero-Tolerance Policy
toward ragging, with a dedicated committee and helpdesk to ensure a
friendly atmosphere for newcomers.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Accommodation: Separate hostel buildings are available for men and
women, ensuring privacy and security.

e Room Configuration: Rooms are typically offered on a twin-sharing or
triple-sharing basis, designed to be spacious and well-ventilated.

e Amenities: Each room is furnished with essential items including
individual cots, study tables, chairs, bookshelves, and storage
wardrobes.

e Security: The hostels are secured by dedicated security personnel
and under constant CCTV surveillance, with strict entry/exit protocols.

e Centralized Mess Hall: A large, modern, and hygienic mess hall
serves all resident students.

e Cuisine & Menu: The menu primarily offers both South Indian and
North Indian meals, prepared in a centralized kitchen using hygienic
practices. The diet is balanced to meet the nutritional requirements of
students.


--- Page 847 ---
Safety & Support Systems

e 24/7 Surveillance: The 30-acre campus and all hostel corridors are
monitored by a centralized CCTV surveillance system and
round-the-clock professional security personnel.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: PIMS follows a zero-tolerance policy
towards ragging. A dedicated Anti-Ragging Committee and Squad
conduct regular rounds and ensure compliance with UGC and NMC
regulations.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A high-level committee comprising the
Principal, senior faculty, local police officials, and parent
representatives monitors the campus.

e Student Grievance Redressal Committee (SGRC): Handles
complaints related to academic unfairness, administrative delays, or
infrastructure issues.

Palakkad Institute of Medical Sciences, PalakkadStudent &

e Palakkad Institute of Medical Sciences (PIMS) remains largely

Medical College History & Introduction
P K Das Institute of Medical Sciences is a state-of-the-art super specialty
Medical College with 1000+ beds which aims to provide world-class
healthcare education to all our students. It was established in 2014 in
Palakkad district. It is a healthcare initiative by the Nehru College of
Educational and Charitable Trust.The college is affiliated with the Kerala
University of Health Sciences (KUHS) and recognized by the National
Medical Commission (NMC). It offers the MBBS program along with
postgraduate courses in various specialties. Since its inception, PKDIMS
has focused on academic excellence, ethical medical practice, and holistic
student development.The college’s vision is to be among the top 10
Medical Colleges in India by 2030 in research, medical education, and
excellence in patient care and to create leaders of Medical profession in
patient — centered, science — driven, team — based, high — value health
care.And Its mission is to be a national leader in educating and developing
the next generation of doctors, nurses, and paramedics; to attract
distinguished medical professionals and teachers and establish centers of
excellence in all specialties; to support and empower students and faculty
in their pursuit of discovery, healing, and innovation; to deliver cutting-edge,


--- Page 855 ---
interdisciplinary, and compassionate clinical care of the highest quality; to
treat every patient with dignity and respect; and to improve the overall
health and well-being of the communities it serves.
Basic College Profile
e PK Das Institute of Medical Sciences is a state-of-the-art super
specialty Medical College established in 2014 in Palakkad district.
e Campus: The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located
in Palakkad.
e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI).
e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences
e Recognised by the National Medical Commission (NMC).

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Qualify Entrance Exam
e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).
e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.


--- Page 858 ---
2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at PKDIMS are processed via
Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through
centralized counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. PKDIMS_ ) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per
your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e Ifa seat is allotted to you at PKDIMS , you get an allotment memo /
letter.

5.Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to PKDIMS within deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.


--- Page 859 ---
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at PKDIMS with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
e Academic Block: The campus features a dedicated multi-level
academic block. This block recently underwent a major renovation,
with a modernized Academic Office inaugurated in November 2025 to
improve student and administrative services.
e Lecture Theaters: The college has six air-conditioned lecture
theaters.
o Four are located in the Academic Block (Level 1 and 2), each
with a capacity for 320 students.
o One theater with a 200-student capacity is situated in the
Hospital Block.
o All theaters are equipped with independent audio-visual aids
and LAN facilities
e Central Library: A 2,400 sq. meter air-conditioned facility spread
over two floors, featuring a seating capacity for 500 people.


--- Page 868 ---
o Resources: It houses approximately 12,000 medical books and
46 national/international journals.

o Digital Library: Equipped with high-speed internet (18 Mbps -
100 Mbps) and access to global e-resources and e-journals.

e Examination Halls: Two air-conditioned examination halls with a
seating capacity of 350 each, equipped with CCTV and mobile
jammers as per KUHS regulations.

e Laboratories and Skill Labs:

o A modern skill lab is located in the Academic Block for practical
training and simulations.

o Specialized laboratories exist for departments like Biochemistry,
Histopathology, and Virology, equipped for both pre-clinical and
para-clinical training.

Clinical Teaching Infrastructure

e Teaching Hospital: The institution operates a 1,000+ bed
super-specialty teaching hospital.

e Specialized Units: Includes advanced ICUs, a 24-hour emergency
and casualty service, a cath lab, and a recently inaugurated
chemotherapy day care center.

e Advanced Diagnostics: Infrastructure includes 1.5T MRI, 64-slice
CT scanners, digital X-ray, and dialysis centers for students.

Sports and Physical Activities


--- Page 869 ---
e Sport Carnival 2025-26: A major campus event held on January
12-13, 2026, featuring competitions in football, volleyball, kho-kho,
athletics, badminton, chess, and carrom.

e Physical Education Unit: Managed by a qualified coach, this unit
organizes regular sports activities and maintains the college's
competitive teams, particularly in football and athletics, which
represent the institution at university levels.

e On-Campus Facilities: Students have access to a gymnasium, two
basketball courts, a cricket ground, a football court, and multiple
indoor shuttle badminton and volleyball courts.

Cultural and Social Life

e Annual Events: The primary annual cultural festival, "Kalopsia,"
includes music, dance, and arts competitions.

e Festival Celebrations: Major regional and national festivals such as
Onam, Christmas, Holi, and Diwali are celebrated annually on
campus. with community lunches and cultural performances.

e Student Council: The Student Council, under the framework of the
Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS), is the primary body
responsible for organizing non-curricular fests, DJ nights, and food
festivals.

e Common Amenities: The campus includes a large 30-acre area with
a garden for evening walks and a centralized cafeteria that serves as
a social hub for both students and faculty.

Hostel & Mess Facilities
Standard Student Hostels:


--- Page 870 ---
e Separate in-campus buildings for boys (198 rooms) and girls (282
rooms).

e Room Configuration: Primary options include triple-sharing and
double-sharing rooms.

e Furnishings: Each student is provided with a cot, study table, chair,
and wardrobe.

e Attached Facilities: Rooms include attached washrooms and
overhead fans.

e Recreation: Common rooms are equipped with LED televisions,
music systems, and indoor games.

e Mess and Dining: Each hostel has its own furnished mess hall. An
additional mess is located on the first floor of the campus canteen.
The menu typically includes a mix of vegetarian and non-vegetarian
Kerala-style cuisine.

Services & Security

e Connectivity: High-speed internet (18 Mbps - 100 Mbps) is available
in recreational areas and for digital learning.

e Maintenance: Daily cleaning and hygiene maintenance are
conducted by the housekeeping department.

e Security: 24-hour security personnel and CCTV monitoring are
standard. Strict hostel rules, including a 9:30 PM curfew, are enforced
for student safety.

e Laundry: Professional laundry services are available for all residents.

Student Support and Grievance Systems


--- Page 871 ---
e Anti-Ragging Infrastructure: The college has a _ permanent
Anti-Ragging Committee and an Anti-Ragging Squad.

o The Squad conducts surprise raids on hostels and vulnerable
campus spots to eliminate potential harassment.

o The system operates with a "zero-tolerance" policy in line with
KUHS and NMC regulations.

e Mentorship and Counseling: Students have access to a Student
Support & Guidance Programme, which provides confidential
counseling with professionals and academic guidance to help
manage stress.

e Student Council: An elected Student Council acts as a formal bridge
between the student body and administration, ensuring student
voices are heard in campus affairs.

Internship Placement Quality - Quick Summary

e PK Das Institute of Medical Sciences offers structured internship
training with good exposure in major departments such as
Medicine, Surgery, OBG, Pediatrics, and Emergency. Steady
patient inflow ensures practical hands-on experience in ward
work, procedures, and case management, helping interns gain
clinical confidence.

e There is no formal campus placement system, as is common in
medical colleges. Graduates typically pursue Junior Residency,
hospital jobs, or prepare for NEET-PG. Overall, the college
provides a solid clinical foundation for higher studies and medical
careers.


--- Page 872 ---
For more detailed and updated information, students are advised
to directly contact the college administration or visit the official
website.

PK Das Institute of Medical Science Student Parent
Review
Student Review
Students generally describe PK Das Medical College as a clinically focused
institution with steady patient inflow that supports practical learning.
Regular classes, structured academic schedules, and approachable faculty
members are commonly appreciated. The hospital exposure during clinical
years and internship is considered a strong point.


--- Page 873 ---
On the other hand, some students feel that certain infrastructure facilities
and hostel amenities could be improved further. Campus life is moderately
active, with academic activities taking primary focus.
Overall : PKDIMS provides good clinical exposure and disciplined
academics, making it suitable for students who prioritize hands-on medical
training.
Parent Review
Parents generally view PK Das Medical College as a disciplined and
academically stable institution. They appreciate the structured teaching
system, regular academic monitoring, and steady clinical exposure
provided through the attached hospital. Safety within the campus and
faculty accessibility are often considered positive aspects.
However, some parents feel that hostel facilities and certain infrastructure
areas can be further upgraded for enhanced student comfort. Overall,
parents consider the institution reliable for medical education with a strong
focus on clinical training.
Overall : PKDIMS is regarded as academically dependable with good
clinical exposure, though improvements in campus amenities are expected.

PUSHPAGIRI INSTITUTE OF MEDICAL
SCIENCE AND RESEARCH CENTRE

PUSHPAGIRI

LOGO
Medical College History & Introduction
Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and Research Centre is one
of the first private medical colleges in Kerala,established in 2002 with a
mission to “work towards a Knowledge Society with life in abundance,
through Science and Technology, improving Health Care for our immediate
community, the state, the country, and the world at large.” The institution is
a Christian Minority Medical College with a strong emphasis on
value-based education, professional ethics, and holistic development.|ts
guiding vision is: “We care, God cures.”
Pushpagiri, originally known as Cherupushpagiri, was the first official
residence (Aramana) of His Lordship Late Jacob Mar Theophilos, a key
collaborator of the Servant of God, Geevarghese Mar lIvanios, in the
cause of Reunion and Catholic Communion in Malankara. The
institution traces its origins to a small clinic with eight beds in 1959,
established to provide rural maternity care. Over the decades, it
expanded into a full-fledged 678-bedded, hi-tech super-specialty
medical college hospital, serving thousands of patients annually.


--- Page 886 ---
The Church’s commitment to education was first demonstrated through
nursing education at Pushpagiri, which began in 1964. The formation of
the Pushpagiri Medical Society in 1992 marked a new era of growth and
expansion, culminating in the establishment of the medical college in
2002. Since then, Pushpagiri has developed premier institutions in
Nursing (2002), Pharmacy (2004), Dental Sciences (2006), and Allied
Health Sciences (2008), establishing itself as a center of excellence in
healthcare education, research, and patient care.
Basic College Profile
e Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and Research Centre is the
one of the first private medical colleges in Kerala, started in 2002.
e Institution Type: Private Self-Financing Medical College
e Minority Status: Christian-minority institution.
e Campus: The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located
in Thiruvalla.
e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)
e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences, National Medical
Commission.
e Religious Affiliation:Syro Malabar Catholic

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences
and Research Centre (PIMSRC) are processed via Commissioner
for Entrance Examinations, Kerala (CEE) through centralized
counselling/web-based allotment.


--- Page 889 ---
e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and Research Centre
(PIMSRC) ) + quota options (state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your
eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e lf a seat is allotted to you at Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences
and Research Centre (PIMSRC) , you get an allotment memo / letter.

5.Reporting to College & Document Verification

e Report to Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and Research
Centre (PIMSRC) within deadline with original certificates: NEET
scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets & passing certificates,transfer /
conduct certificate, domicile / caste / reservation proof (if applicable),
ID proof, birth certificate, etc.

e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.

6.Join the Course

e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and Research Centre
(PIMSRC) with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure
The Central Library
e The Central Library, Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences and
Research Centre, Thiruvalla was established in the year 2002,
September 18th along with the Medical College with a total area of


--- Page 905 ---
10567 sq ft. Approved by National Medical Commission (NMC) and
affiliated to Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS).

e PIMS&RC has a computerized library facility in the Academic Block in
2 floors having a total 400 seating capacity. It is well stocked with
international and national journals. A library with an Online Public
Access Catalogue enables the users to know about the status of any
book in the library.

e The Central Library has a rich collection of 21,000 books, 51
International and 68 National journals, 1573 bounded volumes, 450
theses and 773 CD/DVD collections. Apart from that, the Central
Library has an E Database (Clinical Key & DELNET) containing more
than 1300 E-books and 685 E-journals.

e There is also a separate 19 departmental Library which possesses
150 - 200 books in each department.

e Services and facilities provided by the Central Library are;
Reprographic facility, Current affairs service, Medical updates, online
database, Career Corner etc

Lecture Hall

e Lecture halls are thoughtfully designed to provide a comfortable and
engaging learning environment.

e It is equipped with tiered seating and ergonomic cushioned chairs,
each hall ensures clear visibility and interaction between students
and faculty.

e The interiors feature warm tones and decorative brick paneling,
creating an inviting and professional atmosphere.


--- Page 906 ---
e Advanced lighting and acoustic systems support focused learning,
making the space ideal for lectures, seminars, presentations, and
academic discussions.

e With ample space to accommodate a large number of students, these
halls reflect our commitment to quality education and student comfort.

Canteen

e Booster Chaya is the favorite hangout spot for students and staff
alike, located at the heart of the college campus.

e It is known for its energetic atmosphere and quick service, it offers a
variety of snacks, hot beverages, and refreshing drinks at affordable
prices.

e The signature "booster tea" served here is especially popular, giving
the canteen its iconic name. Whether it's a quick break between
lectures or a casual chat with friends, Booster Chaya has become an
integral part of everyday college life.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e The institution proudly conducts its annual CME on July 25th every
year, in a gesture to commemorate the birth of the first test tube baby.

e Academic Excellence: The college reported a 99% pass rate for its
MD/MS postgraduate exams in the 2025 session under KUHS.

e Scientific Conferences & CMEs: Regular Continuing Medical
Education (CME) programs, national and state-level conferences,
specialty workshops, and symposiums across departments such as


--- Page 907 ---
Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, OBG, Orthopedics, and Community
Medicine.

e Workshops & Skill Training Programs: Hands-on training sessions
in| emergency medicine, basic and advanced life support
(BLS/ACLS), trauma care, laparoscopic _ skills, suturing,
ultrasound-guided procedures, and simulation-based learning.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A multi-specialty setup with over 763 teaching beds
(total hospital capacity often cited near 900 to 1,200 beds across all
units).

e Patient Inflow:The hospital manages around 1,000+ outpatient
visits every day.It also provides care to approximately 800
inpatients, ensuring strong clinical exposure.

e Specialized Units: It features modern Intensive Care Units (ICUs),
including dedicated Medical, Surgical, Cardiac, Neonatal (NICU), and
Paediatric (PICU) units.

e Surgical & Diagnostic Facilities: The facility includes 14 operation
theatres, a 128-slice MDCT scanner, 1.5 Tesla MRI, and a 24-hour
fully automated laboratory and blood bank with component separation
units.

e Specialty Services: The hospital houses over 40 clinical
departments, offering services in super-specialties such as
Cardiology, Neurology, Nephrology (with dialysis), and Oncology.

e Annual College Fest & Arts Festival: A multi-day cultural

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences provides separate,

the campus for easy access to academic and hospital facilities.

e Rooms are spacious, well-ventilated, and furnished with beds, study
tables, wardrobes, and adequate lighting to support a comfortable

e Wi-Fi connectivity is available to support academic work and online
learning.

e Common rooms with television, indoor games, and recreational
facilities are provided to promote student interaction and relaxation.
Laundry services and housekeeping support are also available.

e The mess facilities follow strict hygiene standards and serve
nutritious, balanced meals catering to diverse dietary preferences.

Safety & Support Systems

e Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences places strong emphasis on
student safety, well-being, and academic support, creating a secure
and nurturing campus environment.

e The campus is protected by 24x7 trained security personnel,
CCTV surveillance, and controlled entry and exit points for academic
buildings, hostels, and hospital areas. Separate hostel wardens
ensure continuous supervision and student safety, especially for
residential students.

e The institution follows a strict anti-ragging policy in accordance
with UGC and NMC guidelines. An active Anti-Ragging Committee
and Squad function throughout the year, and awareness programs
are conducted to promote a respectful campus culture. Any
complaints are addressed promptly and confidentially.

e A dedicated student grievance redressal system allows students to
raise academic, personal, or administrative concerns without fear.
Faculty mentors and advisors are assigned to guide students
academically and personally.

e The college also provides counseling and mental health support
services, ensuring emotional well-being and stress management.
Academic mentoring, remedial teaching, and career guidance
sessions are offered to support student performance and professional
development.

College rules & discipline


--- Page 910 ---
e Pushpagiri Institute of Medical Sciences follows a strict code of
conduct to maintain academic excellence, professionalism, and a
respectful campus environment.

e Students are expected to maintain regular attendance, adhere to the
academic timetable, and actively participate in clinical and academic
activities. Punctuality, proper dress code, and professional
behavior are strictly enforced, especially within hospital and clinical
settings.

e The institution enforces a zero-tolerance policy toward ragging,
substance abuse, misconduct, and indiscipline. Any violation of
rules is addressed through a structured disciplinary process involving
faculty, wardens, and disciplinary committees.

Note: To know more about the rules and regulations, please read the
college admission prospectus carefully before admission.

Way to reach
e By Rail (Train):
The nearest railway station is Tiruvalla Railway Station (TRVL), which
is approximately 1.9 km from the institute. You can easily find
auto-rickshaws or taxis at the station to reach your destination.
e By Bus (Road):
The institute is located near the private bus stand in Thiruvalla,
making it highly accessible by public buses. Various public and
private buses ply the routes through Tiruvalla.
e By Air (Flight):
The nearest major airport is Cochin International Airport (COK), which
is about 115 km away. From the airport, you can hire a taxi or use


--- Page 915 ---
airport bus services to reach Tiruvalla. Alternatively, you could
consider Trivandrum International Airport (TRV), which is also a
viable option.

LOGO:

MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Dr. Somervell Memorial CSI Medical College (Dr SMCSI MCH) established
in 2002, attached to the Dr. Somervell Memorial Mission Hospital is at
Karakonam, a village, in the southern border of the Thiruvananthapuram
District of the State of Kerala. The Hospital, the Medical College and all
other institutions attached are run by the South Kerala Diocese of the
Church of South India (SIUC) and managed by the South Kerala Medical
Mission.
The Dr. Somervell Memorial CSI Medical College (SMCSI) in Karakonam,
Kerala, offers a comprehensive range of healthcare programs at the
undergraduate, postgraduate, and diploma levels. At the undergraduate
level, the primary medical degree is the MBBS, which has an annual intake
of 150 students and lasts 5.5 years including a compulsory internship. The
college also provides a B.Sc. in Nursing (4 years) and a B.Sc. in Nursing
(Post Basic) (2 years). Postgraduate medical education includes Doctor of
Medicine (MD) and Master of Surgery (MS) programs in specialisations


--- Page 920 ---
such as General Medicine, Paediatrics, Dermatology, Radiology,
Psychiatry, Anaesthesiology, General Surgery, Orthopaedics, and
Obstetrics & Gynaecology. Additionally, the institution offers a Master of
Hospital Administration (MHA) and various paramedical programs,
including Bachelor of Physiotherapy (BPT) and two-year diplomas in
Medical Laboratory Technology (DMLT), Operation Theatre and
Anaesthesia Technology (DOTAT), Ophthalmic Assistance (DOA),
Radiological Technology (DRT), and Dialysis Technology (DDT).
Mission
Mission is to offer excellent spiritual care, emotional support, guidance and
education to the patients, families, staff and students of Dr. S.M CSI
Medical College and Hospital, Karakonam and the community at large, for
their healing, growth and well-being.
Vision
To give glory and honor to God.
To develop a clinical pastoral education programme.
To take initiative and leadership in linking the medical institution and
community for preventive education, medicine and service.
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Dr. Somervell Memorial CSI Medical College &

Hospital (often referred to as Karakonam Medical College).

e Location: Karakonam, Thiruvananthapuram District, Kerala.

e Year of Establishment: 2002.

e Type of College: Private, Self-financing, and Minority Institution.


--- Page 921 ---
e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS),
Thrissur (Previously affiliated with the University of Kerala).

e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala for 85% State Quota; Medical Counselling Committee
(MCC) for 15% All India Quota.

e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC), formerly
Medical Council of India (MCI).

e MBBS Intake: 150 seats.

e Course Duration: 5.5 years (includes 4.5 years of academic study
and 1 year of compulsory rotatory internship).

e Hospital Type: Multi-specialty Teaching Hospital
(Charitable/Mission-based).

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: 672 beds.

e Total ICU Beds: 30+ beds, including a fully equipped 15-bed Medical
Intensive Care Unit (MICU) and specialized 10-bed Neonatal ICUs
(Level-3).

e Total Operation Theatres: 11 total, consisting of 9 Major and 2 Minor
operation theatres.

e Total Outpatients: Our out-patient strength is around 120-140 per
day with bed occupancy of almost 86-90 % on all days.

e Emergency Services: 24/7 Casualty and Trauma Care with a
dedicated 25-bed emergency department.

Medical Commission (NMC) and the Indian Nursing Council (INC).

e Clinical Exposure: Extensive hands-on training via its high bed
occupancy (approx. 86-90%) and rotation through affiliated Rural
Health Training Centres in Kazhakottam and Urban Health Training
Centres in Nellikakuzhy.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. Qualify NEET-UG: Score the required percentile and ensure 50%
marks in PCB (Physics, Chemistry, Biology) in 12th grade.

2. CEE Kerala Registration: Register on the CEE Kerala (KEAM) portal.
Upload your NEET score and category/minority certificates.

3. Option Entry: Select Dr. Somervell (KCM) as your preferred choice on
the CEE website and lock your options.


--- Page 924 ---
4. Seat Allotment: Download the Allotment Memo once CEE assigns
you a seat based on your rank.
5. College Reporting: Visit the college in Karakonam with original
documents (10th/12th marks, TC, NEET scorecard) for verification.
6. Fee Payment: Pay the tuition and special fees to confirm your seat
and join the course.

Academic Infrastructure

e Smart Classrooms: Equipped with e-learning facilities, LCD
projectors, and advanced audio-visual aids.

e Departmental Labs: Separate, well-equipped labs for Anatomy
(Dissection Hall), Physiology, Biochemistry, Pathology, and
Microbiology.

e Skill Lab: A modern Clinical Skill Simulation Lab where students
practice procedures on manikins before performing them on patients.

e Museums: Extensive anatomy and pathology museums featuring wet
specimens, models, and charts for self-directed learning

e Resources: A vast _ collection of medical textbooks,
national/international journals, and reference materials.


--- Page 937 ---
e Digital Library: Access to e-journals and online databases (like
UpToDate or ClinicalKey) via high-speed internet.

e Reading Rooms: Separate spacious reading areas for students and
faculty, including an External Reading Room that stays open for
extended hours.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlight

e Public Health Days: Active observance of World TB Day, World
Breastfeeding Week, and World Suicide Prevention Day through
awareness rallies and camps.

e University Ranks: Students frequently secure 1st Ranks in KUHS
examinations for MS Ophthalmology and MS General Surgery.

e Active Projects: The campus hosts over 100 completed and 60
ongoing research projects involving students and faculty.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A 672-bedded multi-specialty facility.

e Specialized Units: Includes a 24/7 Casualty & Trauma Care centre, a
Cath Lab, Dialysis unit, and specialized ICUs (Medical, Surgical,
Neonatal, and Pediatric).

e Diagnostic Facilities: Equipped with 1.5T MRI, Multi-slice CT Scan,
Mammography, and fully automated 24-hour clinical laboratories for
Biochemistry, Pathology, and Microbiology.

e Specialties: Dedicated departments for Cardiology, Nephrology,
Orthopaedics, and Radiodiagnosis, among others


--- Page 938 ---
e Patient Inflow: The hospital caters to the underprivileged population
of Thiruvananthapuram and Kanyakumari districts, ensuring exposure
to a high volume of primary and tertiary cases.

e Departmental Strengths: The Pediatrics department is highly
regarded, featuring a 72-bed ward and Level-3 Neonatal ICUs that
handle extreme preterm cases.

e Hands-on Training: Clinical rotations start early, with students
participating in daily Out-Patient (OP) services (averaging 120—140
patients/day in specific departments like Pediatrics) and 24-hour
emergency duties.

Campus Life

e Rules & Curfew: The campus is known for its strict discipline. Curfew
is generally 7:00 PM for girls and 9:00 PM for boys, with permission
slips required for leaving campus.

e Athletics: The college places a strong emphasis on physical fitness.
Facilities include two basketball courts, two volleyball courts, a
football/cricket ground, and four badminton courts.

e Major Festivals: Annual arts and sports fests such as "Confluence"
and "Confesta" are the highlights of campus life, typically held
between September and November.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Clinical Exposure: The hospital serves a diverse patient base from
both Kerala and Tamil Nadu, offering significant "hands-on"
experience in diagnosing and treating various cases.


--- Page 939 ---
e Compulsory Service: Completion of the internship includes a
mandatory rural service component, which is a prerequisite for
medical council registration.

e Post-Internship Paths: Most graduates transition into roles as Medical
Officers within the institution or private sector, while many focus on
preparing for NEET PG exams.

Hostel & Mess Facilities
A separate hostel is available in the campus for both boys and girls.
Accommodation is provided for undergraduate students, interns,
residents and nurses. The hostel has a visitor room, a study room
with facilities for computers and internet. Recreational facility rooms
having T.V., Music, Indoor games etc. and messing facilities for the
students are available in the hostel.


--- Page 940 ---
Safety & Support Systems

e 24/7 Surveillance: The campus is equipped with CCTV monitoring in
common areas, hostel entrances, and academic blocks.

e Security Personnel: Round-the-clock security guards manage entry
and exit points, ensuring only authorized personnel and students
enter the residential zones.

e Strict Curfews: For safety, the 7:00 PM curfew for female students is
strictly enforced. Outings require prior written approval from the
Warden and notification to parents.

College rules &amp; discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A dedicated committee and squad
conduct regular surprise visits to hostels and campus premises
to prevent harassment.

e Penalties: Students found guilty of ragging face immediate
suspension or rustication from the college, and the institution is
required to file a police report under relevant criminal laws.

e Grievance Redressal Committee: This body addresses academic
and non-academic complaints, ensuring a fair hearing for all
parties involved.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles
issues related to gender-based discrimination or sexual
harassment.

Student Review
Academics: Excellent. Teachers are supportive, and the high patient
flow (Kerala-TN border) offers superior clinical experience.Safety:
Very safe. It is a ragging-free campus with a strong bond between
seniors and juniors.Infrastructure: Mixed. The library and labs are
great, but classrooms lack Wi-Fi, and some buildings are old.Hostel &
Mess: The biggest downside. Rooms are often crowded, and
students frequently complain about poor food quality.
Rules: Very strict. It has a "school-like" atmosphere with early curfews
(7 PM for girls) and rigid discipline.

Overall:SMCSI offers excellent clinical exposure and supportive faculty in a

safe, ragging-free environment, but students must navigate extremely strict

curfews. and subpar hostel facilities.

Parent Review
Safe & Disciplined: Parents love the strict security and ragging-free
environment. For many, the early curfews and rigid rules provide
peace of mind regarding their child's safety.High Value for Money
(Clinical): They feel the clinical training is worth the fees. Since the
hospital is always busy, parents see their children becoming confident
doctors quickly.Academic Discipline: Many appreciate the
"school-like" monitoring, as it ensures students stay focused on the
heavy MBBS syllabus and pass university exams.


--- Page 942 ---
Concerns over Food & Living: The most common parental complaint
is the hostel and mess. Parents often feel the living conditions and
food quality do not match the high fees paid.
Overall:The college for its strict discipline, high safety standards, and
excellent clinical training, though they frequently express dissatisfaction
with the poor hostel infrastructure and mess food quality relative to the fees
paid.

approximately 1 hour and 15 minutes to reach via NH66.

LOGO
MEDICAL COLLEGE - OVERVIEW AND OBJECTIVES
Established in 2006, the Sree Uthradom Thirunal (SUT) Academy of
Medical Sciences is a private institution managed by the Sri Moogambigai
Charitable and Educational Trust. Its history is rooted in the SUT Specialty
Hospital, which was inaugurated in 1987 as a pioneer for tertiary care in
Thiruvananthapuram and was the first in Kerala to perform coronary artery
bypass surgery on a beating heart. The academy currently offers a
comprehensive range of medical programs, including its flagship MBBS
degree with an annual intake of 150 students, along with various
postgraduate (MD/MS) specializations such as General Medicine,
Paediatrics, Anaesthesiology, and Orthopaedics. Additionally, the institution
provides Allied Health Science courses, including B.Sc. in Nursing and
specialized technical programs like Respiratory Technology.
Vision
e To be an international leader in medical education and research.
e To empower future doctors through innovation and excellence.
e To provide compassionate, high-quality patient care.
Mission
e Quality Education: Deliver top-tier medical training using modern
teaching tools.Research: Encourage students and staff to pursue
medical breakthroughs.


--- Page 947 ---
e Community Service: Actively participate in national health programs

and public outreach.
Basic College Profile

e Name of Institution: Sree Uthradom Thirunal Academy of
Medical Sciences (SUTAMS).

e Location: Vencode, Vattappara, Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala -
695028.

e Year of Establishment: 2006.

e Type of College: Private (Non-Government).

e University Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences
(KUHS), Thrissur.

e Counselling Authority: Commissioner for Entrance Examinations
(CEE), Kerala (through KEAM/NEET-UG counselling).

e Recognised By: National Medical Commission (NMC) / Medical
Council of India (MCI).

e MBBS Intake: 150 seats.

e Course Duration: 5.5 years (including a 1-year compulsory
rotatory internship).

e Hospital Type: Multi-specialty Teaching Hospital (SUT Specialty
Hospital, 470 beds).

Teaching Hospital Statistics (2025)

e Total Hospital Beds: 470 beds.

e Total ICU Beds: Approximately 17 intensive care beds, supplemented
by specialized units like a 12-bed Coronary Care Unit (CCU).

e Total Operation Theatres: Equipped with multiple major and minor
operation theaters featuring remote-controlled tables and halogen
shadowless lights.

e Total Outpatients: Serves approximately 1,150+ outpatients daily.


--- Page 949 ---

emergency medicine support.

e Hospital Accreditation: Recognized and approved by the National
Medical Commission (NMC); the pathology department also aligns
with NABL/NABH standards.

e Clinical Exposure: Offers extensive hands-on training in core
specialties such as General Medicine, Surgery, Pediatrics, and OBG,
as well as super-specialties like Interventional Cardiology

MBBS (Course) — Core Details

e Total Duration: 5.5 years, comprising 4.5 years of academic study
and a 1-year compulsory rotatory internship.

e Annual Intake: 150 seats.

e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences (KUHS).

Assessment / exam format:

e Frequency: At least two Periodic Content Tests (PCT) and one Prelim
(Model) Examination per phase.

e Eligibility: Students must secure a minimum of 50% marks in IA
(separately for theory and practicals) to appear for final university
exams.

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)

1. CEE Kerala Registration: Even before NEET results, candidates must
register on the CEE Kerala portal during the KEAM application
window (typically February—March).

2. NEET Score Submission: Once NEET-UG results are announced,
candidates must log back into the CEE portal to upload their NEET
scores and rank.

3. State Merit List: CEE publishes a State Medical Rank List based on
the submitted NEET scores.

4. Option Registration (Choice Filling): Eligible candidates register their
college preferences (e.g., SUTAMS as a priority) through the
Centralised Allotment Process (CAP).

5. Seat Allotment: Allotment is done across multiple rounds based on
merit, preference, and seat availability (Government, Management, or
NRI quotas).

6. Confirmation & Reporting: Allotted candidates must pay the tuition fee
via the CEE portal and report to the college with original documents
for final verification.
