Academic Infrastructure
e Lecture Halls: There are three lecture theatres specifically for the
medical college and one for the hospital. The college halls have a
seating capacity of 120 students each and are equipped with
audio-visual aids including LCD projectors, microphones, and
overhead projectors.
e The Central Library serves as the primary hub for academic
resources.Space and Capacity: Spans 1,600 square meters with


--- Page 966 ---
separate indoor and outdoor reading rooms for students (100 seats)
and staff (20 seats).

e Academic learning is directly integrated with the 470-bed SUT
Specialty Hospital.

e Clinical Exposure: Students undergo rotations in advanced
departments like Interventional Cardiology, Neurosurgery, and
Orthopaedics.

e Skill Centers: The institution provides state-of-the-art simulation labs
and skill centers for practicing clinical procedures before entering live
patient environments.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e The Department of Pharmacology. and Respiratory Medicine
frequently lead research-oriented webinars and CMEs, such as
ASTHMACON 2024 and EYECON 2024, which focus on recent
clinical advancements.

e CME "OTOCON 2026": The ENT department hosted this specialized
conference.

e Health Awareness Programs: Recent initiatives include a World AIDS
Day flash mob (December 2024), a free health camp for World COPD
Day (November 2024), and a Self Defence Class for female staff and
students led by Kerala Police.

Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure
The hospital provides a _ high-volume clinical environment with
comprehensive facilities


--- Page 967 ---
e Specialized Units: Known for its dedicated Cardiology Center, which
performed Kerala's first beating-heart coronary bypass.

e Critical Care: Includes 17 Intensive Care (ICU) beds, 12 Coronary
Care (CCU) beds, and 4 post-operative recovery beds.

e Emergency & Wards: Features a 16-bed central casualty service, a
60-bed Pediatric ward, a 120-bed General ward, and a 10-bed Labor
room.

e Diagnostics: Fully equipped medical laboratories for biochemistry,
microbiology, serology, hematology, and histopathology are integrated
within the hospital.

e Diverse Patient Load: Exposure to a wide range of cases across
departments like General Medicine, Pediatrics, Orthopedics, and
Obstetrics & Gynaecology.

e Hands-on Training: Opportunities to observe and assist in advanced
procedures, including laparoscopic surgeries and high-risk pregnancy
management.

Campus Life

e Sports and Fitness: Facilities are available for football, basketball,
and volleyball, alongside indoor games like carrom, chess, and table
tennis. A gymnasium (health club) is located on the top floor of the
hostel for daily workouts.

e Student Organizations: The NSS Unit is highly active, organizing
social awareness campaigns such as anti-drug flash mobs, street
plays, and health education sessions.

Hostel & Mess Facilities


--- Page 968 ---
e The SUT Academy of Medical Sciences provides separate
on-campus residential buildings for men and women, integrated with
a central mess system. The facilities are designed to support
approximately 150 students per batch within a disciplined, green
campus environment.

e The mess serves both vegetarian and non-vegetarian options
separately. While historically rated as average, recent reviews from
2026 indicate a change in management has improved food quality.

Safety & Support SystemsSafety

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A dedicated body comprising the Principal,
faculty heads, and student representatives monitors campus
activities.

e Mentorship Program: Students are assigned to a Faculty Mentor who
provides academic guidance and personal support throughout the
MBBS course.

College rules & discipline (anti-ragging, grievance
redressal, hostels)

e An anti-ragging squad which also includes senior faculty members
has been formed and the members make evening/night rounds
(every day by turn) in the campus including hostels, canteen and
other sensitive areas.

e Institutional rules & hostel regulations: the college
prospectus/admission download pages include the institution’s rules
and hostel regulations (disciplinary actions, penalties, attendance
rules). Read the prospectus carefully before admission.

Student Review

e Faculty members as the "best part" of the institute, noting they are
approachable, well-qualified, and instrumental in helping students
manage the hectic Competency-Based Medical Education (CBME)
curriculum.

e A major highlight is the "huge patient load" at the 470-bed teaching
hospital, which provides superior hands-on training compared to
many other private institutions.

e While classroom facilities like air-conditioned lecture halls and
well-equipped labs are praised, some students characterize the
overall infrastructure as "average" or "sub-par" due to a small campus
footprint and limited buildings.

OVERALL:Sree Uthradom Thirunal (SUT) Academy of Medical Sciences is
a high-discipline, academically focused private institution that prioritizes
clinical competence over campus luxury.

Parent Review

e The strong anti-ragging committee and 24/7 security provide peace of
mind regarding student safety.

e The high patient load at the associated hospital is seen as a major
asset, ensuring their wards get better clinical exposure than at many
other self-financing colleges.

e Professors are widely reviewed as supportive and approachable,
maintaining a low student-teacher ratio for better personal attention.

Overall:SUT Academy of Medical Sciences emphasize a secure and
academically rigorous environment, though they often highlight
administrative and lifestyle trade-offs common to private medical colleges

At GetMyAdmission (GMA), we evaluate medical institutions based on
academic standards, clinical exposure, infrastructure quality,
affordability, and overall student support. Sree Uthradom Thirunal
Academy of Medical Sciences (SUTAMS), Thiruvananthapuram, is a
private medical college in Kerala known for its modern infrastructure
and steadily developing hospital services for MBBS education.
Student Perspective
Students commonly highlight:

e Well-maintained campus with modern lecture halls, laboratories, and

learning facilities.
e Structured academic schedule with regular internal assessments and
monitored clinical postings.


--- Page 971 ---
e Supportive faculty, especially in pre-clinical and para-clinical
departments.
e Comfortable hostel facilities and disciplined campus atmosphere.
Students also mention that:
e Clinical exposure is moderate and may not be as high as older
government colleges in the state.
e Patient inflow, while steady, is still developing compared to major
tertiary care centers.
Parent Perspective
Parents appreciate:
e Clean and organized campus with good infrastructure standards.
e Safe hostel facilities with proper supervision.
e Transparent academic functioning and systematic management.
e Location advantage of being in Thiruvananthapuram city.
However, parents also consider:
e The higher fee structure compared to government medical colleges.
e The need for continued hospital expansion to strengthen clinical
exposure further.
Overall Assessment
Sree Uthradom Thirunal Academy of Medical Sciences offers a
well-structured academic environment with good infrastructure and
disciplined functioning. While clinical exposure is improving, it may not yet
match the intensity of long-established government institutions.


--- Page 972 ---
The college is suitable for students who prioritize a modern campus
environment, organized academics, and a private institutional setup within
Thiruvananthapuram.

Ni TRAVANCORE MEDICAL COLLEGE
LOGO:

Medical College - History & Introduction

Travancore Medical College, Kollam is a Minority Educational Institution . It
was established by ‘Quilon Medical Trust’, Kollam in the academic year
2009-2010. The College offers MBBS Courses. and Post Graduate Medical
MD/MS Courses, Recognized by the National Medical Commission and
affiliated with the Kerala University of Health Sciences. The teaching
hospital attached to the College is the ‘Travancore Medical College
Hospital’ which is a well-known tertiary care hospital in Kerala State
situated at ‘Travancore Medicity’ adjacent to Kollam City, the Cashew
Capital of the World. The Medical College & Hospital renders Medical
education to deserving poor students at concessional rates and treatment
to deserving patients at concessional rates irrespective of caste and creed.
Vision is to become the top most Medical College in South India within a
decade, with State of the art infrastructure and excellent faculty in a serene
campus adjacent to the city limit of Kollam Corporation to attract people
from all over South India.Mission of the Medical College & Hospital to
achieve the objects of the Trust renders Medical education to deserving
students at concessional rates and treatment at concessional rates to poor
patients irrespective of caste and creed. The Institutional so conducts free


--- Page 978 ---
medical camps involving specialist doctors in various branches for the
benefit of poor and needy and provide free treatment, or at concessional
rate, to deserving patients in association with the Muslim Association,
Kollam and other similar charitable organizations.Travancore Medicity is
committed to providing the highest quality medical treatment while
consistently striving to satisfy and delight patients through compassionate
and efficient care. The institution focuses on sustainable growth by creating
value through responsible profits, ensuring long-term development and
excellence. It also aims to serve both national and international patients
with comprehensive care in all aspects, supporting their quick recovery and
overall well-being.
Basic College Profile
e Travancore Medical College Hospital (as hospital) established in
2007.
e Travancore Medical College was established by ‘Quilon Medical
Trust’, Kollam in the academic year 2009-2010.
e Institution Type : Private Self-Financing Medical College
e Minority Status : Muslim-minority institution.
e Campus : The college + hospital + related infrastructure are located
in Mylapore, Thattamala,Kollam.
e Counselling Authority: CEE Kerala (State Quota/ Minority/ NRI)
e Affiliation: Kerala University of Health Sciences.
e Recognised by: National Medical Commission (NMC)

Admission Procedure for MBBS (Undergraduate)
1.Qualify Entrance Exam

e You must appear in and qualify NEET-UG (with required
percentile/marks).

e Also, your 10+2 (Physics, Chemistry, Biology + English) must meet
eligibility: usually 50% aggregate PCB for general, 40% for reserved
(SC/ST/OBC) as per state rules.

2. Register for State-Level Counselling

e Admissions in Kerala (state quota / self-financing / management/
minority / NRI) for MBBS at Travancore Medical college ,Kollam are
processed via Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala
(CEE) through centralized counselling/web-based allotment.

e You need to register on the official CEE portal, submit required
credentials (NEET result, academic records, domicile / caste /
reservation proofs if applicable).

3.Option Filling / Choice Preference

e Once registered, you fill in your priorities: course (MBBS) + colleges
(e.g. Travancore Medical College,Kollam) + quota options
(state-quota, minority,NRI) — as per your eligibility & preference.

e Lock your choices before the deadline. Option-filling and locking is
mandatory to participate in seat allotment.

4.Seat Allotment by CEE / Counselling Authority

e Based on your NEET rank, reservation category, preferences,and
seat availability, the counselling authority does seat allotment.

e lf a seat is allotted to you at Travancore Medical College,Kollam , you
get an allotment memo / letter.


--- Page 982 ---
5.Reporting to College & Document Verification
e Report to Travancore Medical College,Kollam within deadline with
original certificates: NEET scorecard, 10th/12th marksheets &
passing certificates,transfer / conduct certificate, domicile / caste /
reservation proof (if applicable), ID proof, birth certificate, etc.
e Pay the required tuition fee (and other fees like admission fee,etc.) to
confirm admission.
6.Join the Course
e Once verification and fee payment is done — you join MBBS 1st year
at Travancore Medical College,Kollam with all admitted students.

Academic Infrastructure

e Library : The Central Library is housed in the Academic block of the
Medical College. The library has a seating capacity of 250 students.
At present there are 15036 books in the library. There are 60 Indian
and 14 foreign journals currently subscribed in the library. The Central
Library has space for Room for Librarian, Internet, External reading,
Journal reading, Reprography, Audio Visual, Staff reading. Current
periodicals and Back volume Binding area etc.

e Air Conditioned Auditorium : A large auditorium for academic
seminars, professional workshops, and cultural events.

e Lecture Halls Theater Type : Large, gallery-style lecture halls
equipped with smart boards, LED projectors, and advanced
audio-visual systems.

e Transport Facility : The college provides organized transport
services for students, staff, and hospital personnel, connecting the
campus with major routes, nearby towns, and hostels, ensuring safe
and convenient daily commuting.

e Internet Cafe : A dedicated internet café is available on campus with
high-speed connectivity, computers, and printing facilities to support
academic research, online learning, and administrative work.


--- Page 993 ---
e Common Rooms : Separate common rooms for boys and girls are
provided, offering rest areas, lockers, washrooms, and seating
spaces for relaxation between academic sessions.

e College Council Hall : The College Council Hall serves as the
central venue for official meetings, academic discussions, faculty
conferences, student councils, and institutional events.

e Optical Store : An on-campus optical store provides eye-testing
services, prescription glasses, contact lenses, and basic ophthalmic
accessories for students, staff, and patients.

e Medical Education Unit : The Medical Education Unit conducts
faculty development programs, teaching-learning workshops,
curriculum planning, assessment training, and promotes innovative
medical education practices.

e Research Labs : Well-equipped research laboratories support
undergraduate and postgraduate research activities, including clinical
research, biomedical studies, and academic projects across
departments.

e Parking Facilities : The campus has designated parking areas for
two-wheelers, four-wheelers, ambulances, and_ staff vehicles,
ensuring organized and secure vehicle management.

e Bank & ATM’s : An on-campus bank branch provides essential
financial services such as account management, deposits,
withdrawals, and _ fee-related transactions for students and
staff.Multiple ATM facilities are available within the campus for easy
access to cash and basic banking services at all times.

e Sports and Recreation Facility: The college offers sports grounds,
indoor games facilities, gymnasium, and recreational areas to


--- Page 994 ---
promote physical fitness, mental well-being, and extracurricular
engagement among students.

e Skill Lab : A modern simulation center featuring medical mannequins
and simulators is used to train students in clinical procedures before
they interact with patients.

e Security : The campus is secured with 24x7 security personnel,
CCTV surveillance, controlled entry and exit points, and regular
patrols to ensure the safety of students, staff, and visitors.

e Yoga : Dedicated spaces are available for yoga, meditation, and
wellness activities, promoting physical fitness, mental health, stress
management, and overall student well-being.

e Canteens & Cafeterias :On-campus cafeterias provide hygienic,
affordable, and nutritious food options, refreshments, catering to
students, staff, and visitors throughout the day.

Events, Achievements & Research Highlights

e NABH Accreditation: TMC Hospital is the first fully NABH-accredited
Medical College Hospital in Kollam, a testament to its commitment to
high-quality healthcare standards.

e Medical Workshops: Recently conducted high-impact training such
as the AHA-accredited Basic Life Support (BLS) and Advanced
Cardiovascular Life Support (ACLS) training programs.

e Travancore Medical College regularly organizes academic
conferences, Continuing Medical Education (CME) programs,
workshops, seminars, health camps, and medical awareness
programs. Annual college festivals, cultural events, sports meets, and


--- Page 995 ---
observance of national and international health days contribute to a
vibrant campus life.
Hospital Infrastructure & Clinical Exposure

e Bed Capacity: A robust 850-bed strength, catering to a diverse
patient demographic from across Southern Kerala.

e Critical Care (ICU Complex): Features 10 specialized ICU units with
a combined strength of over 100 beds. These include Medical,
Surgical, Neonatal (NICU), Pediatric (PICU), and Neuro ICUs.

e Surgical Suites: 14 state-of-the-art Operation Theatres equipped
with Laminar Air Flow to maintain a germ-free environment for
complex procedures.

e Patient Inflow: Students benefit from a high volume of clinical cases,
with the hospital seeing an average of over 1,000 outpatients per day.

e Blood bank; Emergency & trauma care: Full diagnostic
services,blood bank, emergency/trauma services and critical care
blocks are present as part of the hospital infrastructure.

e Specialty & Super-specialty departments:Travancore Medical
College, Kollam offers major specialty departments such as Medicine,
Surgery, Pediatrics, Obstetrics & Gynecology, Orthopedics,
Anesthesiology, Ophthalmology, ENT, Dermatology, Psychiatry,
Radiology, Pathology, Community Medicine, and basic sciences.
Super-specialty services include Cardiology, Neurology,
Neurosurgery, Nephrology, Urology, Gastroenterology, Pulmonology,
Endocrinology, Oncology, Cardiothoracic Surgery, Plastic Surgery,
Pediatric Surgery, and Critical Care Medicine, ensuring advanced
Clinical training and exposure.


--- Page 996 ---
Campus Life

e Sports & recreation: Campus has sports facilities, gym, indoor
games and organizes cultural events & student activities.

e Student clubs & academic events: Active CME,
workshops,conferences, and student fests — plus participation in
research & community programs via the hospital trust.

e Students benefit from well-maintained hostels, recreational facilities,
sports grounds, gymnasium, yoga and wellness centers, cafeterias,
and common rooms.

e Student associations and committees encourage leadership,
teamwork, and holistic development, creating a supportive and
vibrant campus environment.

Hostel & Mess Facilities

e Separate hostels for boys and girls are available.

e Mess & central kitchen serving hostellers; mess charges included in
hostel/mess fee lines of the admission PDF. Quality/menus reported
as standard — best confirmed by speaking to current students.

Safety & Support Systems

e 24/7 Surveillance: The entire campus, including academic blocks,
hospital premises, and hostel perimeters, is monitored by an
extensive CCTV network and round-the-clock professional security
personnel.

e Emergency Infrastructure: The campus is equipped with modern
fire-fighting systems and features a dedicated 24-hour trauma care


--- Page 997 ---
unit and emergency department within the Travancore Medicity
Hospital to handle any medical emergencies immediately.

e Anti-Ragging Committee: In strict compliance with National Medical
Commission (NMC) and UGC regulations, TMC has a proactive
Anti-Ragging Committee and Squad. Any form of harassment is met
with zero tolerance, and students have access to dedicated helpline
numbers.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): A formal body exists to
address grievances related to gender-based discrimination or
harassment, ensuring a safe professional environment for female
students and staff.

e Grievance Redressal: A dedicated cell is available for students to
report academic or administrative concerns, with a_ structured
pathway for resolution.

e Mentorship Program: Each student is assigned a faculty mentor
who provides academic guidance and personal support, helping
students navigate the transition into medical school.

e Counseling Services: Recognizing the mental health challenges of
medical education, the college offers access to the Psychiatry and
Psychology Department for confidential counseling and stress
management.

Internship placement quality — quick summary

e Case Diversity: Interns manage a high patient inflow (average
1,000+ outpatients daily), providing hands-on experience in diverse
medical conditions across 30+ departments.


--- Page 998 ---
e Super-Specialty Rotation: Unique exposure to advanced units like
Interventional Cardiology, Neurosurgery, and Oncology, which is often
limited in smaller teaching hospitals.

e Skill Mastery: Practical training focuses on core competencies,
including emergency trauma management, surgical assistance in 14
OTs, and ICU protocols.

e Rural & Urban Postings: Rotations at affiliated Primary Health
Centres (PHCs) and Urban Health Training Centers ensure interns
are proficient in both community health and tertiary care.

e Interns receive a monthly stipend as mandated by the Kerala State
Government for self-financing medical colleges.

e After internship many graduates either take jobs at hospitals, or
pursue PG entrance .

College rules & discipline

1. Anti-Ragging Measures

TMC follows a zero-tolerance policy towards ragging. The system is
layered to ensure immediate intervention:

e Anti-Ragging Committee: A high-level body including the Principal,
senior faculty, local police officials (usually the Sub-Inspector of
Kottiyam), and representatives from the local media and civil
administration.

e Anti-Ragging Squad: A dedicated team of faculty members who
conduct surprise raids in hostels, canteens, and recreational areas to
prevent any unauthorized interactions between seniors and juniors.


--- Page 999 ---
e National Helpline: In addition to internal contacts, the college
prominently displays the National Anti-Ragging Helpline
(1800-180-5522).

e Orientation: Every new batch undergoes an awareness program
detailing the legal consequences of ragging, which can include
expulsion and a permanent ban from medical practice.

2. Student Grievance Redressal
The college provides a formal platform for students to voice concerns
without fear of academic retaliation:

e Grievance Redressal Cell: Chaired by the Vice Principal, this
committee handles allegations of unfair practices, academic issues,
or personal harassment.

e Internal Complaints Committee (ICC): Specifically handles cases
related to sexual harassment and ensures a safe workplace/learning
environment for female students and staff.

e SSGP Nodal Officer: A dedicated Student Support and Guidance
Program (SSGP) nodal officer is appointed to monitor the general
well-being and mental health of the student body.

3. Hostel Discipline & Rules
The hostel rules are strictly enforced to maintain an academic atmosphere:

e Hostel residents are expected to maintain discipline, respect fellow
students, staff, and hostel authorities, and follow all college
regulations.

e Attendance and entry/exit timings must be strictly adhered to, and
late entries require prior permission.


--- Page 1000 ---
e Ragging in any form is strictly prohibited, and any violation will attract
severe disciplinary action as per UGC and institutional rules.
e Cleanliness, safety, and peaceful co-living are mandatory, and
students are responsible for the care of hostel property.
e For detailed rules and updated regulations, students are advised to
refer to the college hostel handbook or admission prospectus.

environment with experienced faculty, well-equipped laboratories, and
modern teaching facilities. Students appreciate the structured curriculum,
regular clinical postings, and exposure to a wide range of medical
specialties, which help in building strong clinical skills.
Campus life is balanced with academics and extracurricular activities,
including cultural events, sports, and wellness programs. The hostels and
mess facilities are generally well-maintained, and the campus provides
good safety, security, and student support systems. Overall, students find
TMC Kollam to be a conducive institution for medical education and
professional development.
Overall : Travancore Medical College, Kollam provides a strong academic
environment with good clinical exposure, experienced faculty, and
supportive infrastructure. Students generally appreciate the balanced
campus life, safety measures, and overall learning experience.
